
 
                 Prathamaḥ paṭalaḥ

                 yasmin sarvaṃ yataḥ sarvaṃ | yaḥ sarvaṃ sarvataś ca yaḥ | 
 yaś ca sarvamayo nityaṃ | tasmai sarvātmane namaḥ || (RA_1.1) 
 kailāsaśikhare ramye | nānāratnavibhūṣite | 
 nānādrumalatākīrṇe | guptasambandhavarjite || (RA_1.2) 
 devadevaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ | nīlakaṇṭhaṃ trilocanam | 
 praṇamya śirasā devī | pārvatī paripṛcchati || (RA_1.3) 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 devadeva mahādeva | kāla kāmāṅgadāhaka | 
 kulakaulamahākaula- | siddhakaulādināśana || (RA_1.4) 
 tvatprasādāc chrutaṃ sarvam | aśeṣam avadhāritam | 
 yadi te 'ham anugrāhyā | yadyahaṃ tava vallabhā || (RA_1.5) 
 sūcitā sarvatantreṣu | yā punarna prakāśitā | 
 jīvanmuktiriyaṃ nātha | kīdṛśī vaktumarhasi || (RA_1.6) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 sādhu sādhu mahābhāge | sādhu parvatanandini | 
 sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā devi | bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā || (RA_1.7) 
 ajarāmaradehasya | śivatādātmyavedanam | 
 jīvanmuktir mahādevi | devānām api durlabhā || (RA_1.8) 
 piṇḍapāte ca yo mokṣaḥ | sa ca mokṣo nirarthakaḥ | 
 piṇḍe tu patite devi | gardabho 'pi vimucyate || (RA_1.9) 
 yadi muktirbhagakṣobhe | kiṃ na muñcanti gardabhāḥ | 
 ajāś ca vṛṣabhāścaiva | kiṃna muktā gaṇāmbike || (RA_1.10) 
 tasmāt saṃrakṣayet piṇḍaṃ | rasaiścaiva rasāyanaiḥ | 
 śukramūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ | yadi muktirniṣevaṇāt || (RA_1.11) 
 kiṃna muktā mahādevi | śvānaśūkarajātayaḥ | 
 ṣaḍdarśane 'pi muktistu | darśitā piṇḍapātane || (RA_1.12) 
 karāmalakavat sāpi | pratyakṣaṃ nopalabhyate | 
 akathyam api deveśi | sadbhāvaṃ kathayāmi te || (RA_1.13) 
 śūnyapāpo mantrayājī | na piṇḍaṃ dhārayet kvacit | 
 devānām api deveśi | durlabhaṃ piṇḍadhāraṇam || (RA_1.14) 
 kiṃ punarmānuṣāṇāṃ tu | dharaṇītalavāsinām | 
 dharme naṣṭe kuto dharmaḥ | dharme naṣṭe kutaḥ kriyā ||
                    (RA_1.15) 
 kriyānaṣṭe kuto yogaḥ | yoge naṣṭe kuto gatiḥ | 
 gatinaṣṭe kuto mokṣo | mokṣe naṣṭe na kiṃcana || (RA_1.16) 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 jīvanmuktisvarūpaṃ tu | devadeva śrutaṃ mayā | 
 tatpratyupāyaṃ me brūhi | yadyasti karuṇā mayi || (RA_1.17) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 karmayogena deveśi | prāpyate piṇḍadhāraṇam | 
 rasaś ca pavanaśceti | karmayogo dvidhā mataḥ || (RA_1.18) 
 mūrchito harati vyādhiṃ | mṛto jīvayati svayam | 
 baddhaḥ khecaratāṃ kuryāt | raso vāyuś ca bhairavi ||
                    (RA_1.19) 
 jñānānmokṣaḥ sureśāni | jñānaṃ pavanadhāraṇāt | 
 tatra devi sthiraṃ piṇḍaṃ | yatra sthairye rasaḥ prabhuḥ ||
                    (RA_1.20) 
 acirājjāyate devi | śarīram ajarāmaram | 
 manasaś ca yathā dhyānaṃ | rasayogādavāpyate || (RA_1.21) 
 satyaṃ sa labhate devi | jñānaṃ vijñānapūrvakam | 
 tasya mantrāś ca sidhyanti | yo 'śnāti mṛtasūtakam ||
                    (RA_1.22) 
 yāvanna śaktipātas tu | na yāvat pāśakṛntanam | 
 tāvattasya kuto buddhiḥ | jāyate mṛtasūtake || (RA_1.23) 
 madyamāṃsaratā nityaṃ | bhagaliṅgeṣu ye ratāḥ | 
 teṣāṃ vinaṣṭabuddhīnāṃ | rasajñānaṃ sudurlabham || (RA_1.24) 
 kulaśāsanahīnānāṃ | saddarśanam akāṅkṣiṇām | 
 na sidhyati raso devi | pibanti mṛgatṛṣṇikām || (RA_1.25) 
 gomāṃsaṃ bhakṣayed yas tu | pibedamaravāruṇīm | 
 kulīnaṃ tamahaṃ manye | rasajñamapare 'dhamāḥ || (RA_1.26) 
 na garbhaḥ sampradāyārthe | raso garbho vidhīyate | 
 tenāyaṃ labhate siddhiṃ | na siddhiḥ sūtakaṃ vinā ||
                    (RA_1.27) 
 yāvanna harabījaṃ tu | bhakṣayet pāradaṃ rasam | 
 tāvattasya kuto muktiḥ | kutaḥ piṇḍasya dhāraṇam ||
                    (RA_1.28) 
 madyamāṃsaratāprajñā | mohitāḥ śivamāyayā | 
 jalpanti ca vayaṃ muktā | yāsyāmaḥ śivamandiram || (RA_1.29) 
 piṇḍadhāraṇayoge ca | nispṛhā mandabuddhayaḥ | 
 khaṇḍajñānena deveśi | rañjitaṃ sacarācaram || (RA_1.30) 
 svadehe khecaratvaṃ ca | śivatvaṃ yena labhyate | 
 tādṛśe tu rasajñāne | nityābhyāsaṃ kuru priye || (RA_1.31) 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 avatāraṃ rasendrasya | māhātmyaṃ tu sureśvara | 
 śrotum icchāmi deveśa | vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ || (RA_1.32) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ mahābhāge | guhyādguhyataraṃ tvayā | 
 anugrahakaraṃ dhyānaṃ | lokānāmupakārakam || (RA_1.33) 
 tvaṃ mātā sarvabhūtānāṃ | pitā cāhaṃ sanātanaḥ | 
 dvayoś ca yo raso devi | mahāmaithunasambhavaḥ || (RA_1.34) 
 svairataḥ sambhavāddevi | pāradaḥ kīrtito mahaḥ | 
 pārado gadito yaś ca | parārthaṃ sādhakottamaiḥ || (RA_1.35) 
 sūto 'yaṃ matsamo devi | mama pratyaṅgasambhavaḥ | 
 mama deharaso yasmāt | rasastenāyamucyate || (RA_1.36) 
 darśanāt sparśanāt tasya | bhakṣaṇāt smaraṇādapi | 
 pūjanāc ca pradānāc ca | dṛśyate ṣaḍvidhaṃ phalam ||
                    (RA_1.37) 
 kedārādīni liṅgāni | pṛthivyā yāni kāni ca | 
 tāni dṛṣṭvā tu yatpuṇyaṃ | tatpuṇyaṃ rasadarśanāt ||
                    (RA_1.38) 
 candanāgurukarpūra- | kuṅkumāntargato rasaḥ | 
 mūrchitaḥ śivapūjāyāṃ | śivasāṃnidhyasiddhaye || (RA_1.39) 
 bhakṣaṇāt parameśāni | hanti pāpatrayaṃ rasaḥ | 
 tathā tāpatrayaṃ hanti | rogān doṣatrayodbhavān || (RA_1.40) 
 durlabhaṃ brahmaniṣṇātaiḥ | prāpyate paramaṃ padam | 
 hṛdvyomakarṇikāntaḥstha- | rasendrasya maheśvari ||
                    (RA_1.41) 
 smaraṇānmucyate pāpaiḥ | sadyo janmāntarārjitaiḥ ||
                    (RA_1.42) 
 svayaṃbhūliṅgasāhasraiḥ | yatphalaṃ samyagarcanāt | 
 tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ | rasaliṅgārcanādbhavet || (RA_1.43) 
 adhamaḥ khagavādas tu | vilavādas tu madhyamaḥ | 
 uttamo mantravādas tu | rasavādo mahottamaḥ || (RA_1.44) 
 mantratantraparijñāne | rasayogasya dūṣakāḥ | 
 prayānti narakaṃ sarve | chittvā sukṛtasaṃcayam || (RA_1.45) 
 rasavidyā parā vidyā | trailokye 'pi sudurlabhā | 
 bhuktimuktikarī yasmāt | tasmāddeyā guṇānvitaiḥ || (RA_1.46) 
 astīti bhāṣate kaścit | kaścinnāstīti bhāṣate | 
 āstike tu bhavetsiddhiḥ | tasya sidhyati bhūtale ||
                    (RA_1.47) 
 nāstikenānubhāvena | nāsti nāstīti yo vadet | 
 tasya nāsti priye siddhir | janmakoṭiśatair api || (RA_1.48) 
 brahmajñānena mukto 'sau | pāpī yo rasanindakaḥ | 
 nāhaṃ trātā bhave tasya | janmakoṭiśatair api || (RA_1.49) 
 śvāno 'yaṃ jāyate devi | yāvat janmasahasrakam | 
 trikoṭijanmalakṣāṇi | mārjāro jāyate rasāt | 
 rāsabho lakṣajanmāni | lakṣajanmāni vāyasaḥ || (RA_1.50) 
 kṛmiko lakṣajanmāni | kukkuṭo janmalakṣakam | 
 gṛdhrako lakṣajanmāni | yaḥ pāpī rasanindakaḥ || (RA_1.51) 
 ālāpaṃ gātrasaṃsparśaṃ | yaḥ kuryād rasanindakaiḥ | 
 yāvajjanmasahasraṃ tu | sa bhavedduḥkhapīḍitaḥ || (RA_1.52) 
 rasavīryavipāke ca | sūtakastvamṛtopamaḥ | 
 tena janmajarāvyādhīn | harate sūtakaḥ priye || (RA_1.53) 
 gurumārādhayet pūrvaṃ | viśuddhenāntarātmanā | 
 sampradāyaṃ prayacchanti | gurau tuṣṭe marīcayaḥ ||
                    (RA_1.54) 
 gurusevāṃ vinā karma | yaḥ kuryān mūḍhacetanaḥ | 
 sa yāti niṣphalaṃ karma | svapnalabdhaṃ dhanaṃ yathā ||
                    (RA_1.55) 
 yaḥ karma kurute dṛṣṭaṃ | tasya lābhaḥ pade pade | 
 kārayed rasavādaṃ tu | tuṣṭena guruṇā priye || (RA_1.56) 
 siddhyupāyopadeśo 'yam | ubhayorbhogamokṣadaḥ | 
 rasārṇavaṃ mahātantram | idaṃ paramadurlabham || (RA_1.57) 
 gopyaṃ guruprasādena | labdhaṃ syāt phalasiddhaye | 
 labdhvātra rasakarmāṇi | nāhaṃkāraṃ samācaret || (RA_1.58) 
 anujñātaś ca guruṇā | labdhvā cājñāṃ rasāṅkuśīm | 
 bhairavīṃ tanum āśritya | sādhayed rasabhairavam ||
                    (RA_1.59) 
 evamuktā rasotpattiḥ | māhātmyaṃ ca sureśvari | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_1.60) 
 
 
 Dvitīyaḥ paṭalaḥ [Dīkṣāvidhāna] 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 rasopadeśadātā ca | kathaṃ syādvada me prabho | 
 śiṣyaścaiva kathaṃ deva | rasānuṣṭhānatatparaḥ || (RA_2.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 nispṛho nirahaṃkāro | lobhamāyāvivarjitaḥ | 
 kulamārgarato nityaṃ | gurupūjārataś ca yaḥ || (RA_2.2) 
 dāntaḥ śiṣyopadeśajñaḥ | śaktimān gatamatsaraḥ | 
 dharmajñaḥ satyavāk dakṣaḥ | śīlavān guṇavān śuciḥ ||
                    (RA_2.3) 
 anekarasaśāstrajño | rasamaṇḍapakovidaḥ | 
 rasadīkṣāvidhānajño | yantrauṣadhimahārasān || (RA_2.4) 
 rāgasaṃkhyāṃ bījakalāṃ | dvaṃdvamelāpanaṃ viḍam | 
 rañjanaṃ sāraṇaṃ tailaṃ | dalāni krāmaṇāni ca || (RA_2.5) 
 varṇotkarṣaṃ mṛdutvaṃ ca | jāraṇāṃ bālabaddhayoḥ | 
 khecarīṃ bhūcarīṃ caiva | yo vetti sa gururmataḥ || (RA_2.6) 
 deśakālakriyābhijño | dayādākṣiṇyasaṃyutaḥ | 
 lobhamāyāvinirmukto | mantrānuṣṭhānatatparaḥ || (RA_2.7) 
 sāmudralakṣaṇopeto | gambhīro guruvatsalaḥ | 
 devāgniyoginīcakra- | kulapūjārataḥ sadā | 
 śiṣyo vinītastantrajñaḥ | satyavādī dṛḍhavrataḥ || (RA_2.8) 
 ye narāḥ kumbhakuddāla- | dhvajaśaṅkhādilāñchitaiḥ | 
 karair adhiṣṭhitā devi | yojyās te nidhisādhane || (RA_2.9) 
 balavanto mahāsattvāḥ | kṛṣṇaraktavilocanāḥ | 
 vakraghoṇāḥ sadā krūrāḥ | praśastā bilasādhane || (RA_2.10) 
 nirmāṃsamūrdhapiṇḍīkān | raktakeśān gatālasān | 
 kaṭhinān uṣṇapādāṃś ca | dhātuvāde niyojayet || (RA_2.11) 
 ādau parīkṣayed devi | sādhakān susamāhitān | 
 brāhmaṇān kṣatriyān vaiśyān | śūdrāṃścānukrameṇa tu ||
                    (RA_2.12) 
 jitendriyāḥ kleśasahā | nityodyamasamanvitāḥ | 
 śūrāś ca kṛtavidyāś ca | praśastāḥ sādhakāḥ priye ||
                    (RA_2.13) 
 rasadīkṣāvihīnā ye | proktalakṣaṇavarjitāḥ | 
 viplāvakāḥ pāparatāḥ | varjayet tān prayatnataḥ || (RA_2.14) 
 duścāriṇī durācārā | niṣṭhurā kalahapriyā | 
 bahvāśinī ca duścittā | koṭarākṣī ca nirdayā | 
 rasanindākarī yā ca | tāṃ nārīṃ parivarjayet || (RA_2.15) 
 īdṛśībhir varārohe | sampūrṇaṃ kṣitimaṇḍalam | 
 na tādṛśī bhavennārī | yādṛśī rasabandhakī || (RA_2.16) 
 kākiṇī kīkaṇī nārī | tathaiva kāñcikācinī | 
 kṛṣṇapakṣe ṛtumatī | sā nārī kākiṇī smṛtā || (RA_2.17) 
 ubhayapakṣe ṛtumatī | sā nārī kīkaṇī matā || (RA_2.18) 
 śuklapakṣe ṛtumatī | sā nārī kāñcikācinī || (RA_2.19) 
 navayauvanasampannā | surūpā cāruhāsinī | 
 sūkṣmakeśā tu yā nārī | kṣīrāhārapriyā sadā || (RA_2.20) 
 priyālāpakarī nityaṃ | śivaśāstrakathāpriyā | 
 padmākāraṃ mukhaṃ yasyā | dṛṣṭirindīvarākṛtiḥ || (RA_2.21) 
 daśanā vajrasadṛśāḥ | pravālasadṛśo 'dharaḥ | 
 yasyāḥ payodharau devi | tuṅgapīnau samāv ubhau || (RA_2.22) 
 aśvatthapattrasadṛśī | yonī yasyā bhagaḥ samaḥ | 
 yatpādau māṃsalau snigdhau | vartulāvartaromakau ||
                    (RA_2.23) 
 śyāmā ca madhye kṣāmā ca | tanvī bhaktiparā śive | 
 padminī sā tu vijñeyā | prasannā mṛgalocanā || (RA_2.24) 
 pūrṇimāyāmamāyāṃ vā | pakṣe pakṣe rajasvalā | 
 ṣaḍbhedā kākiṇī nāmnā | pūrvaproktā rasapradā || (RA_2.25) 
 yasya tuṣṭo mahādevas | tasya siddho rasāyane | 
 tayaiva devadeveśi | rasakarmāṇi kārayet || (RA_2.26) 
 tasya hi nirmalā buddhir | niścitā rasasādhane | 
 tasmādguruś ca śiṣyaś ca | pūrvoktaḥ siddhibhāgbhavet ||
                    (RA_2.27) 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 īdṛśair lakṣaṇaiḥ nārīṃ | kutaḥ prāpnoti sādhakaḥ | 
 yatra rūpaṃ mahādeva | lakṣaṇaṃ nātra vidyate || (RA_2.28) 
 lakṣaṇaṃ vidyate yatra | bhāvanā nātra vidyate | 
 athavā rūpahīnāyā | rūpaṃ kena pravartate || (RA_2.29) 
 lakṣaṇatritayaṃ kutra | tvayā dṛṣṭaṃ maheśvara | 
 tadetajjāyate yena | tamupāyaṃ vada prabho || (RA_2.30) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 śṛṇu devi paraṃ guhyaṃ | yat surair api durlabham | 
 pituḥ sadāśivājjātaṃ | janma yaccaṇḍikodare || (RA_2.31) 
 tāsāṃ buddhirbhaveddevi | nirmalā rasasādhane | 
 dāpayet tvaritāmantraṃ | japettaṃ darpavarjitā || (RA_2.32) 
 lakṣamantraṃ japedyā tu | jāyate sā sulakṣaṇā | 
 baddhvā tu khecarīṃ mudrāṃ | japet pheṭkārabhairavīm ||
                    (RA_2.33) 
 mameyaṃ caṇḍikā mātā | janma ca tripurāntakāt | 
 kālikāhaṃ samudbhūtā- | smīdṛśaṃ saṃsmaret tu sā ||
                    (RA_2.34) 
 bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca | trailokye kathayet tu sā | 
 sahāyāstādṛśāstasya | yādṛśī bhavitavyatā || (RA_2.35) 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 devadeva mahādeva | samastajñānabhājana | 
 rasadīkṣāṃ tu pṛcchāmi | sādhakānāṃ hitāya vai || (RA_2.36) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 śṛṇu bhairavi yadbhāvam | apūrvaṃ varṇayāmi te | 
 rasadīkṣāvidhānaṃ tu | tasmānnigaditaṃ śṛṇu || (RA_2.37) 
 yatra rājā nayaparo | balavān dharmatatparaḥ | 
 mantrī ca dharmatattvajño | bhaktiśraddhāsamanvitaḥ ||
                    (RA_2.38) 
 tatredaṃ kārayet karma | rasabandhaṃ rasāyanam | 
 janā māheśvarā yatra | tatra sthāne tu kārayet || (RA_2.39) 
 kārayed vijane sthāne | paśuryatra na vidyate | 
 sugupte suṣame sthāne | sarvabādhāvivarjite || (RA_2.40) 
 prākāraparikhopete | kapāṭārgalarakṣite | 
 ekānte nirmale hṛdye | nānāpuṣpadrumānvite || (RA_2.41) 
 haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇe | cakravākopaśobhite | 
 divyauṣadhigaṇopete | sajale śyāmaśādvale || (RA_2.42) 
 kumudotpalakahlāra- | kadalīṣaṇḍamaṇḍite | 
 citrite bhavanodyāne | kārayet parameśvari || (RA_2.43) 
 tanmadhye devadeveśi | mattavāraṇasaṃyutam | 
 vātāyanasamopetam | ūrdhvanirgāmidhūmakam || (RA_2.44) 
 raktapatākāsaṃyuktaṃ | sajjopakaraṇaṃ tathā | 
 pravibhaktauṣadhituṣā- | kāṣṭhāraṇyotpalālayam || (RA_2.45) 
 samālikhitadigdevaṃ | samarcitavināyakam | 
 pratiṣṭhitam umeśābhyāṃ | lokapālaiś ca rakṣitam ||
                    (RA_2.46) 
 nirmāpayed ekatalaṃ | dvitalaṃ vāpi maṇḍapam | 
 atha pakṣe site devi | candratārābalānvite || (RA_2.47) 
 puṇye tithau muhūrte ca | lagne saumyagrahekṣite | 
 snātaḥ śuklāmbaradharaḥ | śuklamālyānulepanaḥ || (RA_2.48) 
 madhusarpirdadhikṣīra- | tilaiḥ saṃpūjya bālikāḥ | 
 kapilāgomayālipte | hiraṇyakalaśāvṛte || (RA_2.49) 
 yavasiddhārthakāstīrṇe | gandhamālyopaśobhite | 
 tatreṣṭikābhiḥ racite | karapīṭhe sureśvari || (RA_2.50) 
 śilāpaṭṭaṃ samutkīrya | śilāpaṭṭārgalaṃ priye | 
 nyāsaṃ rasāṅkuśenaiva | kṛtvāṅgulihṛdādiṣu || (RA_2.51) 
 rasaliṅgaṃ nyasettatra | hemnā ca sahitaṃ priye | 
 oṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ sūtarājasya | mūlamantra udāhṛtaḥ || (RA_2.52) 
 tasmin rasāṅkuśīṃ devīṃ | mūlenāvāhayetpriye | 
 caturasre tu dikpālān | pūjayitvā bahiḥ kramāt || (RA_2.53) 
 nandinaṃ ca mahākālaṃ | bhṛṅgirīṭaṃ mahābalam | 
 kumbhakarṇaṃ ca sugrīvaṃ | bhṛṅgīkaṃ ca dṛḍhāyudham ||
                    (RA_2.54) 
 dvāre caturdhā vinyasya | pūjayed dakṣavāmayoḥ | 
 śukraṃ pūrve 'bhisaṃpūjya | skandamāgneyagocare || (RA_2.55) 
 dakṣiṇasyāṃ tato rudraṃ | pavanaṃ nairṛte tathā | 
 śivaṃ paścimabhāge tu | pāvakaṃ vāyave nyaset | 
 umāmuttarabhāge tu | vyāpakaṃ ceśagocare || (RA_2.56) 
 lepikā kṣepikā caiva | kṣārikā rañjikā tathā | 
 lohaṭī bandhakārī ca | bhūcarī mṛtyunāśinī || (RA_2.57) 
 vibhūtiḥ khecarī caiva | daśa dūtyaḥ krameṇa ca | 
 pūjyāstvaṣṭadale padme | ūrdhvādhas tu daleṣu ca ||
                    (RA_2.58) 
 mākṣiko vimalaḥ śailaś | capalo rasakastathā | 
 sasyako gandhatālau ca | pūrvādikramayogataḥ || (RA_2.59) 
 aṣṭādaśabhujā rudrāḥ | pañcavaktrās tryambakāḥ | 
 candrārdhaśobhimukuṭā | nīlagrīvā vṛṣadhvajāḥ || (RA_2.60) 
 svasvavarṇadharāḥ sarve | 'pyaṣṭavidyeśvarāstathā | 
 pūjanīyā maheśāni | dvitīye 'ṣṭadalāmbuje || (RA_2.61) 
 karṇikāyāṃ tu pūrvādi- | pūrvaṃ śakticatuṣṭayam | 
 mālinī hemaśaktiś ca | parā śaktirbalā smṛtā | 
 aparā vajraśaktiś ca | kāntijñeyaṃ parāparam || (RA_2.62) 
 madhye tāsāṃ ca śaktīnāṃ | sarvajñaṃ rasabhairavam | 
 śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ | pañcavaktraṃ tryambakam ||
                    (RA_2.63) 
 jvalatpiṅgogranetraṃ ca | jvalajjihvānanaṃ tathā | 
 jvaladbhruvaṃ jvalatkeśaṃ | duṣprekṣyaṃ pretaviṣṭaram ||
                    (RA_2.64) 
 jaṭāmukuṭasaṃyuktaṃ | candrārdhakṛtaśikharam | 
 vyāghracarmadharaṃ nāgo- | pavītaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam ||
                    (RA_2.65) 
 aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ devam | īṣatprahasitānanam | 
 dvātriṃśārṇena manunā | pūjayet sakalaṃ śivam || (RA_2.66) 
 raseśvarasya mantraṃ ca | kathyamānaṃ nibodha me ||
                    (RA_2.67) 
 oṃ hrīṃ krīṃ raseśvarāya mahākālāya mahābalāyāghorabhairavāya vajravīra
                    krodhakaṅkāla kṣlauḥ kṣlaḥ || Ras_2.68 || 
 tasyotsaṅge mahādevīṃ | ratnābharaṇabhūṣaṇām | 
 uttaptahemarucirāṃ | pītavastrāṃ trilocanām || (RA_2.69) 
 śvetacāmarayor madhye | muktāc chattreṇa śobhitām | 
 aṅkuśaṃ cākṣamālāṃ ca | dadhatīṃ dakṣahastayoḥ || (RA_2.70) 
 pāśābhaye ca vāmābhyāṃ | candrārdhakṛtaśekharām | 
 rasāṅkuśīṃ mahādevīṃ | nīlagrīvāṃ kṛpāmayīm || (RA_2.71) 
 pūjayed rasasiddhyarthaṃ | vidyayā pañcabījayā | 
 vāgbhavaṃ bhuvaneśīṃ ca | śrībījaṃ ca sureśvari || (RA_2.72) 
 mādanaṃ śaktibījaṃ ca | vidyā paramadurlabhā | 
 dhūpadīpaistu naivedyaiḥ | puṣpatāmbūlacandanaiḥ ||
                    (RA_2.73) 
 śāntipāṭhasya nirghoṣaiḥ | stotramaṅgalanisvanaiḥ | 
 ghaṇṭāṭaṅkārasaṃyuktaiḥ | pūjāṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi ||
                    (RA_2.74) 
 aghoreṇa baliṃ dadyāt | sarvavighnopaśāntaye | 
 bhūtebhyo yakṣarakṣabhyo | piśācebhyaś ca yatnataḥ ||
                    (RA_2.75) 
 aghoramantrasaṃyuktam | oṃkārādinamo 'ntakam | 
 sarvakarmākaraṃ devi | vighnopadravanāśanam || (RA_2.76) 
 yathāśakti japitvā tu | vidyāmeva rasāṅkuśīm | 
 kuṇḍaṃ vidhāya deveśi | yonicakraṃ samekhalam || (RA_2.77) 
 tatrājyatilasaṃyuktaṃ | homaṃ kṛtvā krameṇa tu | 
 kalaśaṃ sthāpayed devi | payaḥpūrṇaṃ phalānvitam ||
                    (RA_2.78) 
 pañcaratnasamopetaṃ | vāsobhiḥ pariveṣṭitam | 
 tatrāṣṭādaśavidyābhir | abhimantrya pṛthak pṛthak ||
                    (RA_2.79) 
 gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūrṇaṃ | pallavair upaśobhitam | 
 arghyapātraṃ ca saṃpūjya | vardhanyābhyukṣya sādhakam ||
                    (RA_2.80) 
 śatamaṣṭottaraṃ caivam | arghyapātrodakena tu | 
 abhiṣicya vidhānena | kumbhatoyena mantravit || (RA_2.81) 
 vidyāmupadiśeddevi | pāṭhayed rasasādhakam | 
 kumāroyoginīyogi- | sādhakāṃś ca yathocitaiḥ || (RA_2.82) 
 tarpayed annapānaiś ca | jāgaraṃ tatra kārayet | 
 evaṃvihitadīkṣas tu | sādhakaḥ kṣuranāyike || (RA_2.83) 
 mahābhūtamayīṃ tatra | varṇapañcakasaṃyutām | 
 pañcabījātmikāṃ vidyāṃ | prāṇāyāmātmasūtrake || (RA_2.84) 
 mudrāṃ rasāṅkuśīṃ baddhvā | lakṣamekaṃ japetpriye | 
 tasya sidhyati deveśi | nirvighnaṃ rasabhairavaḥ ||
                    (RA_2.85) 
 praṇavādinamo 'ntas tu | tarpaṇānte japaḥ paraḥ | 
 ahiṃsā candanaṃ satyaṃ | puṣpam asteyadhūpanam || (RA_2.86) 
 brahmacaryaṃ mahādīpam | apratigrahaghaṇṭikām | 
 pāyasānnaṃ maheśāni | sarvabhūtadayātmakam || (RA_2.87) 
 saṃgūhyārādhayed devīṃ | sa bhavetsiddhibhājanam | 
 sahasraṃ vā śataṃ vāpi | trisaṃdhyaṃ saṃjapedimām ||
                    (RA_2.88) 
 asyā ājñāprasādena | jāyate khecaro rasaḥ | 
 divyauṣadhyaś ca tasyaiva | sidhyanti suravandite ||
                    (RA_2.89) 
 anaṅkuśaṃ samāruhya | vane mattagajaṃ yathā | 
 tathā rasāṅkuśābhijño | rasendraṃ prāpya sīdati || (RA_2.90) 
 vidyayā saha mantavyaṃ | guroḥ satsampradāyinaḥ | 
 rasaprayogajātaṃ tu | sarvataḥ siddhimicchatā || (RA_2.91) 
 atha praśnāvatārāya | pūrvoktaṃ rasabhairavam | 
 samāhitamanā dhyāyet | tadālīnaṃ samācaret || (RA_2.92) 
 anāhate brahmarandhre | manaḥ kṛtvā nirāmaye | 
 karanyāsaṃ purā kṛtvā | aṅganyāsamanantaram | 
 yathāśakti japenmantraṃ | rasendrasya samāhitaḥ || (RA_2.93) 
 catuṣkoṇaṃ punaḥ kṛtvā | madhye ṣaṭkoṇamaṇḍalam | 
 hastamātraṃ dvihastaṃ vā | taṇḍulair vimalair likhet ||
                    (RA_2.94) 
 sugandhair lepite sthāne | pūjayec candanādibhiḥ ||
                    (RA_2.95) 
 karṇikāyāṃ nyaseddevi | pūrvoktaṃ rasabhairavam | 
 ṣaṭkoṇe devatāṣaṭkaṃ | mahākālādi vinyaset || (RA_2.96) 
 mahākālaṃ mahābalam | aghoraṃ vajravīrakam | 
 nyaset krodhaṃ ca kaṅkālaṃ | mālāmantraiḥ samarcayet ||
                    (RA_2.97) 
 oṃ hrīṃ krauṃ kṣlaiṃ kṣlaṃ hrīṃ hrīṃ hrīṃ hrūḥ huṃ phaṭ raseśvarāya
                    mahākālabhairavāya raudrarūpāya kṛṣṇapiṅgalalocanāya | 
 avatara 2 avatāraya 2 jalpa 2 jalpaya 2 śubhāśubhaṃ kathaya 2 kathāpaya 2
                    mahārakṣāṃ kuru 2 rasasiddhiṃ dehi | 
 iti mālāmantrāḥ | 
 oṃ mahākālabhairavāya hṛdayāya namaḥ | 
 oṃ mahābalabhairavāya śirase svāhā | 
 oṃ aghorabhairavāya śikhāyai vauṣaṭ | 
 oṃ vajravīrabhairavāya kavacāya hum | 
 oṃ krodhabhairavāya netrāya vauṣaṭ | 
 oṃ kaṅkālabhairavāya astrāya phaṭ | 
 sarvatra svāhāntam | 
 evam aṅganyāsāḥ | 
 evam aṅgulīnyāsān kuryādādau | 
 ete ṣaḍaṅge pūjane ca mūlamantrāḥ | 
 evaṃ nyāsākṣaraḥ kuṭaiḥ | gandhapuṣpaiḥ samarcayet | 
 pūrṇakumbhaṃ nyasenmadhye | śarāvaṃ taṇḍulaiḥ saha ||
                    (RA_2.98) 
 tasyopari ghṛtadīpaṃ | vartīṃ mantraiś ca mantrayet ||
                    (RA_2.99) 
 samānīya kumārīṃ tu | kumāraṃ vā suśobhanam | 
 ekadvitricatuḥpañca | yathālābhaṃ samānayet | 
 gandhapuṣpair dhūpadīpaiḥ | naivedyena ca pūjayet ||
                    (RA_2.100) 
 ekaikasyā nyasenmantraṃ | hṛdayādyāś ca devatāḥ ||
                    (RA_2.101) 
 tato nirīkṣya taddīpaṃ | sarvāstatra kumārikāḥ | 
 paśyanti devatā dīpe | kumārāś ca śubhāśubham | 
 siddhiṃ vāpyathavāsiddhiṃ | kathayanti kumārikāḥ ||
                    (RA_2.102) 
 praśnāvatāraṃ jñātveti | rasakarmaṇi saṃcaret || (RA_2.103) 
 yaḥ purā devadeveśi | rasendre bhāvitātmavān | 
 saptajanma mṛto jāto | na tyajed rasabhāvanam || (RA_2.104) 
 evaṃ śubhāśubhaṃ jñātvā | devatānugrahānvitaḥ | 
 maṇḍape pūrvavaddevīm | arcayitvā rasāṅkuśīm || (RA_2.105) 
 ācāryam api saṃpūjya | dhūpasrakcandanādibhiḥ | 
 aghoreṇa baliṃ dattvā | tataḥ karma samācaret || (RA_2.106) 
 oṣadhyo maṇḍape prācyāṃ | rasasvedo 'gnigocare | 
 dakṣiṇasyāṃ lohamāro | nairṛtyāṃ peṣaṇādikam || (RA_2.107) 
 drutikriyā tu vāruṇyāṃ | vāyavye dhamanaṃ priye | 
 varṇotkarṣas tu kauberyām | aiśānyāṃ rasavedhanam ||
                    (RA_2.108) 
 āsanaṃ tu guror madhye | niveśya suranāyike | 
 niyāmanādikaṃ karma | krāmaṇāntaṃ varānane | 
 rasāṅkuśena mantreṇa | kartavyaṃ sādhakena tu || (RA_2.109) 
 yaḥ purā devadeveśi | varṇito rasabhairavaḥ | 
 sadyojātaṃ tasya jānu | vāmadevaṃ tu guhyakam || (RA_2.110) 
 aghoraṃ hṛdayaṃ tasya | vaktraṃ tatpuruṣaṃ smṛtam | 
 yāvad bhrūmadhyam īśānam | ardhacandraṃ lalāṭakam ||
                    (RA_2.111) 
 bindur deveśi tasyordhve | bindorūrdhve sthito nadaḥ | 
 lalāṭaśirasor madhye | śaktistatraiva saṃsthitā ||
                    (RA_2.112) 
 vyāpinī brahmarandhrasthā | tasyordhve tūnmanā bhavet | 
 unmanā unmanībhāvam | unmanāpadamavyayam || (RA_2.113) 
 tasyordhve paramaṃ satyaṃ | vyomasthāyi parātparam | 
 śūnyaṃ śūnyaṃ punaḥ śūnyaṃ | triśūnyaṃ ca nirāmayam ||
                    (RA_2.114) 
 nabhaś ca gaganaṃ vyoma | khamākāśaṃ ca kevalam | 
 niṣkalaṃ nirmalaṃ nityaṃ | nistaraṅgaṃ nirāmayam ||
                    (RA_2.115) 
 niṣprapañcaṃ nirādhāraṃ | nirguṇaṃ guṇagocaram | 
 evaṃrūpaṃ sadā dhyāyet | svadehe rasabhairavam ||
                    (RA_2.116) 
 yadā ca niścalaṃ dhyāyet | yadā ca niścalaṃ manaḥ | 
 vahnimadhye tadā sūto | badhyate niścalastathā ||
                    (RA_2.117) 
 yadā ca calati dhyānaṃ | raso vahnau na tiṣṭhati ||
                    (RA_2.118) 
 maṇḍalasya bahiḥ rātrau | surāmatsyāmiṣādibhiḥ | 
 arcayed yakṣagandharvān | piśācān rākṣasāṃstathā ||
                    (RA_2.119) 
 kriyākaraṇavighnāś ca | phalavighnāś ca koṭiśaḥ | 
 sambhavanti tathā tattac | chāntyai ca vaṭukeśvaram | 
 arcānugrahaṣaṭkaṃ ca | sampūjyādau samācaret || (RA_2.120) 
 karmānte ca punarbālam | aṣṭāṣṭakamanugraham | 
 sampūjya viniyuñjyāt tat | siddhadravyaṃ tu siddhidam ||
                    (RA_2.121) 
 siddhas tu nāśayed vādaṃ | taddeśaṃ tu parityajet | 
 bhramenmādhukarīṃ bhikṣāṃ | susiddhe tu mahārase ||
                    (RA_2.122) 
 pramādādutthito vighno | rasabandhe kṛte sati | 
 rasaśāntirvidhātavyā | rasakṣobhaṃ na kārayet || (RA_2.123) 
 rasaṃ na darśayed devi | nārīhaste na pātayet | 
 nāryai guhyaṃ na vaktavyaṃ | dravyaṃ tābhyo hi gopayet ||
                    (RA_2.124) 
 paradravyair na kartavyaṃ | paradārānna saṃspṛśet | 
 parānnaṃ naiva bhuñjīta | parāṃścaiva na viśvaset ||
                    (RA_2.125) 
 na deyaṃ duṣṭabuddhīnāṃ | goṣṭhīrūpeṇa yācake || (RA_2.126) 
 aṣṭamyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ ca | amāvāsyāṃ yugādiṣu | 
 ayane viṣuve caiva | caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ | 
 rasotsavaṃ prakurvīta | yathāvittānusārataḥ || (RA_2.127) 
 evaṃ rasotsavaṃ devi | yaḥ kuryādbhaktisaṃyutaḥ | 
 brahmahatyādipāpāni | naśyanti vividhāni ca || (RA_2.128) 
 anena vidhinā yatra | pūjāṃ kurvanti sādhakāḥ | 
 na tatra rogadaurgatyaṃ | netayaḥ prabhavanti ca ||
                    (RA_2.129) 
 evaṃvidhāṃ rase pūjāṃ | pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi | 
 paścāt karma vidhātavyam | ātmanaḥ śubham icchatām ||
                    (RA_2.130) 
 anyathā kurute yas tu | tasya siddhir na jāyate | 
 apāyaḥ pāpaśaṅkā ca | buddhibhaṅgo hi jāyate || (RA_2.131) 
 avajñā rogajātaṃ ca | saṃdehaś ca pade pade | 
 ālasyād gurulobhāc ca | parasya kathanena ca | 
 utpannam api vijñānaṃ | haranti kulakāḥ priye || (RA_2.132) 
 dīkṣito rasakarmāṇi | mantranyāsavid ācaret | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_2.133) 
 
 
 Tṛtīyaḥ paṭalaḥ [Mantranyāsāḥ] 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 bhagavan devadeveśa | lokanātha jagatpate | 
 mantranyāsaṃ samācakṣva | rasakarmopakārakam || (RA_3.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi | mantramūrtiṃ rasāṅkuśīm | 
 pañcamaṃ tu gṛhaṃ devi | durlabhaṃ devadānavaiḥ || (RA_3.2) 
 catvāraḥ pradhānagṛhāḥ | haṃsagṛhaṃ tu pañcamam | 
 yatra siddhir makārādiḥ | tiṣṭhate pañcame gṛhe || (RA_3.3) 
 liṅgāśrayaṃ yathā rūpaṃ | liṅgimāyā tu liṅginī | 
 gaganena tu sā jñeyā | bhagarekhā tu pañcame || (RA_3.4) 
 praṇavaṃ pūrvam uccārya | bījaṃ śabdamanuttaram | 
 hrīṃkāraṃ caiva krīṃkāraṃ | haṃsabuddhimanantaram || (RA_3.5) 
 kālapāśaṃ mahāmantraṃ | gṛhṇīyāt sādhakeśvaraḥ | 
 mahārambhe tu tanmantraṃ | pratīhāraṃ rasāṅkuśīm || (RA_3.6) 
 lakṣamekaṃ japettasya | mahāsiddhiḥ pravartate | 
 bālavatsapurīṣaṃ tu | tataḥ kenaiva grāhayet || (RA_3.7) 
 citāgnibhasma tenaiva | grāhayet parameśvari | 
 kṣetraṃ taduttamaṃ sthānaṃ | rasendrastatra tiṣṭhati ||
                    (RA_3.8) 
 mārjanyā mārjayetsthānaṃ | kubjikākhyā tu khecarī | 
 dvātriṃśadakṣarā devi | pañcanādeṣu saṃsthitā || (RA_3.9) 
 tataḥ siddhāś ca catvāraḥ | puruṣāṣṭādaśa smṛtāḥ | 
 arthapañcakasaṃyuktā | dhyānaṃ syāt pañcakaṃ punaḥ ||
                    (RA_3.10) 
 yoginīṣaṭkasaṃyuktaṃ | saptaviṃśatkramānvitam | 
 ekāśītipadair yuktaṃ | pañcāvaraṇasaṃyutam || (RA_3.11) 
 anena kramayogena | mārjanīṃ paripūjayet | 
 anena mārjayet kṣetraṃ | rasendro yatra tiṣṭhati ||
                    (RA_3.12) 
 upalepaṃ tu tatraiva | caṇḍaghaṇṭāṃ tu kārayet | 
 pūrve gṛhe tu sā devī | caṇḍaghaṇṭā vyavasthitā || (RA_3.13) 
 caṇḍabhairavikā devī | saṃsthitā dakṣiṇe gṛhe | 
 gomayaṃ tena gṛhṇīyāl | lepanārthaṃ varānane || (RA_3.14) 
 caṇḍakāpālinī devī | saṃsthitā cottare gṛhe | 
 gṛhītvā codakaṃ tena | lepayed bhūmimaṇḍalam || (RA_3.15) 
 saptadaśākṣarāṃ kālīṃ | khallapāṣāṇato nyaset | 
 dvātriṃśadakṣaraṃ ghoraṃ | mardake tu niyojayet || (RA_3.16) 
 gṛhṇīyāt kāñjikāṃ devi | kālapāśena mantritaḥ | 
 evaṃ sukarmasaṃyogaṃ | kurute khecarīkulam || (RA_3.17) 
 aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi | yāḥ sthitā divyakhecarī | 
 tāḥ sarvāḥ kiṃkarāstasya | auṣadhaṃ peṣayanti tāḥ ||
                    (RA_3.18) 
 tāsāṃ sarvaṃ tu mantraikaṃ | caturakṣarasaṃyutam | 
 so 'haṃ haṃsaḥ | 
 sā vidyā khecarīṇāṃ tu | nāmnāṃ tu kulakhecarī || (RA_3.19) 
 rājikāṃ saindhavaṃ nyasya | sā vidyā kulakhecarī | 
 mantrayet kāñjikāṃ tatra | mantrarājo rasāṅkuśī || (RA_3.20) 
 astravidyāṃ japettatra | yā jñātā pūrvabhārgave | 
 guḍeṣṭakāṃ tu saṃmardya | priye tanmarditaṃ rasam ||
                    (RA_3.21) 
 kā kathā mantrarājasya | na vākyaṃ triśirasya ca | 
 ṣaḍaṅgaṃ yojayet tāṃ tu | tvaritaṃ dhārayet tataḥ ||
                    (RA_3.22) 
 ḍāmarākhyaṃ mahāmantraṃ | dhamanīṣu niyojayet | 
 cintāmaṇimahāvidyāṃ | kavaceṣu niyojayet || (RA_3.23) 
 caṇḍikāyā mahāmantraṃ | taṃ tu pātre niyojayet | 
 navavidyāṃ varārohe | vinyasettuṣagomaye || (RA_3.24) 
 tripurābhairavīṃ devīṃ | rājikākāñjike nyaset | 
 guḍasya kālarātris tu | nyastavyā vīravandite || (RA_3.25) 
 trikūṭākṣaṃ trinetraṃ tu | analasya tu vinyaset | 
 udake vinyaseddevi | caturaśīticaṇḍikāḥ || (RA_3.26) 
 kṣetrapālamaghorāstraṃ | nyastavyaṃ koṣṭhake priye | 
 mahāpāśupatāstraṃ tu | mūṣāyāṃ ca niyojayet || (RA_3.27) 
 etanmantragaṇaṃ devi | rasasthāne niyojayet | 
 tadā tu sidhyate tasya | sādhakasya phalaṃ priye ||
                    (RA_3.28) 
 rasāṅkuśaṃ mahāmantraṃ | japet tu hṛdayāntare | 
 anye ye yoginīmantrāḥ | sarvānnārīś ca jāpayet || (RA_3.29) 
 aprakāśaṃ tu tenaiva | mantrarājaṃ rasāṅkuśam | 
 aprakāśaṃ ca nārīṇāṃ | rakṣayetpraṇavaṃ tathā | 
 mahāsamayavibhraṃśaṃ | nārīṇāṃ hṛdayaṃ yathā || (RA_3.30) 
 kubjikādyāstu ye mantrā | mayā te saṃprakāśitāḥ | 
 trailokyaṃ kṣobhitāste tu | na manyante mama priye ||
                    (RA_3.31) 
 rasāṅkuśena jñānena | trailokyaṃ vaśyatāṃ vrajet ||
                    (RA_3.32) 
 mantranyāsamiti jñātvā | yantramūṣāgnimānavit | 
 kurvāṇo rasakarmāṇi | siddhiṃ prāpnoti sādhakaḥ || (RA_3.33) 
 
 
 Caturthaḥ paṭalaḥ [Yantramūṣāgnivarṇanaḥ] 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 yantramūṣāgnimānāni | na jñātvā mantravedyapi | 
 kiṃ karoti mahādeva | tāni me vaktumarhasi || (RA_4.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 rasoparasalohāni | vasanaṃ kāñjikam viḍam | 
 dhamanīlohayantrāṇi | khallapāṣāṇamardakam || (RA_4.2) 
 koṣṭhikā vakranālaṃ ca | gomayaṃ sāramindhanam | 
 mṛnmayāni ca yantrāṇi | musalolūkhalāni ca || (RA_4.3) 
 saṇḍasīpaṭṭasaṃdaṃśaṃ | mṛtpātrāyaḥkaṭorakam | 
 pratimānāni ca tulā- | chedanāni kaṣopalam || (RA_4.4) 
 vaṃśanāḍīlohanāḍīm | ūṣāṅgārāṃs tathauṣadhīḥ | 
 snehāmlalavaṇakṣāra- | viṣāṇyupaviṣāṇi ca || (RA_4.5) 
 evaṃ saṃgūhya sambhāraṃ | karmayogaṃ samācaret || (RA_4.6) 
 dravadravyeṇa bhāṇḍasya | pūritārdhodarasya ca | 
 mukhe tiryakkṛte bhāṇḍe | rasaṃ sūtreṇa lambitam | 
 taṃ svedayet talagataṃ | dolāyantramiti smṛtam || (RA_4.7) 
 lohamūṣādvayaṃ kṛtvā | dvādaśāṅgulamānataḥ | 
 īṣac chidrānvitām ekāṃ | tatra gandhakasaṃyutām || (RA_4.8) 
 mūṣāyāṃ rasayuktāyām | anyasyāṃ tāṃ praveśayet | 
 toyaṃ syāt sūtakasyādhaḥ | ūrdhvādho vahnidīpanam || (RA_4.9) 
 rasonakarasaṃ bhadre | yatnato vastragālitam | 
 dāpayetpracuraṃ yatnāt | āplāvya rasagandhakau || (RA_4.10) 
 sthālikāyāṃ nidhāyordhvaṃ | sthālīm anyāṃ dṛḍhāṃ kuru | 
 saṃdhiṃ vilepayed yatnāt | mṛdā vastreṇa caiva hi ||
                    (RA_4.11) 
 sthālyantare kapotākhyaṃ | puṭaṃ karṣāgninā sadā | 
 yantrasyādhaḥ karīṣāgniṃ | dadyāttīvrāgnimeva vā ||
                    (RA_4.12) 
 evaṃ tu tridinaṃ kuryāt | tato yantraṃ vimocayet | 
 taptodake taptacullyāṃ | na kuryāc chītale kriyām ||
                    (RA_4.13) 
 na tatra kṣīyate sūto | na ca gacchati kutracit | 
 anena kramayogena | kuryādgandhakajāraṇam || (RA_4.14) 
 ūrdhvaṃ vahniradhaścāpo | madhye tu rasasaṃgrahaḥ | 
 mūṣāyantramidaṃ devi | jārayed gaganādikam || (RA_4.15) 
 garbhayantraṃ pravakṣyāmi | piṣṭikābhasmakāraṇam | 
 caturaṅguladīrghāṃ tu | mūṣikāṃ mṛnmayīṃ dṛḍhām || (RA_4.16) 
 tryaṅgulāṃ madhyavistāre | vartulaṃ kārayen mukham | 
 lohasya viṃśatirbhāgā | eko bhāgas tu gugguloḥ || (RA_4.17) 
 suślakṣṇaṃ peṣayitvā tu | toyaṃ dadyāt punaḥ punaḥ | 
 mūṣālepaṃ tataḥ kuryāt | tale piṣṭīṃ ca nikṣipet ||
                    (RA_4.18) 
 tuṣakarṣāgninā bhūmau | mṛdusvedaṃ tu kārayet | 
 ahorātraṃ trirātraṃ vā | rasendro bhasmatāṃ vrajet ||
                    (RA_4.19) 
 jāraṇe māraṇe caiva | rasarājasya rañjane | 
 yantramekaṃ paraṃ marma | yatrauṣadhyo mahābalam ||
                    (RA_4.20) 
 auṣadhīrahitaścāyaṃ | haṭhādyantreṇa badhyate | 
 sarvatra sūtako yāti | muktvā bhūdharalakṣaṇam || (RA_4.21) 
 devatābhiḥ samākṛṣṭo | loṣṭastho 'pi hi gacchati | 
 tasmādyantrabalaṃ caikaṃ | na vilaṅghyaṃ vijānatā ||
                    (RA_4.22) 
 mantrauṣadhisamāyogāt | susiddhaṃ kurute hy ayam | 
 mantro 'ghoro 'tra japtavyo | japānte pūjayed rasam ||
                    (RA_4.23) 
 ekānte tu kriyā kāryā | dṛṣṭān yair viphalā bhavet ||
                    (RA_4.24) 
 gandhakasya kṣayo nāsti | na rasasya kṣayo bhavet | 
 kṣayo yantrasya vijñeyaḥ | yantre vikriyate kriyā | 
 alābhe kāntalohasya | yantraṃ lohena kārayet || (RA_4.25) 
 vahnilakṣyam avijñāya | rasasyārdhakṣayo bhavet | 
 yantrakṣayavidhijñasya | caturthāṃśakṣayo bhavet ||
                    (RA_4.26) 
 dvimāsena dvitīyāṃśaṃ | tṛtīyāṃśaṃ tribhirbhavet | 
 mahāgniṃ sahate hy eṣa | sārito yatra tiṣṭhati || (RA_4.27) 
 kharparaṃ sikatāpūrṇaṃ | kṛtvā tasyopari nyaset | 
 aparaṃ kharparaṃ tatra | śanair mṛdvagninā pacet ||
                    (RA_4.28) 
 pañcakṣāraistathā mūtrair | lavaṇaiś ca viḍaṃ tataḥ | 
 haṃsapākaḥ sa vijñāto | yantratantrārthakovidaiḥ ||
                    (RA_4.29) 
 kṛṣṇā raktā ca pītā ca | śuklavarṇā ca mṛttikā | 
 ādyā śreṣṭhā kaniṣṭhāntyā | madhyamā madhyamā matā ||
                    (RA_4.30) 
 dagdhadhānyatuṣopetā | mṛttikā koṣṭhikāvidhau | 
 vakranālakṛtā vāpi | śasyate surasundari || (RA_4.31) 
 gārā dagdhā tuṣā dagdhā | dagdhā valmīkamṛttikā | 
 ajāśvānāṃ malaṃ dagdhaṃ | yāvattat kṛṣṇatāṃ gatam ||
                    (RA_4.32) 
 vāsakasya ca pattrāṇi | valmīkasya mṛdā saha | 
 peṣayed vahnitoyena | yāvattat ślakṣṇatāṃ gatam || (RA_4.33) 
 mardayet tena badhnīyāt | vakranālaṃ ca koṣṭhikām ||
                    (RA_4.34) 
 gārā dagdhā tuṣā dagdhā | dagdhā valmīkamṛttikā | 
 cīramaṅgārakaḥ kiṭṭaṃ | vajreṇāpi na bhidyate || (RA_4.35) 
 dagdhāṅgārasya ṣaḍbhāgā | bhāgaikā kṛṣṇamṛttikā | 
 cīramaṅgārakaḥ kiṭṭaṃ | vajramūṣā prakīrtitā || (RA_4.36) 
 tuṣaṃ vastrasamaṃ dagdhāṃ | mṛttikā caturaṃśikā | 
 kupīpāṣāṇasaṃyuktā | varamūṣā prakīrtitā || (RA_4.37) 
 prakāśā cāndhamūṣā ca | mūṣā tu dvividhā smṛtā || (RA_4.38) 
 prakāśamūṣā deveśi | śarāvākārasaṃyutā | 
 dravyanirvāhaṇe sā ca | vādikaiḥ supraśasyate || (RA_4.39) 
 andhamūṣā tu kartavyā | gostanākārasaṃnibhā | 
 pidhānakasamāyuktā | kiṃcid unnatamastakā || (RA_4.40) 
 pattralepe tathā raṅge | dvaṃdvamelāpake tathā | 
 saiva chidrānvitā mandā | gambhīrā sāraṇocitā || (RA_4.41) 
 tilabhasma dvir aṃśaṃ tu | iṣṭakāṃśasamanvitam | 
 bhasmamūṣā tu vijñeyā | tārāsaṃśodhane hitā || (RA_4.42) 
 mokṣakṣārasya bhāgau dvau | iṣṭakāṃśasamanvitau | 
 mṛdbhāgās tāraśuddhyartham | uttamā varavarṇini || (RA_4.43) 
 raktavargeṇa sammiśrā | raktavargapariplutā | 
 raktavargakṛtālepā | sarvaśuddhiṣu śobhanā || (RA_4.44) 
 śuklavargeṇa sammiśrā | śuklavargapariplutā | 
 śuklavargakṛtālepā | śuklaśuddhiṣu śobhanā || (RA_4.45) 
 viḍavargeṇa sammiśrā | dhṛtimicchati jāraṇe | 
 nirvāhaṇaṃ prakurvīta | raktavargapraliptayā || (RA_4.46) 
 viṣaṭaṅkaṇaguñjābhiḥ | mūṣālepaṃ tu kārayet | 
 prakāśāyāṃ prakurvīta | yadi vāṅgāralepanam || (RA_4.47) 
 tasyāṃ vinyasya mūṣāyāṃ | dravyamāvartayed budhaḥ | 
 lepo varṇapuṭaṃ devi | raktamṛtsindhubhūkhagaiḥ || (RA_4.48) 
 āvartamāne kanake | pītā tāre sitā prabhā | 
 śulve nīlanibhā tīkṣṇe | kṛṣṇavarṇā sureśvari || (RA_4.49) 
 vaṅge jvālā kapotābhā | nāge malinadhūmakā | 
 śaile tu dhūsarā devi | āyase kapilaprabhā || (RA_4.50) 
 ayaskānte dhūmravarṇā | sasyake lohitā bhavet | 
 vajre nānāvidhā jvālā | khasattve pāṇḍuraprabhā || (RA_4.51) 
 na visphuliṅgo na ca budbudaś ca | yadā na rekhāpaṭalaṃ na śabdaḥ | 
 mūṣāgataṃ ratnasamaṃ sthiraṃ ca | tadā viśuddhaṃ pravadanti
                    loham || (RA_4.52) 
 pratīvāpaḥ purā yojyo | niṣekastadanantaram | 
 chādanaṃ tu pratīvāpaḥ | niṣekaṃ majjanaṃ viduḥ | 
 abhiṣekaṃ tadicchanti | snapanaṃ kriyate tu yat || (RA_4.53) 
 vāpo niṣekaḥ snapanaṃ | drute nirmalatāṃ gate | 
 uṣṇenaiva hi vāñchanti | śītalaṃ na ca vāñchati || (RA_4.54) 
 śukladīptiḥ saśabdaś ca | yadā vaiśvānaro bhavet | 
 lohāvartaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ | sattvaṃ patati nirmalam ||
                    (RA_4.55) 
 ṣoḍaśāṅgulavistīrṇaṃ | hastamātrāyataṃ śubham | 
 dhātusattvanipātārthaṃ | koṣṭhakaṃ varavarṇini || (RA_4.56) 
 vaṃśakhādiramādhūka- | badarīdārusambhavaḥ | 
 paripūrṇaṃ dṛḍhāṅgāraiḥ | dhamedvātena koṣṭhakam | 
 bhastrayā jvālamārgeṇa | jvālayec ca hutāśanam || (RA_4.57) 
 pravitatamukhabhāgaṃ saṃvṛtāntaḥpradeśaṃ | sthalaracitacirāntarjālakaṃ koṣṭhakaṃ
                    syāt | 
 bakagalasamamānaṃ vaṅkanālaṃ vidheyaṃ | śuṣiranalinikā syānmṛnmayī dīrghavṛttā ||
                    Ras_4.58 || 
 mṛnmaye lohapātre vā | ayaskāntamaye 'thavā | 
 pāṣāṇe sphaṭike vātha | muktāśailamaye 'thavā || (RA_4.59) 
 sudṛḍho mardakaḥ kāryaḥ | caturaṅgulakocchrayaḥ | 
 sa ca lohamayaḥ śailo | hy ayaskāntamayo 'thavā || (RA_4.60) 
 aghorāstrābhidhānena | mahāpāśupatena vā | 
 mantreṇa racayec chuddhiṃ | bhūmiṃ tenaiva śodhayet ||
                    (RA_4.61) 
 indhanāni ca sarvāṇi | dravyāṇi ca viśeṣataḥ | 
 dāhakaṃ jvālayet tena | khallaṃ tenaiva śodhayet ||
                    (RA_4.62) 
 rasaṃ viśodhayet tena | vinyaset divase śubhe | 
 khallopari nyasitvā ca | śivamūrtimanusmaret || (RA_4.63) 
 devatānugrahaṃ prāpya | yantramūṣāgnimānavit | 
 deveśi rasasiddhyarthaṃ | jānīyāt oṣadhīrapi || (RA_4.64) 
 yantramūṣāgnimānāni | varṇitāni sureśvari | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_4.65) 
 
 
 Pañcamaḥ paṭalaḥ [Oṣadhinirṇaya] 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 niyāmanādikaṃ karma | krāmaṇāntaṃ sureśvara | 
 yayā sampadyate hy eṣām | oṣadhīṃ vaktumarhasi || (RA_5.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 sarpākṣo vahnikarkoṭī | kañcukī jalabindujā | 
 śatāvarī bhṛṅgarājaḥ | śarapuṅkhā punarnavā || (RA_5.2) 
 maṇḍūkaparṇī matsyākṣī | brahmadaṇḍī śikhaṇḍinī | 
 anantā kākajaṅghā ca | kākamācī kapotikā || (RA_5.3) 
 viṣṇukrāntā sahacarā | sahādevī mahābalā | 
 balā nāgabalā kṛṣṇā | cakramardaḥ kuruṅgiṇī || (RA_5.4) 
 pāṭhā cāmalakī nīlī | jvālinī padmacāriṇī | 
 phaṇitrijihvā gojihvā | kokilākṣo ghanadhvaniḥ || (RA_5.5) 
 ākhuparṇī triparṇī ca | dviparṇī caikaparṇikā | 
 tittiḍī kṣīriṇī rāsnā | meṣaśṛṅgī ca kukkuṭī || (RA_5.6) 
 kṛṣṇaparṇī ca tulasī | śvetā ca girikarṇikā | 
 etā niyāmakauṣadhyaḥ | puṣpamūladalānvitāḥ | 
 dolāsvedaḥ prakartavyo | mūlenānena suvrate || (RA_5.7) 
 caṇḍālī rākṣasī vyāghrī | khaḍgārī gajakarṇikā | 
 śaṅkhapuṣpyagnidhamanī | lāṅgalī bālamocakā || (RA_5.8) 
 raktasnuhī raktaśṛṅgī | raktikā nīlacitrakaḥ | 
 śṛgālajihvā bṛhatī | vajrā cakrī ca rājikā || (RA_5.9) 
 ekavīrā narakasā | rudantī brahmacāriṇī | 
 uccaṭā māninīkandā | kumārī raktacitrakaḥ || (RA_5.10) 
 lakṣmīḥ śākhoṭakaścaiva | kañcukī meṣaśṛṅgikā | 
 himāvatī somalatā | modā vyāghranakhī śamī || (RA_5.11) 
 kāñcanī vanarājī ca | kākamācī ca keśinī | 
 ajamārī koṭarākṣī | hanūmatyaṅganāyikā || (RA_5.12) 
 narajīvā hemapuṣpī | kākamuṇḍī ca kālikā | 
 toyavallī gajārī ca | haṃsāṅghrī kuhukaṃvikā | 
 tāmbūlī sūryabhaktā ca | rasanirjīvakārikāḥ || (RA_5.13) 
 kaṭutumbī ca gosandhī | devadālīndravāruṇī | 
 vākucī brahmabījāni | kārpāsaṃ kṛṣṇajīrakam || (RA_5.14) 
 kaṅgunī kṛṣṇakanakaṃ | śvetārkaṃ ca pipīlijam | 
 dantinī yavaciñcā ca | karkoṭī kāravallikā || (RA_5.15) 
 gojihvā kākajaṅghā ca | mahākālī ca śambarī | 
 śvetaguñjā sitāṅkolaḥ | paṭolī bilvameva ca | 
 ekaikamoṣadhībījaṃ | mārayed rasabhairavam || (RA_5.16) 
 raktasnuhī somalatā | rudantī raktacitrakaḥ | 
 śākhoṭakī dagdharuhā | modinī vṛddhadārukaḥ || (RA_5.17) 
 triśūlī kṛṣṇamārjārī | cakrikā kṣīrakukkuṭī | 
 devadālī śaṅkhapuṣpī | kākamācī hanūmatī || (RA_5.18) 
 nīlajyotis tṛṇajyotir | utkaṭā hemavallarī | 
 tridaṇḍī brahmadaṇḍī ca | cakrāṅkī sthalapadminī ||
                    (RA_5.19) 
 nāgajihvā nāgakarṇī | vīrā vartulaparṇikā | 
 arkapattrī vaṃśapattrī | tāmraparṇī tatheśvarī | 
 indurī devadeveśi | rasabandhakarāḥ priye || (RA_5.20) 
 tīvragandharasasparśair | dravyaiḥ sthāvarajaṅgamaiḥ | 
 mriyate badhyate caiva | rasaḥ svedanamardanāt || (RA_5.21) 
 sūryāvartaś ca kadalī | vandhyā kośātakī tathā | 
 vajrakandodakakaṇā | kākamācī ca śigrukaḥ || (RA_5.22) 
 devadālī ca deveśi | drāvikāḥ parikīrtitāḥ | 
 doṣān haranti yogina | dhātūnāṃ pāradasya ca || (RA_5.23) 
 kākamācī ghanaravaḥ | kāsamardaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ | 
 varāhakarṇī saṭirī | haṃsadāvī śatāvarī || (RA_5.24) 
 tāmbūlī nāginī brahmī | haṃsapādī ca lakṣaṇā | 
 arjunī kṣīranālī ca | kāravello 'rkapattrikā | 
 vyāghrī cavī kuravakaḥ | krāmikāḥ suravandite || (RA_5.25) 
 brahmadaṇḍaḥ sudaṇḍaś ca | lohadaṇḍastṛtīyakaḥ | 
 ete rasāyane yogyā | brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ || (RA_5.26) 
 bhūpāṭalī ca kaumārī | siṃhavallī ca śūkarī | 
 hemaparṇī paṭolī ca | nāgavallī ca bhṛṅgarāṭ | 
 ityaṣṭa mūlikāḥ proktāḥ | pañcaratnaṃ śṛṇu priye ||
                    (RA_5.27) 
 mantrasiddhāsanā devī | tathā kaṅkālakhecarī | 
 indirā ca kṣamāpālī | pañcamī tu niśācarī | 
 pañcaratnamidaṃ devi | rasaśodhanajāraṇe || (RA_5.28) 
 rasasya bandhane śastam | ekaikaṃ suravandite | 
 rasāṅkuśena gṛhṇīyāt | pañcaratnāni suvrate | 
 dadāti khecarīṃ siddhiṃ | rasabhairavasaṃgame || (RA_5.29) 
 trikṣāraṃ ṭaṅkaṇakṣāro | yavakṣāraś ca sarjikā | 
 tilāpāmārgakadalī | palāśaśigrumocikāḥ | 
 mūlakārdrakaciñcāś ca | vṛkṣakṣārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || (RA_5.30) 
 amlavetasajambīra- | luṅgāmlacaṇakāmlakam | 
 nāraṅgaṃ tintiṇīkaṃ ca | cāṅgeryamlagaṇottamāḥ || (RA_5.31) 
 sāmudraṃ saindhavaṃ caiva | cūlikālavaṇaṃ tathā | 
 sauvarcalaṃ ca kācaṃ ca | lavaṇāḥ pañca kīrtitāḥ ||
                    (RA_5.32) 
 saktukaṃ kālakūṭaṃ ca | sitamustā tathaiva ca | 
 śṛṅgī kṛṣṇaviṣaṃ caiva | pañcaite tu mahāviṣāḥ || (RA_5.33) 
 snuhyarkonmattakaṃ caiva | karavīraṃ ca lāṅgalī | 
 pañcaivopaviṣā mukhyāḥ | tailāni hy uttamāni vai | 
 kusumbhakaṅguṇīnaktā- | tilasarṣapajāni tu || (RA_5.34) 
 hastyaśvachāganārīṇāṃ | mūtraṃ gavyaṃ ca pañcamam ||
                    (RA_5.35) 
 pittaṃ pañcavidhaṃ matsya- | gavāśvanarabarhijam ||
                    (RA_5.36) 
 vasā pañcavidhā matsya- | meṣāhinarabarhijā || (RA_5.37) 
 kapotacāṣagṛdhrāṇāṃ | śikhikukkuṭayoś ca viṭ || (RA_5.38) 
 mañjiṣṭhā kuṅkumaṃ lākṣā | khadiraścāsanaṃ tathā | 
 raktavargas tu deveśi | pītavargamataḥ śṛṇu | 
 kusumbhaṃ kiṃśukaṃ rātrī | pataṃgo madayantikā || (RA_5.39) 
 śuklavargaḥ sudhākūrma- | śaṅkhaśuktivarāṭikāḥ || (RA_5.40) 
 guñjāṭaṅkaṇamadhvājya- | guḍā drāvaṇapañcakam || (RA_5.41) 
 kācaṭaṅkaṇasauvīraṃ | śodhanatritayaṃ priye || (RA_5.42) 
 sarve malaharāḥ kṣārāḥ | sarve cāmlāḥ prabodhakāḥ | 
 viṣāṇi ca tamoghnāni | snehā mārdavakārakāḥ || (RA_5.43) 
 ityoṣadhigaṇāḥ proktāḥ | siddhidā rasasaṃgame | 
 kriyāṃ kurvanti tadyogāt | śaktayaś ca mahārasāḥ ||
                    (RA_5.44) 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_5.45) 
 
 
 Ṣaṣṭhaḥ paṭalaḥ [Abhrakādilakṣaṇasaṃskāranirṇaya] 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 devadeva mahādeva | śaktīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ katham | 
 rasakarmaṇi yogyatve | saṃskāras tasya kathyatām || (RA_6.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 kadācidgirijā devī | haraṃ dṛṣṭvā manoharam | 
 mumoca yattadā vīryaṃ | tajjātaṃ śubhamabhrakam | 
 pītaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tathā śuklaṃ | raktaṃ bhūmeś ca saṃgamāt ||
                    (RA_6.2) 
 abhrakaṃ kāntapāṣāṇaṃ | vajraṃ vaikrāntakaṃ śṛṇu || (RA_6.3) 
 pinākaṃ darduraṃ nāgaṃ | vajraṃ cābhraṃ caturvidham | 
 pināke 'gniṃ praviṣṭe tu | śabdaś ciṭiciṭir bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.4) 
 dardure 'gniṃ praviṣṭe tu | śabdaḥ kukkuṭavadbhavet | 
 agniṃ praviṣṭaṃ nāgaṃ tu | phūtkāraṃ devi muñcati || (RA_6.5) 
 agniṃ praviṣṭaṃ vajraṃ tu | vajravattiṣṭhati priye ||
                    (RA_6.6) 
 kuṣṭhapradaṃ pinākābhraṃ | darduraṃ maraṇapradam | 
 nāgaṃ dehagataṃ nityaṃ | vyādhiṃ kuryād bhagaṃdaram ||
                    (RA_6.7) 
 rase rasāyane caiva | yojyaṃ vajrābhrakaṃ priye | 
 anekavarṇabhedena | taccaturvidhamabhrakam || (RA_6.8) 
 raktaṃ pītaṃ ca hemārthe | kṛṣṇaṃ hemaśarīrayoḥ | 
 tārakarmaṇi śuklaṃ ca | kācakiṭṭaṃ sadā tyajet || (RA_6.9) 
 ekapattraṃ kṛtaṃ pūrvam | abhrakaṃ suranāyike | 
 agastyapuṣpatoyena | kumudānāṃ rasena ca || (RA_6.10) 
 kapitindukajambīra- | meghanādapunarnavaiḥ | 
 yavaciñcāranālāmla- | karavīrāruṇotpalaiḥ || (RA_6.11) 
 vanasūraṇabhūdhātrī- | bhiṇḍīmūlāmlavetasaiḥ | 
 meṣaśṛṅgīśaśavasā- | śṛṅgatailaśamīrasaiḥ || (RA_6.12) 
 vajravallīkṣīrakanda- | maricaiḥ sumukhena ca | 
 tridinaṃ svedayed devi | jāyate doṣavarjitam || (RA_6.13) 
 dhānyābhrakaṃ purā kṛtvā | suślakṣṇaṃ navanītavat | 
 triṃśatpalaṃ vyomarajaḥ | kṣudramatsyapaladvayam ||
                    (RA_6.14) 
 tilacūrṇapalaṃ guñjā- | tripalaṃ pādaṭaṅkaṇam | 
 godhūmabaddhā tatpiṇḍī | pañcagavyena bhāvitā || (RA_6.15) 
 dhamanāt koṣṭhikāyantre | bhastrābhyāṃ tīvravahninā | 
 patatyabhrakasattvaṃ tu | sattvāni nikhilāni ca || (RA_6.16) 
 svedanauṣadhiniryāsa- | lolitaṃ puṭitaṃ muhuḥ | 
 mṛtaṃ tu pañcanicula- | puṭair bahulapotakam || (RA_6.17) 
 piṇḍitaṃ vyoma niṣkledaṃ | dattvā sattvaṃ nirañjanam | 
 umāphalaiś ca puṣpaiś ca | ṣaṣṭikāmlapariplutaiḥ | 
 aumadaṇḍavimardena | gamanaṃ dravati sphuṭam || (RA_6.18) 
 agnijāraṃ nave kumbhe | sthāpayitvā dharottaram | 
 gaganaṃ dravati kṣipraṃ | muktāphalasamaprabham || (RA_6.19) 
 śatadhā kañcukīcūrṇaṃ | kañcukīrasabhāvitam | 
 drāvayed gaganaṃ devi | lohāni sakalāni ca || (RA_6.20) 
 dhānyāmlake paryyuṣitaṃ | niculakṣāravāriṇi | 
 sthitaṃ taddravatāṃ vāti | nirleparasasannibham || (RA_6.21) 
 agastyapuṣpatoyena | piṣṭvā sūraṇakandake | 
 koṣṭhabhūmigataṃ māsaṃ | jāyate rasasannibham || (RA_6.22) 
 chāgamūtreṇa saṃsiktaṃ | kapitindukareṇunā | 
 abhrakaṃ vāpitaṃ devi | jāyate jalasannibham || (RA_6.23) 
 kākinīvījacūrṇena | ghṛṣṭamabhrakajaṃ rajaḥ | 
 snuhikṣīreṇa saptāhaṃ | siktaṃ dhmātaṃ drutaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.24) 
 apāmārgasya pañcāṅgam | abhrakaṃ ca supeṣitam | 
 sthāpayen mṛnmaye pātre | tadbhavet salilaṃ yathā ||
                    (RA_6.25) 
 ghṛṣṭamabhrakacūrṇaṃ tu | kapālīmaricaiḥ saha | 
 śilayā vāpitaṃ bhūyo 'py | agastyarasasaṃyutam || (RA_6.26) 
 mārjārapādīsvarasa- | phalamūlāmlamarditam | 
 mātuluṅgaphale nyastaṃ | vrīhimadhye nidhāpayet | 
 taddravet pakṣamātreṇa | śilāsaindhavayojitam || (RA_6.27) 
 ekapatrīkṛtaṃ sapta- | dinaṃ munirase kṣipet | 
 dārvīmaricasaṃmiśraṃ | maurvīrasapariplutam || (RA_6.28) 
 sauvarccalayuto meghā | vajravallīrasaplutaḥ | 
 śarāvasaṃpuṭe dhmāto | jāyate jalasannibhaḥ || (RA_6.29) 
 vegāphalasya cūrṇena | samamabhrakajaṃ rajaḥ | 
 bhāvitāṃ kuliśakṣīre | dhmātaṃ dravati tatkṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_6.30) 
 vajravallīrasaiḥ piṣṭvā | vyoma sauvarcalānvitam | 
 śarāvasaṃṣuṭe paktvā | dravet salilasannibham || (RA_6.31) 
 gomāṃsasaindhavārkaistu | munitoyayutaṃ punaḥ | 
 kadalīkandakāntaḥsthaṃ | gomayāgnau tryahaṃ dravet ||
                    (RA_6.32) 
 kṛṣṇābhrapatraṃ saṃgṛhya | pīlutailena lepayet | 
 saptāhamātape taptam | āmle kṣiptvā dinatrayam || (RA_6.33) 
 vajrārkacitrakakṣāraṃ | tumbīkṣārastathārjunaḥ | 
 sarjakṣāro yavakṣāra- | ṣṭaṅkaṇaścāṣṭamo bhavet || (RA_6.34) 
 kṣīrakandarasaṃ caiva | vajrakandarasaṃ tathā | 
 vṛhatītrayasaṃyuktaṃ | kṣāravargañca lepayet || (RA_6.35) 
 kalkenānena liptaṃ tat | patrābhraṃ kāṃsyabhājane | 
 dhamanāt sūryyatāpotthāt | tridinena drutaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.36) 
 athavābhrakapatraṃ tu | kañcukokṣīramadhyagam | 
 bhāvayec ca tathā tena | yāvaccūrṇaṃ tato bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.37) 
 grāhayed abhrapatrāṇi | nikṣipyāmle dinatrayam | 
 lepayet tena kalkena | kāṃsyapātre nidhāpayet | 
 sūryyatāpena saptāhaṃ | drutiḥ sañjāyate kṣaṇāt || (RA_6.38) 
 kākāṇḍīphalacūrṇena | drāvakaiḥ pañcabhistathā | 
 abhrakasya yutaṃ cūrṇaṃ | dhmātaṃ mūṣāgataṃ dravat ||
                    (RA_6.39) 
 bhrāmakaṃ cumbakaṃ caiva | karṣakaṃ drāvakaṃ tathā | 
 evaṃ caturvidhaṃ kāntaṃ | romakāntañca pañcamam || (RA_6.40) 
 ekadvitricatuḥpañca | sarbbatomukhameva tat | 
 pītaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tathā raktaṃ | trivarṇaṃ syāt pṛthak pṛthak ||
                    (RA_6.41) 
 krameṇa devatāstatra | brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ || (RA_6.42) 
 sparśavedhi bhavet pītaṃ | kṛṣṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rasāyane | 
 raktavarṇaṃ mahābhāge | rasabandhe praśasyate || (RA_6.43) 
 bhrāmakaṃ tu kaniṣṭhaṃ syāt | cumbakaṃ madhyamaṃ priye | 
 uttamaṃ karṣakaṃ devi | drāvakaṃ cottamottamam || (RA_6.44) 
 bhrāmayellohajātaṃ tu | tatkāntaṃ bhrāmakaṃ priye | 
 cumbayec cumbakaṃ kāntaṃ | karṣayet karṣakaṃ priye ||
                    (RA_6.45) 
 yatsākṣāddrāvayellohaṃ | takrāntaṃ drāvakaṃ bhavet | 
 tadromakāntaṃ sphuṭitāt | yathā romodgamo bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.46) 
 kaniṣṭhaṃ syādekamukhaṃ | madhyaṃ dvitrimukhaṃ bhavet | 
 catuḥpañcamukhaṃ śreṣṭham | uttamaṃ sarvatomukham ||
                    (RA_6.47) 
 bhrāmakaṃ cumbakañcaiva | vyādhināśe praśasyate | 
 rase rasāyane caiva | karṣakaṃ drāvakaṃ hitam || (RA_6.48) 
 madonmattagajaḥ sūtaḥ | kāntamaṅkuśamucyate | 
 kṣetraṃ khātvā grahītavyaṃ | tatprayatnena bhūyasā ||
                    (RA_6.49) 
 mārutātapavikṣiptaṃ | varjayet surasundari | 
 bahiḥsthitaṃ tvayaskāntaṃ | chāgaraktena bhāvayet ||
                    (RA_6.50) 
 chāgaraktapraliptena | vāsasā pariveṣṭayet | 
 chāgacarmaparīveṣṭya | vinyaset pūrvvavat kṣitau ||
                    (RA_6.51) 
 uddhṛtaṃ saptabhirmāsaiḥ | toyakumbhe vinikṣipet ||
                    (RA_6.52) 
 raktapuṣpaiḥ sadā pūjyaṃ | raktamālyānulepanaiḥ | 
 pūjitaṃ madyamāṃsaiś ca | yojyaṃ rasarasāyane || (RA_6.53) 
 saṃskṛtaṃ chāgaraktena | bhrāmakaṃ cumbakaṃ bhavet | 
 anena kramayogena | drāvakaṃ bhavati priye || (RA_6.54) 
 sūtalohasya vakṣyāmi | saṃskāramatisaukhyadam | 
 jīvadehe praveśe ca | dehasaukhyabalapradam || (RA_6.55) 
 kāntalohaṃ vinā sūto | dehe na krāmati kvacit | 
 vedhayed vyāpayec chīghraṃ | tailabindurivāmbhasi ||
                    (RA_6.56) 
 na sūtena vinā kānto | na kāntaḥ sūtavarjitaḥ | 
 kāntasūtasamāyuktaḥ | prayogo dehadhārakaḥ || (RA_6.57) 
 yavakṣārantu saṃgṛhya | snigdhabhāṇḍe nidhāpayet | 
 maricābhrakacūrṇena | piṇḍībandhantu kārayet | 
 kāntalohaṃ draveddhmātaṃ | nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || (RA_6.58) 
 triṃśaccumbakakāntaṃ ca | piṣṭvā tu triphalāmbhasā | 
 tenaiva kṣālanaṃ kāryyaṃ | pañcaniṣkaṃ tu ṭaṅkaṇam ||
                    (RA_6.59) 
 jīrṇavastre vinikṣipya | madhusarpiryutaṃ puṭet | 
 saṃsthāpya māsaparyyantaṃ | tatra śuddhirbhavetpriye ||
                    (RA_6.60) 
 sināḍikāyā mūlaṃ tu | daśaniṣkamitaṃ yutam | 
 phalatrayakaṣāyana | khalle tu parimardayet || (RA_6.61) 
 trimūṣāsu samaṃ sthāpyam | aṣṭāṅgulamitāsu ca | 
 mūṣakālepanaṃ kāryyaṃ | tanmūlaṃ niṣkamātrakam || (RA_6.62) 
 śivapañcamukhīkāryyā | mūṣāṃ prati samaṃ tataḥ | 
 yantrahaste susaṃbadhya | khoṭakaṃ ca śilātale || (RA_6.63) 
 tailena miśritaṃ kṛtvā | kāntanāgaṃ labhettataḥ | 
 abhrakakramayogena | drutipātañca sādhayet || (RA_6.64) 
 surāsurair mathyamāne | kṣīrode mandarādriṇā | 
 pītaṃ tadamṛtaṃ devair | amaratvam upāgatam || (RA_6.65) 
 pibatāṃ bindavo devi | patitā bhūmimaṇḍale | 
 śuṣkāste vajratāṃ yātā | nānāvarṇā mahābalāḥ || (RA_6.66) 
 bindavaḥ ke 'pi sañjātāḥ | sasyakā vimalāstathā | 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣattriyā vaiśvāḥ | śudrāścaivamanekadhā ||
                    (RA_6.67) 
 śvetā raktāstathā pītā | kṛṣṇāścaiva caturvidhāḥ | 
 puruṣāś ca striyaścaiva | napuṃsakam anukramāt || (RA_6.68) 
 vṛttāḥ phalakasaṃpūrṇās | tejasvanto mahattarāḥ | 
 puruṣāste niboddhavyā | rekhābinduvivarjitāḥ || (RA_6.69) 
 rekhābindusamāyuktāḥ | khaṇḍāścaiva tu yoṣitaḥ | 
 trikoṇāḥ pattalā dīrghāḥ | vijñeyāste napuṃsakāḥ ||
                    (RA_6.70) 
 sattvavanto balopetā | lohe krāmaṇaśīlinaḥ | 
 rasabandhakarāḥ śīghraṃ | puṃvajrāḥ suravandite || (RA_6.71) 
 śarīrakāntijananāḥ | strīvajrāḥ svalpaśaktayaḥ | 
 napuṃsakāḥ sattvahīnāḥ | kaṣṭaṃ lohe kramanti ca ||
                    (RA_6.72) 
 kṣatriyāḥ sarvakāryyeṣu | varjyāś ca rasakarmaṇi | 
 uttamā madhyamāścaiva | kaniṣṭhāḥ parikīrtitāḥ || (RA_6.73) 
 sthūlātisthūlamadhyāś ca | sūkṣmāḥ sūkṣmatarāḥ priye | 
 āsphoṭadāhabhedaiś ca | nirvyaṅgā nirupadravāḥ | 
 vīryyavantaś ca te jyeṣṭhā | nirmalā balavattarāḥ ||
                    (RA_6.74) 
 rasāyane bhaved vipro hy | aṇimādiguṇapradaḥ | 
 kṣatriyo mṛtyunāśārtho | valīpalitarogahā || (RA_6.75) 
 dravyakāro tathā vaiśyaḥ | śarīraṃ dṛḍhatāṃ nayet | 
 vyādhipraśamanaṃ śūdro | vayaḥstambhaṃ karoti ca ||
                    (RA_6.76) 
 klībe klīvāḥ striyaḥ strīṇāṃ | sarbbeṣāṃ puruṣā hitāḥ ||
                    (RA_6.77) 
 yathā jātistathotsāhaṃ | yathā sattvaṃ tathā guṇān | 
 yathā rucistathā śīlaṃ | yathā śīlaṃ tathā varam | 
 yathā varastathā varṇaṃ | kurvanti kuliśāḥ priye ||
                    (RA_6.78) 
 śyāmā śamī ghanaravo | vaṣābhūnmattakodravāḥ | 
 ākhukarṇī munitaruḥ | kulatthaṃ cāmlavetasam || (RA_6.79) 
 meṣaśṛṅgī raso 'pyeṣāṃ | kandasya sūraṇasya tu | 
 śodhayet tridinaṃ vajraṃ | śuddhimeti sureśvari || (RA_6.80) 
 meṣaśṛṅgaṃ bhujaṅgāsthi | kūrmapṛṣṭhaṃ śilājatu | 
 snukkīlālarasaṃ stanyaṃ | kāntapāṣāṇameva ca || (RA_6.81) 
 vajrakaṃ cāpi vaikrāntaṃ | tanmadhye prakṣipet priye | 
 tīvrānale puṭaṃ dattvā | puṭāntaṃ yāvad āgatam || (RA_6.82) 
 kulatthaṃ kodravaṃ cāpi | hayamūtreṇa peṣayet | 
 taptaṃ nipecayet pīṭhe | yāvattadbhasmatāṃ gatam ||
                    (RA_6.83) 
 eṣa kāpāliko yogo | vajramāraṇa uttamaḥ || (RA_6.84) 
 mākṣikaṃ meṣaśṛṅgaṃ ca | śilāgandhakaṭaṅkaṇam | 
 vaikrāntaṃ tālakaṃ cāpi | vajrīkṣīrapariplutam || (RA_6.85) 
 lepaṃ mūṣodare dattvā | samāvarttaṃ tu kārayet | 
 mriyante hīrakāstatra | dvandve samyaṅmilanti ca ||
                    (RA_6.86) 
 gandhakaṃ ca śilādhātuṃ | bhrāmakasya mukhaṃ tathā | 
 śaśakasya ca dantāṃś ca | vetasāmlena peṣayat || (RA_6.87) 
 anena siddhakalkena | mūṣālepaṃ tu kārayet | 
 andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ | vajraṃ tu mriyate kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_6.88) 
 tenaiva militaṃ vajraṃ | tārahemni na saṃśayaḥ || (RA_6.89) 
 tālakaṃ gandhakaṃ kāntaṃ | tāpyaṃ karpūraṭaṅkaṇam | 
 ciñcāsthi meṣaśṛṅgaṃ ca | strīrajaḥparipeṣitam | 
 mūṣālepagataṃ dhmātaṃ | vajraṃ tu mriyate kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_6.90) 
 śarapuṅkhasya pañcāṅgaṃ | peṣyaṃ strīrajasā tataḥ | 
 peṭārībījam athavā | saṃpeṣyaṃ taṇḍulāmbhasā || (RA_6.91) 
 peṣyaṃ trikarṣakārpāsa- | mūlaṃ vā taṇḍulāmbhasā | 
 āraktarākāmūlaṃ vā | strīstanyena tu peṣitam || (RA_6.92) 
 peṣayed vajrakandaṃ vā | vajrīkṣīreṇa suvrate | 
 tatkalkapuṭitaṃ dhmātaṃ | vajraṃ caiva mṛtaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.93) 
 mahānadīśvetaśuktyāṃ | dinam ekan tu bhāvitam | 
 kṣīreṇottaravāruṇyāḥ | kalkenānena suvrate || (RA_6.94) 
 tālena meṣaśṛṅgyā ca | vajravallyā ca veṣṭitam | 
 andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ | vajraṃ tu mriyate kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_6.95) 
 kāntasya piṣṭikāmadhye | vajraṃ devi vinikṣipet | 
 peṣayed gandhatailena | mriyate vajram īśvari || (RA_6.96) 
 kulatthāmbhasi kāsīsa- | saurāṣṭrītālakānvite | 
 apāmārgakṣārayute | vajraṃ siktaṃ mṛtaṃ bhavet || (RA_6.97) 
 amṛtākandatimira- | bījatvakkṣīraveṣṭitam | 
 meṣaśṛṅgagataṃ vajraṃ | mṛlliptaṃ mriyate puṭaiḥ ||
                    (RA_6.98) 
 peṭārī haṃsapādī ca | vajravallī ca sūraṇam | 
 aśvatthasyāṅkurā devi | sarve strīstanyapeṣitāḥ || (RA_6.99) 
 anena siddhakalkena | veṣṭitaṃ bṛhatīphale | 
 kṣiptaṃ bahirmṛdā liptaṃ | mriyate saptabhiḥ puṭaiḥ ||
                    (RA_6.100) 
 śvetendurekhāpuṣpāmbu- | gandhakatrayamākṣikaiḥ | 
 veṣṭitaṃ kuliśaṃ devi | puṭapākāt mṛtaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.101) 
 aśvatthabadarībhiṇḍī- | mākṣīkaṃ karkaṭāsthi ca | 
 snuhīkṣīreṇa saṃpeṣya | puṭādvipro mṛto bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.102) 
 karavīrārkadugdhena | meṣaśṛṅgaṃ sahiṅgulam | 
 udumbarasamāyuktaṃ | puṭāt kṣatriyamāraṇam || (RA_6.103) 
 bālā cātibalā caiva | gandhakaṃ karkaṭāsthi ca | 
 kṣīreṇottaravāruṇyāḥ | puṭanādvaiśyamāraṇam || (RA_6.104) 
 kaṇḍūlasūraṇenaiva | śilayā laśunena ca | 
 nyagrodhaśaṅkhadugdhena | śūdro 'pi mriyate kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_6.105) 
 sthūlā bahusthūlapuṭaiḥ | naśyanti phalakādayaḥ | 
 susvinnā iva jāyante | mṛdutvamupajāyate || (RA_6.106) 
 piṣṭvāmalakapañcāṅgaṃ | gaurābhām indravāruṇīm | 
 anena veṣṭitaṃ vajraṃ | mriyate saptabhiḥ puṭaiḥ ||
                    (RA_6.107) 
 mātṛvāhakajīvasya | madhye vajraṃ vinikṣipet | 
 dolāsvede tryahaṃ devi | guṇapattrasamaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_6.108) 
 eraṇḍavṛkṣamadhye tu | vajraṃ devi vinikṣipet | 
 ekamāse gate devi | guṇapattrasamaṃ bhavet || (RA_6.109) 
 kāntasya piṣṭikāmadhye | vajraṃ devi vinikṣipet | 
 kārpāsanimbapattraṃ ca | badarīpattrasaṃyutam || (RA_6.110) 
 ekatra peṣayet tat tu | kāntagolakaveṣṭitam | 
 bāhye tāmbūlapattreṇa | sthāpayej jānumadhyataḥ ||
                    (RA_6.111) 
 yāmadvayena tadvajraṃ | jāyate mṛdu niścitam | 
 tatkṣaṇānmriyate vajraṃ | tāre hemni na saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_6.112) 
 jambīraphalamadhyasthaṃ | vastrapoṭalikāgatam | 
 kvāthayet kodravakvāthe | krameṇānena tu tryaham | 
 tad vajraṃ jāyate khoṭaṃ | hemnā milati tatkṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_6.113) 
 nāgavallyā praliptaṃ tu | tat pattreṇaiva veṣṭitam | 
 jānumadhye sthitaṃ yāmaṃ | mṛdu saṃjāyate dhruvam ||
                    (RA_6.114) 
 mūle vajralatāyāstu | mṛdu vajraṃ vinikṣipet | 
 puṭaṃ dadyāt prayatnena | bhasmībhavati tatkṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_6.115) 
 sukhādbandhakaraṃ hy āśu | sattvaṃ muñcati tatkṣaṇāt | 
 sarvamṛtyupraśamanāḥ | sarvasiddhikarāś ca te || (RA_6.116) 
 asthiśṛṅkhalamadhyasthaṃ | kṛtvā vajraṃ virandhritam | 
 jalabhāṇḍe tu tat svinnaṃ | saptāhaṃ dravatāṃ vrajet ||
                    (RA_6.117) 
 kṣāratrayaṃ rāmaṭhaṃ ca | caṇakāmlāmlavetasam | 
 kṣiptvā jvālāmukhīkṣīraṃ | sthalakumbhīrasena ca ||
                    (RA_6.118) 
 etaistu marditaṃ vajraṃ | snuhyarkapayasā tathā | 
 dolāyāṃ svedayed devi | jāyate rasavad yathā || (RA_6.119) 
 athavāpyabhrakaṃ svinnaṃ | mauktikaṃ ca pravālakam | 
 mākṣikaṃ nīlapuṣpaṃ ca | pītaṃ marakataṃ mahat | 
 vaiḍūryasphaṭikādīni | dravanti salilaṃ yathā || (RA_6.120) 
 lohajātaṃ tathā dhmātam | agnivarṇaṃ tu dṛśyate | 
 vāpitaṃ sakṛd ekena | mṛtaṃ jalasamaṃ bhavet || (RA_6.121) 
 muktāphalaṃ tu saptāhaṃ | vetasāmlena bhāvitam | 
 jambīrodaramadhyasthaṃ | dhānyarāśau nidhāpayet | 
 puṭapākena taccūrṇaṃ | jāyate salilaṃ yathā || (RA_6.122) 
 śṛṇu devi mahābhāge | vaikrāntākhyaṃ mahārasam ||
                    (RA_6.123) 
 daityendro mahiṣaḥ siddho | haradehasamudbhavaḥ | 
 durgā bhagavatī devī | taṃ śūlena vyamardayat || (RA_6.124) 
 tasya raktaṃ tu patitaṃ | yatra yatra sthitaṃ bhuvi | 
 tatra tatra tu vaikrānto | vajrākāro mahārasaḥ ||
                    (RA_6.125) 
 vindhyasya dakṣiṇe cāsti | uttare nāsti sarvathā | 
 vikṛntayati lohāni | tena vaikrāntakaḥ smṛtaḥ || (RA_6.126) 
 śvetaḥ pītastathā rakto | nīlaḥ pārāvataprabhaḥ | 
 mayūravālasadṛśaś | cānyo marakataprabhaḥ || (RA_6.127) 
 dehasiddhikaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ | pīte pītaḥ site sitaḥ | 
 sarvārthasiddhido raktaḥ | tathā marakataprabhaḥ | 
 śeṣe dve niṣphale varjye | vaikrāntamiti saptadhā ||
                    (RA_6.128) 
 yatra kṣetre sthitaṃ devi | vaikrāntaṃ tatra bhairavam | 
 vināyakaṃ ca sampūjya | gṛhṇīyāt sādhakottamaḥ ||
                    (RA_6.129) 
 vaikrāntaṃ cūrṇitaṃ sūkṣmaṃ | surāsuranamaskṛtam | 
 vyāghrīkandasya madhyasthaṃ | dhamayitvā puṭe sthitam ||
                    (RA_6.130) 
 aśvamūtreṇa mṛdvagnau | svedayet saptavāsarāt | 
 chāyāśuṣkaṃ tataḥ kuryād | idaṃ vaikrāntamuttamam ||
                    (RA_6.131) 
 athavā lavaṇakṣāra- | mūtrāmlakṛṣṇatailakaiḥ | 
 kulatthakodravakvāthe | svedayet sapta vāsarān ||
                    (RA_6.132) 
 vandhyācūrṇaṃ tu vaikrāntaṃ | samāṃśena tu cūrṇayet | 
 ajāmūtreṇa saṃbhāvya | chāyāśuṣkaṃ tu kārayet | 
 andhanāle dhamitvā tu | mūṣāsattvaṃ tu jāyate || (RA_6.133) 
 mokṣamoraṭapālāśa- | kṣāragomūtrabhāvitam | 
 vajrakandaśiphākalka- | lākṣāṭaṅkaṇasaṃyutam || (RA_6.134) 
 vaikrāntasambhavaṃ cūrṇaṃ | meṣaśṛṅgīdravānvitam | 
 piṇḍitaṃ mūkamūṣāyāṃ | dhmātaṃ sattvaṃ vimuñcati ||
                    (RA_6.135) 
 vaikrāntaṃ vajrakandaṃ ca | peṣayed vajravāriṇā | 
 māhiṣe navanīte ca | sakṣaudraṃ piṇḍitaṃ tataḥ | 
 śodhayitvā dhamet sattvam | indragopasamaṃ patet ||
                    (RA_6.136) 
 ketakīsvarasaḥ kāṅkṣī | maṇimatthaṃ sakhecaram | 
 svedanājjāyate devi | vaikrāntaṃ rasasaṃnibham ||
                    (RA_6.137) 
 suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ | kāntalohasya vā rajaḥ | 
 anena svedavidhinā | dravanti salilaṃ yathā || (RA_6.138) 
 ityuktamabhrakādīnāṃ | caturṇāṃ lakṣaṇādikam | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_6.139) 
 
 iti śrīpārvatīparameśvarasaṃvāde rasārṇave rasasaṃhitāyām
                    abhrakādilakṣaṇasaṃskāranirṇayo nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ paṭalaḥ 
 
 
 7 [Mahārasoparasalohalakṣaṇasaṃskāraratnadrāvaṇamāraṇanirṇayaḥ] 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 saha lakṣaṇasaṃskārair | ājñāpaya mahārasān | 
 anyac ca tādṛśaṃ deva | rasavidyopakārakam || (RA_7.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 mākṣiko vimalaḥ śailaś | capalo rasakastathā | 
 sasyako daradaścaiva | srotoñjanam athāṣṭakam | 
 aṣṭau mahārasāścaivam | etān prathamataḥ śṛṇu || (RA_7.2) 
 kṛṣṇas tu bhārataṃ śrutvā | yoganidrāmupāgataḥ | 
 tasya pādatale viddhaṃ | vyādhena mṛgaśaṅkayā || (RA_7.3) 
 ye tatra patitā bhūmau | kṣatādrudhirabindavaḥ | 
 te nimbaphalasaṃsthānā | jātā vai mākṣikopalāḥ || (RA_7.4) 
 mākṣiko dvividhastatra | pītaśuklavibhāgataḥ | 
 vimalastrividho devi | śuklaḥ pītaś ca lohitaḥ || (RA_7.5) 
 tailāranālatakreṣu | gomūtre kadalīrase | 
 kulatthakodravakvāthaiḥ | mākṣikaṃ vimalaṃ tathā | 
 muhuḥ śūraṇakandasthaṃ | svedayed varavarṇini || (RA_7.6) 
 kṣārāmlalavaṇair aṇḍa- | tailasarpiḥsamanvitam | 
 puṭatrayaṃ pradātavyaṃ | taddvayaṃ śodhitaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_7.7) 
 mākṣikaṃ cūrṇitaṃ stanya- | snuhyarkakṣīrabhāvitam | 
 sattvaṃ muñcati sudhmātaṃ | ṭaṅkakaṅkuṣṭhamoditam || (RA_7.8) 
 kadalīkandatulasī- | nāraṅgāmlapariplutam | 
 saptasaptapuṭopetaṃ | pañcadrāvakasaṃyutam | 
 strīstanyamoditaṃ dhmātaṃ | sattvaṃ muñcati mākṣikam ||
                    (RA_7.9) 
 kṣaudragandharvatailābhyāṃ | gomūtreṇa ghṛtena ca | 
 kadalīkandasāreṇa | bhāvitaṃ mākṣikaṃ muhuḥ | 
 mūṣāyāṃ muñcati dhmātaṃ | sattvaṃ śulvanibhaṃ mṛdu ||
                    (RA_7.10) 
 devadālīrasaṃ kṣiptvā | pādāṃśaṭaṅkaṇair yutam | 
 prakaṭāṃ mūṣikāṃ kṛtvā | dhamet sattvam apekṣitam ||
                    (RA_7.11) 
 kimatra citraṃ kadalīrasena | supācitaṃ sūraṇakandasampuṭe | 
 vātāritailena puṭena tāpyaṃ | puṭena dagdhaṃ varaśuddhim eti ||
                    (RA_7.12) 
 gomūtraiś ca snuhikṣīraiḥ | bhāvyameraṇḍatailakaiḥ | 
 mākṣikaṃ dinam ekaṃ tu | marditaṃ vaṭakīkṛtam | 
 abhravaddhamayet sattvaṃ | sasyakasyāpyayaṃ vidhiḥ ||
                    (RA_7.13) 
 tāpyam āvartakaṃ dhātu- | mākṣikaṃ madhudhātukam | 
 mākṣikaṃ tiktamadhuraṃ | mehārśaḥkṣayakuṣṭhanut | 
 kaphapittaharaṃ balyaṃ | yogavāhi rasāyanam || (RA_7.14) 
 jvarasaṃnipātadāridryāṇyapi yannāmakathanamātreṇa /* 
 naśyanti yojanaśate kas tasmāllohavedhakaraḥ || Ras_7.15 /* 
 vimalaṃ śigrutoyena | kāṅkṣīkāsīsaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ | 
 vajrakandasamāyuktaṃ | bhāvitaṃ kadalīrasaiḥ || (RA_7.16) 
 mokṣakakṣārasaṃyuktaṃ | dhāmitaṃ mūkamūṣayā | 
 sattvaṃ candrārkasaṃkāśaṃ | prayacchati na saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.17) 
 patito 'patitaśceti | dvividhaḥ śailā īśvari | 
 granthāntare 'pi kīrtyo 'sau | kīrtito bahubhiḥ suraiḥ ||
                    (RA_7.18) 
 nidāghe gharmasaṃtaptā | dhātusāraṃ dharādharāḥ | 
 niryāsaṃ ca vimuñcanti | tacchilājatu kīrtitam || (RA_7.19) 
 śilāvad dhātukaṃ dhmātaṃ | śailajaṃ girisānujam | 
 jatvadrijaṃ giriḥ śailaḥ | proktastvayānukīrtitaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.20) 
 kṣārāmlagojalair dhmātaṃ | śudhyate ca śilājatu | 
 athavā goghṛtenāpi | triphaladvyārdrakadravaiḥ | 
 lohapātre vinikṣipya | śodhayet tat tu yatnataḥ || (RA_7.21) 
 śailaṃ vicūrṇayitvā tu | dhānyāmlopaviṣair viṣaiḥ | 
 piṇḍaṃ baddhvā tu vidhivat | pātayec capalaṃ yathā ||
                    (RA_7.22) 
 gauraḥ śveto 'ruṇaḥ kṛṣṇaś | capalas tu praśasyate | 
 haimābhaścaiva tārābho | viśeṣādrasabandhakaḥ || (RA_7.23) 
 śeṣau madhyau ca lākṣāvat | śīghradrāvau tu niṣphalau | 
 vaṅgavaddravate vahnau | capalastena kīrtitaḥ || (RA_7.24) 
 vastreṇa baddhvā capalaṃ | laṅghayed yadi sāgaram | 
 vastraṃ ca veṣṭayet sadyaḥ | tenāsau capalaḥ smṛtaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.25) 
 sārayet puṭapākena | capalaṃ girimastake | 
 dehabandhaṃ karotyeva | viśeṣādrasabandhanam || (RA_7.26) 
 capalaścapalāvedhaṃ | karoti ghanavaccalaḥ | 
 capalo lekhanaḥ snigdho | dehalohakaro mataḥ || (RA_7.27) 
 mṛttikāguḍapāṣāṇa- | bhedato rasakastridhā || (RA_7.28) 
 pītas tu mṛttikākāro | mṛttikārasako varaḥ | 
 guḍābho madhyamo jñeyaḥ | pāṣāṇābhaḥ kaniṣṭhakaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.29) 
 kaṭukālābuniryāse- | nāloḍya rasakaṃ pacet | 
 śuddho doṣavinirmuktaḥ | pītavarṇas tu jāyate || (RA_7.30) 
 kimatra citraṃ rasakaṃ rasena | rajasvalāyāḥ kusumena bhāvitam | 
 krameṇa kṛtvā uragena rañjitaṃ | karoti śulbaṃ tripuṭena
                    kāñcanam || (RA_7.31) 
 kṣīyate nāpi vahnisthaḥ | sattvarūpo mahābalaḥ || (RA_7.32) 
 rasakaṃ cūrṇayitvā tu | baddhvā vastre vicakṣaṇaḥ | 
 mūtre nidhāpayet strīṇāṃ | saptarātraṃ sureśvari ||
                    (RA_7.33) 
 puṣpāṇāṃ raktapītānāṃ | rasaiḥ pattraiś ca bhāvayet ||
                    (RA_7.34) 
 kṣāraiḥ snehaistathā cāmlaiḥ | bhāvitaṃ rasakaṃ muhuḥ | 
 ūrṇālākṣāniśāpathyā- | bhūlatādhūmasaṃyutam || (RA_7.35) 
 mūkamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ | ṭaṅkaṇena samanvitam | 
 sattvaṃ kuṭilasaṃkāśaṃ | muñcatyeva na saṃśayaḥ || (RA_7.36) 
 gobhaddo rasakastutthaṃ | kṣitikiṭṭo rasodbhavaḥ | 
 kharparo netrarogāriḥ | rītikṛttāmrarañjakaḥ || (RA_7.37) 
 rasako rañjako rūkṣo | vātakṛt śleṣmanāśanaḥ | 
 tridoṣaghnaṃ tu tatsattvaṃ | netradoṣavināśanam || (RA_7.38) 
 kālakūṭaviṣaṃ pītvā | garuḍaḥ soḍhumakṣamaḥ | 
 sudhām api tathāvāmat | bhukta āśīviṣāmṛte | 
 svayaṃ vinirgate cañcvoḥ | sasyako 'bhūt sa kālikaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.39) 
 ekadhā sasyakastasya | strīmūtre bhāvayed rajaḥ | 
 śaśaśoṇitamadhye vā | dinamekaṃ nidhāpayet || (RA_7.40) 
 tasya cūrṇaṃ maheśāni | pādasaubhāgyasaṃyutam | 
 karañjatailamadhyasthaṃ | dinamekaṃ nidhāpayet || (RA_7.41) 
 madhyasthamandhamūṣāyāḥ | dhamayet kokilātrayam | 
 indragopakasaṃkāśaṃ | sattvaṃ patati śobhanam || (RA_7.42) 
 ekadhā sasyakastasmāt | dhmāto nipatito bhavet | 
 kālikārahito raktaḥ | śikhikaṇṭhasamākṛtiḥ || (RA_7.43) 
 sasyo mayūratutthaṃ syāt | vahnikṛt kālanāśanaḥ | 
 rasāyane tu yogyaḥ syād | vayaḥstambhakaro bhavet ||
                    (RA_7.44) 
 sasyakaḥ śuddhimāpnoti | raktavargeṇa bhāvitaḥ || (RA_7.45) 
 daradastrividhaḥ proktaś | carmāraḥ śukatuṇḍakaḥ | 
 haṃsapādastṛtīyaḥ syād | guṇavānuttarottaraḥ || (RA_7.46) 
 cūrṇapāradabhedena | dvividho daradaḥ punaḥ || (RA_7.47) 
 gomāṃse māhiṣe mūtre | dadhyamlatilatailayoḥ | 
 ekaikaṃ tridinaṃ paktvā | śikhipittena bhāvayet || (RA_7.48) 
 daradaṃ pātanāyantre | pātayet salilāśaye | 
 sattvaṃ tu sūtasaṃkāśaṃ | jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ || (RA_7.49) 
 laghukandaraso mlec cho | hiṅgulaṃ cūrṇapāradam | 
 maṇirāgajamasyaiva | nāma carmāragandhikam || (RA_7.50) 
 tiktoṣṇaṃ hiṅgulaṃ divyaṃ | rasagandhakasambhavam | 
 lohakuṣṭhaharaṃ divya- | balamedhāgnidīpanam || (RA_7.51) 
 kimatra citraṃ daradaḥ subhāvitaḥ | kṣīreṇa meṣyā bahuśo 'mlavargaiḥ | 
 sitaṃ suvarṇaṃ bahugharmatāpitaṃ | karoti
                    sākṣādvarakuṅkumaprabham || (RA_7.52) 
 valmīkaśikharākāraṃ | bhaṅge nīlotpaladyuti | 
 ghṛṣṭaṃ tu gairikacchāyaṃ | srotojaṃ suravandite ||
                    (RA_7.53) 
 gośakṛdrasamūtreṣu | ghṛtakṣaudravasāsu ca | 
 bhāvitaṃ bahuśastac ca | kṣipraṃ badhnāti sūtakam ||
                    (RA_7.54) 
 evaṃ mahārasāḥ proktāḥ | śṛṇuṣvoparasān priye || (RA_7.55) 
 gandhakastālakaḥ śilā | saurāṣṭrī khagagairikam | 
 rājāvartaś ca kaṅkuṣṭham | aṣṭā uparasāḥ smṛtāḥ || (RA_7.56) 
 śvetadvīpe purā devi | sarvaratnavibhūṣite | 
 sarvakāmamaye ramye | tīre kṣīrapayonidheḥ || (RA_7.57) 
 vidyādharībhirmukhyābhir | aṅganābhiś ca yoṣite | 
 siddhāṅganābhistviṣṭābhis | tathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ||
                    (RA_7.58) 
 devāṅganābhiranyābhiḥ | krīḍitābhiḥ purā priye | 
 gītanṛtyair vicitraiś ca | vādyair nānāvidhaistathā ||
                    (RA_7.59) 
 evaṃ saṃkrīḍamānāyās | tavābhūt prasṛtaṃ rajaḥ | 
 tadrajo 'tīva suśroṇi | sugandhi sumanoharam || (RA_7.60) 
 rajasaścātibāhulyāt | vāsaste raktatāṃ yayau | 
 tatra tyaktvā tu tadvāsaḥ | susnātā kṣīrasāgare || (RA_7.61) 
 vṛtā devāṅganābhistvaṃ | suraiścāpi puraṃ gatā | 
 ūrmibhiste rajovastraṃ | nītaṃ madhye payonidheḥ ||
                    (RA_7.62) 
 evaṃ te śoṇitaṃ bhadre | praviṣṭaṃ kṣīrasāgare | 
 kṣīrābdhimathane caitad | amṛtena sahotthitam | 
 nijagandhena tān sarvān | harṣayaddevadānavān || (RA_7.63) 
 tato devagaṇair uktaṃ | gandhakākhyo bhavatvayam ||
                    (RA_7.64) 
 rasasya bandhanārthāya | jāraṇāya bhavatvayam | 
 ye guṇāḥ pārade proktās | te caivātra bhavantviti ||
                    (RA_7.65) 
 iti devagaṇaiḥ prītaiḥ | purā proktaṃ sureśvari | 
 tenāyaṃ gandhako nāma | vikhyātaḥ kṣitimaṇḍale || (RA_7.66) 
 sa cāpi trividho devi | śukacañcunibho varaḥ | 
 madhyamaḥ pītavarṇaḥ syāc | chuklavarṇo 'dhamaḥ priye ||
                    (RA_7.67) 
 karañjair aṇḍatailena | drāvayitvājadugdhake | 
 siñcedunmattaniryāse | trīnvārāṃstaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||
                    (RA_7.68) 
 jvālinībījacūrṇena | matsyapittaiś ca bhāvayet | 
 bhṛṅgāmbhasā vā saptāhaṃ | bhāvitaḥ kṣālito 'mbhasā ||
                    (RA_7.69) 
 tāpito badarāṅgāraiḥ | ghṛtākte lohabhājane | 
 āvartitaś ca mṛdvagnau | ghṛtāktakarpaṭopari || (RA_7.70) 
 kṣipraṃ bhṛṅgasya niryāse | kṣālito gandhako hitaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.71) 
 gandhako hi svabhāvena | rasarūpaḥ svarūpataḥ | 
 gandhakaṃ śodhayet kṣīre | śṛṅgaverarase tathā || (RA_7.72) 
 rase ca bhṛṅgarājasya | nimbukasya rase tathā | 
 śodhitaḥ saptavārāṇi | gandhako jāyate 'malaḥ || (RA_7.73) 
 tālakaḥ paṭalaḥ piṇḍo | dvidhā tatrādya uttamaḥ | 
 kuṣmāṇḍe tu śataṃ vārān | tālakaṃ svedayed budhaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.74) 
 snukkṣīrakaṭukālābu- | rasayoḥ saptadhā pṛthak | 
 tilasarṣapaśigrūṇi | lākṣā ca lavaṇaṃ guḍaḥ | 
 ṭaṅkaṇaṃ ca yutair hyetaiḥ | tālakaṃ bhūdhare dravet ||
                    (RA_7.75) 
 vyādhighātaphalakṣāraṃ | madhukuṣmāṇḍakaṃ tathā | 
 dravaiḥ punarnavodbhūtaiḥ | saptāhaṃ mardayed budhaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.76) 
 dattvā pādāṃśakaṃ sarvaṃ | tataḥ pātanayantrake | 
 dadyāt puṭaṃ gajākāraṃ | patet sattvaṃ sutālakāt ||
                    (RA_7.77) 
 raktā śilā tu gomāṃse | luṅgāmlena vipācitā | 
 tāṃ raktapītapuṣpāṇāṃ | rasaiḥ pittaiś ca bhāvayet ||
                    (RA_7.78) 
 sitā kṛṣṇā ca saurāṣṭrī | cūrṇakhaṇḍātmikā ca sā ||
                    (RA_7.79) 
 gopittena śataṃ vārān | saurāṣṭrīṃ bhāvayet tataḥ | 
 dhamitvā pātayet sattvaṃ | krāmaṇaṃ cātiguhyakam ||
                    (RA_7.80) 
 kāsīsaṃ trividhaṃ śuklaṃ | kṛṣṇaṃ pītamiti priye ||
                    (RA_7.81) 
 kāsīsaṃ cūrṇayitvā tu | kāsamardarasena ca | 
 rājakośātakītoyaiḥ | pittaiś ca paribhāvayet || (RA_7.82) 
 gairikaṃ trividhaṃ rakta- | hemakevalabhedataḥ | 
 raktavargarasakvātha- | pittaistadbhāvayet pṛthak ||
                    (RA_7.83) 
 anena kramayogena | gairikaṃ vimalaṃ dhamet | 
 kramāt sitaṃ ca raktaṃ ca | sattvaṃ patati śobhanam ||
                    (RA_7.84) 
 rājāvarto dvidhā devi | gulikācūrṇabhedataḥ || (RA_7.85) 
 taccūrṇaṃ devadeveśi | mahiṣīkṣīrasaṃyutam | 
 vipacedāyase pātre | goghṛtena vimiśritam || (RA_7.86) 
 taccūrṇitaṃ sureśāni | kunaṭīghṛtamiśritam | 
 saubhāgyapañcagavyena | piṇḍībaddhaṃ tu kārayet | 
 dhamitaṃ khādirāṅgāraiḥ | sattvaṃ muñcati śobhanam ||
                    (RA_7.87) 
 kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ vidrumacchāyaṃ | tac ca sattvamayaṃ priye ||
                    (RA_7.88) 
 sūryāvartodakakaṇā- | vahniśigruśiphārasaiḥ | 
 kadalīkandasāreṇa | vandhyākośātakīrasaiḥ || (RA_7.89) 
 kākamācīdevadālī- | vajrakandarasaistathā | 
 ebhir vyastaiḥ samastair vā | kṣārāmlasnehasaindhavaiḥ | 
 mahārasāścoparasāḥ | śuddhimāyānti bhāvitāḥ || (RA_7.90) 
 lākṣālavaṇasaubhāgya- | dhūmasārakaṭutrayam | 
 śigrumūlamadhūcchiṣṭaṃ | pathyāgugguludhātavaḥ || (RA_7.91) 
 sarjikāsarjaniryāsa- | piṇyākorṇāsamanvitam | 
 pārāvatamalakṣudra- | matsyadrāvakapañcakam || (RA_7.92) 
 tilasarṣapagodhūma- | māṣaniṣpāvacikkasam | 
 chāgakṣīreṇa saṃyuktaṃ | vajrapiṇḍī tu kīrtitā || (RA_7.93) 
 anayā vajrapiṇḍyā tu | pañcamāhiṣayuktayā | 
 mahārasā moditāstu | pañcagavyena bhāvitāḥ || (RA_7.94) 
 koṣṭhe kharāgninā dhmātāḥ | sattvaṃ muñcanti suvrate | 
 evaṃ śilābhyo jīvebhyo | mṛdbhyaḥ sattvaṃ prajāyate ||
                    (RA_7.95) 
 evaṃ coparasāḥ proktāḥ | śṛṇu lohānyataḥ param || (RA_7.96) 
 suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ | tīkṣṇaṃ vaṅgaṃ bhujaṃgamam | 
 lohaṃ tu ṣaḍvidhaṃ tac ca | yathā pūrvaṃ tadakṣayam ||
                    (RA_7.97) 
 tatrāditaḥ sureśāni | sāraṃ lohadvayaṃ smṛtam | 
 sādhāraṇe tīkṣṇaśulve | vaṅganāgau tu pūtikau || (RA_7.98) 
 rasajaṃ kṣetrajaṃ caiva | lohasaṃkarajaṃ tathā | 
 trividhaṃ jāyate hema | caturthaṃ nopalabhyate || (RA_7.99) 
 raktābhaṃ pītavarṇaṃ ca | dvividhaṃ devi kāñcanam | 
 dāhe raktaṃ sitaṃ chede | nikaṣe kuṅkumaprabham ||
                    (RA_7.100) 
 sagauravaṃ mṛdu snigdhaṃ | tāraśulvavivarjitam | 
 hema ṣoḍaśavarṇāḍhyaṃ | śasyate dehalohayoḥ || (RA_7.101) 
 mṛttikā mātuluṅgāmlaiḥ | pañcavāsarabhāvitā | 
 sabhasmalavaṇā hema | śodhayet puṭapākataḥ || (RA_7.102) 
 śuklaṃ ca tārakṛṣṇaṃ ca | dvividhaṃ rajataṃ priye | 
 guru snigdhaṃ mṛdu śvetaṃ | tāramuttamamiṣyate ||
                    (RA_7.103) 
 nāgena kṣārarājena | drāvitaṃ śuddhimicchati | 
 tāraṃ trivāraṃ nikṣiptaṃ | piśācītailamadhyataḥ ||
                    (RA_7.104) 
 tāmraṃ ca dvividhaṃ proktaṃ | raktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sureśvari | 
 ghanaghātasahaṃ snigdhaṃ | raktapattraṃ mṛdūttamam ||
                    (RA_7.105) 
 snuhyarkakṣīralavaṇa- | kṣārāmlaparilepitam | 
 tāmrapattraṃ ca nirguṇḍī- | rasamadhye tu ḍhālayet ||
                    (RA_7.106) 
 rohaṇaṃ vājaraṃ caiva | tṛtīyaṃ ca paḍālakam | 
 iti tīkṣṇaṃ tridhā tac ca | kāntalohamiti smṛtam ||
                    (RA_7.107) 
 nīlaṃ kṛṣṇamiti snigdhaṃ | sūkṣmadhāramayaḥ śubham | 
 guḍūcī haṃsapādī ca | naktamālaḥ phalatrayam || (RA_7.108) 
 gopālakī gorasānāṃ | tumbururlohanighnakaḥ | 
 eṣāṃ rase ḍhālayet tat | giridoṣanivṛttaye || (RA_7.109) 
 trapu ca dvividhaṃ jñeyaṃ | śvetakṛṣṇavibhedataḥ | 
 śvetaṃ laghu mṛdu snigdham | uttamaṃ vaṅgamucyate ||
                    (RA_7.110) 
 nāgastvekavidho devi | śīghradrāvī mṛdurguruḥ || (RA_7.111) 
 mahiṣasyāsthicūrṇena | vāpāttanmūtrasecanāt | 
 vaṅgaṃ śuddhaṃ bhavet tadvat | nāgo nāgāsthimūtrataḥ ||
                    (RA_7.112) 
 gaurīphalāni kṣurako | rajanītumburūṇi ca | 
 kuberākṣasya bījāni | mallikāyāś ca sundari || (RA_7.113) 
 palāśaśuṣkāpāmārga- | kṣārasnukkṣīrayogataḥ | 
 saptadhā parivāpena | śodhayanti bhujaṃgamam || (RA_7.114) 
 snuhīkṣīrasamāyogāt | vaṅgaṃ cāvāpayet tataḥ || (RA_7.115) 
 snuhyarkakṣīrahalinī- | kañcukīkandacitrakaiḥ | 
 guñjākarañjadhuttūra- | hayagandhāṅghritālakaiḥ ||
                    (RA_7.116) 
 naktamāleṅgudīśakra- | vāruṇīmūlasaṃyutaiḥ | 
 piṣṭair māhiṣatakre tu | saptarātroṣitaistataḥ | 
 niṣekaḥ sarvalohānāṃ | malaṃ hanti na saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.117) 
 devadālīphalarajaḥ- | svarasair bhāvitaṃ muhuḥ | 
 drāvayet kanakaṃ vāpāt | bhūyo na kaṭhinaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_7.118) 
 akhilāni ca sattvāni | drāvayet tatprabhāvataḥ ||
                    (RA_7.119) 
 samāṃśaṃ suragopasya | suradālyāś ca yadrajaḥ | 
 āvāpāt kurute devi | kanakaṃ jalasaṃnibham || (RA_7.120) 
 maṇḍūkāsthivasāṭaṅka- | hayalālendragopakaiḥ | 
 prativāpena kanakaṃ | suciraṃ tiṣṭhati drutam || (RA_7.121) 
 triḥsaptakṛtvo gomūtre | jvālinībhasma gālitam | 
 śoṣayet tasya vāpena | tīkṣṇaṃ mūṣāgataṃ dravet ||
                    (RA_7.122) 
 triḥsaptakṛtvo nicula- | bhasmanā bhāvitena tu | 
 ketakyāstu rasaistīkṣṇam | āvāpāddravatāṃ vrajet ||
                    (RA_7.123) 
 pakvadhātrīphalarasaiḥ | śaṅkhe saptāhabhāvitam | 
 punaḥ kañcukitoyena | bhāvitaṃ saptavāsaram || (RA_7.124) 
 śarāvayugalāntaḥsthaṃ | sudṛḍhaṃ paridhāmitam | 
 tattīkṣṇacūrṇaṃ deveśi | rasarūpaṃ prajāyate || (RA_7.125) 
 tālakaṃ gandhapāṣāṇa- | śilāmākṣikagairikam | 
 kāsīsaṃ khaṇḍasaurāṣṭrī- | tutthamabhrakameva ca ||
                    (RA_7.126) 
 śvaśṛgālatarakṣūṇāṃ | kukkuṭasya malaṃ tathā | 
 mayūragṛdhramārjāra- | viṣṭhā ca samabhāgakam || (RA_7.127) 
 bhāvayet triḥ snuhīkṣīrair | devadālīrasena ca | 
 tatkalkam aṣṭamāṃśena | lohapattrāṇi lepayet || (RA_7.128) 
 dhamed drutaṃ bhavelloham | etair eva niṣecayet | 
 aṅkolasya tu mūlāni | kāñjikena prapeṣayet | 
 lohalepaṃ tato dadyāt | agnisthaṃ dhārayet priye ||
                    (RA_7.129) 
 punarlepaṃ tato dadyāt | paricchinnārasena tu | 
 matsyapittena deveśi | vahnisthaṃ dhārayet priye ||
                    (RA_7.130) 
 punarlepaṃ prakurvīta | lāṅgalīkandasambhavam | 
 tribhirlepair drutaṃ lohaṃ | nirmalaṃ svacchavārivat ||
                    (RA_7.131) 
 cūrṇitaṃ devi kūrmāsthi | meṣaśṛṅgaṃ śilājatu | 
 kurute prativāpena | balavajjalavat sthiram || (RA_7.132) 
 arkāpāmārgamusalī- | niculaṃ citrakaṃ tathā | 
 kadalī potakī dālī | kṣārameṣāṃ tu sādhayet || (RA_7.133) 
 gālayen māhiṣe mūtre | ṣaḍvārānsuravandite | 
 āvāpāddrāvayed eta- | dabhrasattvādijaṃ rajaḥ || (RA_7.134) 
 dantīdanto viśeṣeṇa | drāvayet salilaṃ yathā || (RA_7.135) 
 rasenottaravāruṇyāḥ | plutaṃ vaikrāntajaṃ rajaḥ | 
 prativāpena lohāni | drāvayet salilopamam || (RA_7.136) 
 ratnānāṃ drāvaṇaṃ vakṣye | gaganasya drutiṃ tathā ||
                    (RA_7.137) 
 triphalā ca trikaṭukaṃ | trikṣāraṃ paṭupañcakam | 
 balā cātibalā caiva | tṛtīyā ca mahābalā || (RA_7.138) 
 aśvagandhā cavī nārī | bhūlatā mātṛvāhakaḥ | 
 gopendramaṇḍalī caiva | ṣaḍbindurdvimukhī tathā ||
                    (RA_7.139) 
 dhīrā sūraṇakandaś ca | kañcukī ca punarnavā | 
 snuhyarkonmattahalinī | pāṭhā cottaravāruṇī || (RA_7.140) 
 ayaskānto gokṣuraś ca | mṛdudūrvāmlavetasam | 
 śilājatu ca sauvīraṃ | viṣagandhakaṭaṅkaṇam || (RA_7.141) 
 pṛthagdaśapalaṃ sarvaṃ | sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu kārayet | 
 kumbhadvayaṃ kulatthānāṃ | kāṣṭhena tiniśasya ca ||
                    (RA_7.142) 
 kvāthayen mṛdutāpena | yāvat kumbhāvaśeṣitam | 
 tena kvāthena taccūrṇaṃ | bhāvayed ekaviṃśatim ||
                    (RA_7.143) 
 ratnāni tena liptāni | tatkvāthasthaṃ dhamet punaḥ | 
 ahorātreṇa tānyāśu | dravanti salilaṃ yathā || (RA_7.144) 
 abhrakādīni lohāni | dravanti hy avicārataḥ | 
 nirmalāni ca jāyante | harabījopamāni ca || (RA_7.145) 
 milanti ca rasenāśu | vahnisthānyakṣayāṇi ca | 
 tair drutaiḥ sparśamātreṇa | kṣaṇād badhyeta sūtakaḥ ||
                    (RA_7.146) 
 lohānāṃ māraṇaṃ vakṣye | samāhitamanāḥ śṛṇu | 
 snuhīkṣīreṇa sindūraṃ | kanakaṃ rajataṃ punaḥ || (RA_7.147) 
 tenaiva mākṣikaṃ tāmram | ajākṣīreṇa gandhakam | 
 stanyena hiṅgulaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ | vaṅgatālapalāśakam ||
                    (RA_7.148) 
 nāgaṃ śilārkakṣīreṇa | svacchapattrīkṛtaṃ priye | 
 mārayet puṭapākena | nirutthaṃ bhasma jāyate || (RA_7.149) 
 na so 'sti lohamātaṃgo | yaṃ na gandhakakesarī | 
 nihanyādgandhamātreṇa | yadvā mākṣikakesarī || (RA_7.150) 
 rasībhavanti lohāni | mṛtāni suravandite | 
 haranti rogān sakalān | rasayuktāni kiṃ punaḥ | 
 śīlanānnāśayantyeva | valīpalitarugjarāḥ || (RA_7.151) 
 vajramākṣikatīkṣṇābhraṃ | śasyate dehakarmaṇi | 
 nāgaṃ vaṅgaṃ suvīraṃ ca | dravyakarmaṇi yojayet ||
                    (RA_7.152) 
 paribālaṃ tu yallohaṃ | tathā ca malayodbhavam | 
 etallohadvayaṃ devi | viśeṣāddeharakṣaṇam || (RA_7.153) 
 rāgaṃ mahārasādīnāṃ | jñātvā bījāni sādhayet | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum arhasi ||
                    (RA_7.154) 
 
 

                8 [Bījasādhana]

                  śrīdevyuvāca 
 mahārasānāṃ lohānāṃ | ratnānāṃ ca sureśvara | 
 rāgasaṃkhyāṃ tathā bīja- | sādhanaṃ ca vada prabho ||
                    (RA_8.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 mahāraseṣu dviguṇas | tāmrarāgaḥ sureśvari | 
 giridoṣe kṣayaṃ nīte | sūtakaṃ rañjayanti te || (RA_8.2) 
 sasyakaścapalaś caiva | rājāvartaś ca mākṣikaḥ | 
 vimalo gairikaṃ caiṣām | ekaikaṃ dviguṇaṃ bhavet || (RA_8.3) 
 bhrāmakādiṣu kānteṣv apy | ekadvitriguṇo hi saḥ | 
 ekaikamabhrake caiva | śvetapītāruṇaḥ site || (RA_8.4) 
 aṣṭādaśasahasrāṇi | sthitā rāgāś ca gandhake | 
 ayutaṃ darade devi | śilāyāṃ dvisahasrakam || (RA_8.5) 
 rasake saptasāhasraṃ | kaṅkuṣṭhe tu catuṣṭayam | 
 rasagarbhe prakāśante | jāraṇaṃ tu bhavedyadi || (RA_8.6) 
 dvādaśāgraṃ śataṃ pañca | nāge rāgā vyavasthitāḥ | 
 śatahīnaṃ sahasraṃ tu | vaṅge rāgā vyavasthitāḥ || (RA_8.7) 
 rāgāṇāṃ śatapañcāśat | śulvamadhye vyavasthitāḥ | 
 raktapītāś ca śuklāś ca | hemni rāgāś ca ṣoḍaśa || (RA_8.8) 
 rāgāḥ ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi | śakranīle vyavasthitāḥ | 
 mahānīle ca deveśi | te rāgā dviguṇāḥ sthitāḥ || (RA_8.9) 
 māṇikye tu sureśāni | rāgā lakṣatrayodaśa | 
 gajavārisamutpannaṃ | ratnaṃ muktāphalaṃ viduḥ || (RA_8.10) 
 gaje trīṇi sahasrāṇi | ṣaṭsahasrāṇi vārije | 
 navalakṣaṃ ca rāgāṇāṃ | padmarāge vyavasthitāḥ || (RA_8.11) 
 bhedayet sarvalohāni | yac ca kena na bhidyate | 
 tadvajraṃ tasya deveśi | rāgaṃ lakṣadvayaṃ viduḥ ||
                    (RA_8.12) 
 ṣoḍaśaiva sahasrāṇi | puṣparāge vyavasthitāḥ | 
 pādonalakṣarāgāstu | proktā marakate priye || (RA_8.13) 
 rāgasaṃkhyāṃ na jānāti | saṃkrāntasya rasasya tu | 
 adhikaṃ mārayellohaṃ | hīnaṃ caiva prakāśayet || (RA_8.14) 
 mānavendraḥ prakurvīta | yo hi jānāti pārvati | 
 śatakoṭipramāṇena | rāgasaṃkhyāṃ prakalpayet | 
 sparśanaṃ caivamālokya | śatakoṭistu vidhyate || (RA_8.15) 
 ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi | bījānāṃ sādhanaṃ priye | 
 hematāravaśādbījaṃ | dvividhaṃ tāvadīśvari || (RA_8.16) 
 pītāruṇair hemabījaṃ | tārabījaṃ sitair bhavet | 
 kalpitaṃ rañjitaṃ pakvam | iti bhūyastridhā bhavet ||
                    (RA_8.17) 
 kalpitaṃ dvividhaṃ tac ca | śuddhamiśravibhedataḥ ||
                    (RA_8.18) 
 rasoparasalohānāṃ | bījānāṃ kalpanaṃ pṛthak | 
 śuddhaṃ miśraṃ tu saṃyogāt | yathālābhaṃ sureśvari ||
                    (RA_8.19) 
 sattvamāvartitaṃ vyomni | śodhitaṃ kācaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ | 
 ciñcāphalāmlanirguṇḍī- | pattrakalkaniṣecanaiḥ |
