 pakvaṃ niviḍitaṃ devi | rasapiṣṭikṣamaṃ bhavet || (RA_8.20) 
 snehakṣārāmlavargaiś ca | śilāyāś ca puṭatrayāt | 
 mṛtāhe dhūpanāyantre | dhūpagandhānulepanāt | 
 vaṅgasyāpi vidhānena | tālakasya hatasya vā || (RA_8.21) 
 tāpyahiṅgulayorvāpi | hate ca rasakasya vā | 
 rasagarbhe dravet kṛṣṇaṃ | pattraṃ kanakatārayoḥ ||
                    (RA_8.22) 
 saṃkarākhyaṃ tu durmelyaṃ | priye mṛdukharāhvayam | 
 tataḥ saṃmṛditaṃ devi | dvaṃdvamelāpanaṃ drutam | 
 bhavet samarasaṃ garbhe | rasarājasya ca dravet || (RA_8.23) 
 ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi | dvaṃdvamelāpanaṃ śṛṇu || (RA_8.24) 
 varṣābhūkadalīkanda- | kākamācīpunarnavāḥ | 
 cūrṇaṃ narakapālaṃ ca | guñjāṭaṅkaṇasaṃyutam | 
 kṣīratailena sudhmātaṃ | hemābhraṃ milati priye || (RA_8.25) 
 anenaiva vidhānena | tārābhram api melayet || (RA_8.26) 
 vaṅgamāvartya deveśi | punaḥ sūtakayojitam | 
 kadalīkandatoyena | mardayeṭṭaṅkaṇānvitam | 
 andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ | vaṅgābhraṃ milati kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_8.27) 
 cūrṇaṃ narakapālasya | strīstanyaṃ vanaśigrukam | 
 guñjāṭaṅkaṇasaṃyuktaṃ | vaṅgābhraṃ milati kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_8.28) 
 abhrakaṃ cūrṇayitvā tu | kākamācīrasaplutam | 
 kapitthatoyasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ | rasaṭaṅkaṇasaṃyutam | 
 vaṅgapattrāntaranyastaṃ | dhmātaṃ vaṅgābhrakaṃ milet ||
                    (RA_8.29) 
 āvartya kaṭutailena | bhasmāpāmārgajaṃ kṣipet | 
 vaṅgābhraṃ haritālaṃ ca | nāgābhre tu manaḥśilāḥ ||
                    (RA_8.30) 
 hemābhraṃ nāgatāpyena | tārābhraṃ vaṅgatālakāt | 
 gandhakena tu śulvābhraṃ | tīkṣṇābhraṃ sindhuhiṅgulāt | 
 vaṅgābhraṃ haritālena | nāgābhraṃ śilayā milet || (RA_8.31) 
 lāṅgalī cāmarīkeśaṃ | kārpāsāsthikulatthakam | 
 bhūlatā cāśmadalanī | strīstanyaṃ suragopakaḥ || (RA_8.32) 
 etatpraliptamūṣāyāṃ | sudhmātāstīvravahninā | 
 kāntābhraśailavimalā | milanti sakalān kṣaṇāt || (RA_8.33) 
 latāchuchundarīmāṃsaṃ | viṣaṭaṅkaṇayojitam | 
 mūṣālepena kurute | sarvadvaṃdveṣu melanam || (RA_8.34) 
 abhrakaṃ surasā śṛṅgaṃ | maṇḍūkasya vasā viṣam | 
 guñjāṭaṅkaṇayogena | sarvasattveṣu melanam || (RA_8.35) 
 ṭaṅkaṇorṇāgirijatu- | karṇākhyāmalakarkaṭaiḥ | 
 milanti sarvadvaṃdvāni | strīstanyaparipeṣitaiḥ || (RA_8.36) 
 dhātakīgugguluguḍa- | sarjayāvakaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ | 
 strīstanyapeṣitaiḥ sarvaṃ | dvaṃdvajaṃ tu rasāyane ||
                    (RA_8.37) 
 khasattvaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu | pūrvakalkena saṃyutam | 
 andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ | saṃkaraṃ milati kṣaṇāt || (RA_8.38) 
 vāpitaṃ tāpyarasaka- | sasyakair daradena ca | 
 khasattvaṃ syānnibaddhaṃ ca | dṛḍhaṃ dhmātaṃ milettataḥ ||
                    (RA_8.39) 
 rasoparasalohāni | sarvāṇyekatra dhāmayet | 
 anyonyaṃ dvaṃdvatāṃ yānti | dravanti salilaṃ yathā ||
                    (RA_8.40) 
 bījāni kalpitānyevaṃ | rañjitāni paraṃ śṛṇu || (RA_8.41) 
 ghanaṃ mākṣikacūrṇena | śulvacūrṇena rañjitam | 
 dvaṃdvitaṃ tāpyasattvena | rasarājasya rañjanam || (RA_8.42) 
 āraktavallīgomūtraḥ | bahudhā paribhāvitaiḥ | 
 kunaṭīgandhapāṣāṇair | hemamākṣikahiṅgulaiḥ || (RA_8.43) 
 vāpitaṃ sevitaṃ rakta- | gaṇaiḥ snehair mṛtaṃ tataḥ | 
 rañjanaṃ rasarājasya | tīkṣṇatāmrau viśeṣataḥ || (RA_8.44) 
 kevalaṃ vimalaṃ tāmraṃ | vāpitaṃ daradena ca | 
 kurute triguṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ | lākṣābhaṃ nirmalaṃ rasam ||
                    (RA_8.45) 
 rasakaṃ dviguṇaṃ dattvā | tāmraṃ sudhmātamīśvari | 
 kṛṣṇābhrakasya cūrṇaṃ ca | raktavargair muhuḥ puṭaiḥ ||
                    (RA_8.46) 
 tāpyena vā mṛtaṃ hema | triguṇena nivāpitam | 
 bhāṇḍikāyāṃ tu rasakaṃ | tāpyasaindhavasaṃyutam || (RA_8.47) 
 indragopanibhaṃ yāvat | sarvaṃ dviguṇajāraṇāt | 
 drutaṃ hemanibhaṃ sūtaṃ | kurute nātra saṃśayaḥ || (RA_8.48) 
 abhrakaṃ hema tāmraṃ ca | śilayā mākṣikeṇa ca | 
 gairikeṇa ca mukhyena | rasakena ca rañjayet || (RA_8.49) 
 bījāni rañjitānyevaṃ | pakvabījānyataḥ śṛṇu || (RA_8.50) 
 mahārasānuparasān | tīkṣṇalohāni ca kṣipet | 
 samāṃśaṃ samamākṣīkaṃ | gandhakāvāpayogataḥ || (RA_8.51) 
 śataśo vāpayed etat | akṣīṇaṃ sāvaśeṣitam | 
 samāṃśaṃ rasarājasya | garbhe dravati niścitam || (RA_8.52) 
 tadetadviṣṭikāstambhe | jāraṇāyāṃ sureśvari | 
 rañjane rasarājasya | sāraṇāyāṃ ca śasyate || (RA_8.53) 
 tadeva śataśo rakta- | gaṇaiḥ snehair niṣecitam | 
 adhikaṃ śasyate teṣu | sahasrāṃśena vedhakṛt || (RA_8.54) 
 nirvyūḍhaṃ nāgavaṅgābhyāṃ | kriyāyāṃ hematārayoḥ | 
 khasattvaṃ raviṇā yojyaṃ | dvaṃdvitaṃ syādrasāyane ||
                    (RA_8.55) 
 sasnehakṣārapañcāmlaiḥ | rasaistaistālakādibhiḥ | 
 samadvitriguṇān tāmre | vāhayed vaṅgapannagān || (RA_8.56) 
 raktasnehaniṣiktaṃ tad | rasākṛṣṭiriti smṛtam || (RA_8.57) 
 mākṣikaṃ gandhapāṣāṇaṃ | haritālaṃ manaḥśilām | 
 vaikrāntakaṃ kāntamukhyaṃ | sasyakaṃ vimalāñjanam | 
 rasakaṃ vāpitaṃ śaśvac- | cūrṇitaṃ hemni vāhayet ||
                    (RA_8.58) 
 lohaparpaṭikātāpya- | kaṅkuṣṭhavimalābhrakaiḥ | 
 mṛtaśulvaśilāsattva- | snuhyarkakṣīrahiṅgulaiḥ | 
 nāgo nirjīvatāṃ yāti | puṭayogaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ || (RA_8.59) 
 rasatālakaśaṅkhābhra- | ciñcākṣāraistathā trapuḥ | 
 mṛtaṃ nāgaṃ mṛtaṃ vaṅgaṃ | śulvaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca vā mṛtam | 
 ekaikamuttame hemni | vāhayet suravandite || (RA_8.60) 
 nirutthe pannage hemni | nirvyūḍhe śataśo gaṇe | 
 gorocanānibhaṃ dhāma | bhāskare tārasaṃnibham || (RA_8.61) 
 tīkṣṇābhrakaṃ ravisamaṃ | mākṣikaṃ dviguṇaṃ tathā | 
 āvartitaṃ cūrṇitaṃ ca | māritaṃ saptabhiḥ puṭaiḥ ||
                    (RA_8.62) 
 vyūḍhe śataguṇe hemni | tadbījaṃ jārayet samam | 
 candrārkapattralepena | śatabhāgena vedhayet || (RA_8.63) 
 ūrdhvādho mākṣikaṃ dattvā | śulvaṃ hemasamaṃ bhavet | 
 evaṃ daśaguṇaṃ vyūḍhaṃ | bījaṃ kāraṇasaṃnibham || (RA_8.64) 
 rasakābhraṃ kāntatāmre | bhāgavṛddhyā dhamettataḥ | 
 mākṣikeṇa hataṃ tac ca | bīje nirvāhayet priye || (RA_8.65) 
 dvātriṃśadguṇitaṃ hemni | nāgaṃ tāpyaṃ hataṃ vahet | 
 triṃśadguṇaśilāvāpaṃ | nāgabījamudāhṛtam || (RA_8.66) 
 tāpyatālakavāpena | sattvaṃ pītābhrakasya tu | 
 bīje nirvāhayed etat | yoṣāmṛṣṭasya vedhakam || (RA_8.67) 
 nāgaḥ karoti mṛdutāṃ | nirvyūḍhastāṃ ca raktatām | 
 vāpitaṃ pītatāṃ tīkṣṇaṃ | kāntasthāṃ kālikāṃ viṣam ||
                    (RA_8.68) 
 hemabījamiti proktaṃ | tārabījamataḥ śṛṇu || (RA_8.69) 
 tīkṣṇābhratāpyavimala- | rasakaṃ samabhāgikam | 
 vaṅgabhāgāstu catvāraḥ | sarvaṃ dhmātaṃ vicūrṇitam ||
                    (RA_8.70) 
 puṭena nihataṃ kāryaṃ | vyūḍhaṃ tāraṃ tu vedhayet | 
 dvātriṃśatsadguṇaṃ tāre | vaṅge tāpyaṃ hataṃ vahet | 
 triṃśadguṇāt tālavāpāt | vaṅgabījamudāhṛtam || (RA_8.71) 
 kuṭilaṃ vimalaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ | khasattvaṃ cāpi vāhayet | 
 vaṅgābhraṃ tāpyasattvaṃ vā | tālamākṣikavāpataḥ | 
 śuklapuṣpagaṇaiḥ sekaṃ | snehayuktaistu kārayet || (RA_8.72) 
 uktāni tārabījāni | bījānāṃ rañjanaṃ śṛṇu || (RA_8.73) 
 tīkṣṇamākṣikaśulvaṃ ca | nāgaṃ capalamāritam | 
 sindūrasaṃnibhaṃ yāvat | tena bījāni rañjayet || (RA_8.74) 
 nidhāya kharpare nāgaṃ | brahmabījadalaiḥ saha | 
 dagdhamagnimadho dattvā | vahnivarṇaṃ yadā bhavet ||
                    (RA_8.75) 
 vāsakena vibhītena | śākakiṃśukaśigrubhiḥ | 
 koraṇḍakasya puṣpeṇa | bakulasyārjunasya ca || (RA_8.76) 
 ahimāreṇa nāginyā | kumāryā nāgakanyayā | 
 śilayā ca triguṇayā | kvathitenājavāriṇā || (RA_8.77) 
 bhāvitaṃ kharparasthaṃ ca | plāvayitvā punaḥ punaḥ | 
 saptabhirdivasair eva | māritaṃ suravandite || (RA_8.78) 
 puṭayed gandhakenādāv | āmlaiś ca tadanantaram | 
 idaṃ dalānāṃ bījānāṃ | rasarājasya rañjane | 
 udghāṭe krāmaṇe yojyaṃ | piṣṭīstambhe viśeṣataḥ || (RA_8.79) 
 mañjiṣṭhākiṃśukarase | khadiraṃ raktacandanam | 
 karavīraṃ devadāruṃ | saralaṃ rajanīdvayam || (RA_8.80) 
 anyāni raktapuṣpāṇi | piṣṭvā lākṣārasena tu | 
 tailaṃ vipācayed devi | tena bījāni rañjayet || (RA_8.81) 
 dviguṇe raktapuṣpāṇāṃ | raktapītagaṇasya ca | 
 kvāthe caturguṇe kṣīre | tailamekaṃ sureśvari || (RA_8.82) 
 jyotiṣmatīkarañjākhya- | kaṭutumbīsamudbhavam | 
 pāṭalīpippalīkāma- | kākatuṇḍīrasānvitam || (RA_8.83) 
 bhekaśūkarameṣāhi- | matsyakūrmajalaukasām | 
 vasayā caikayā yuktaṃ | ṣoḍaśāṃśaiḥ supeṣitaiḥ || (RA_8.84) 
 bhūlatāmalamākṣīka- | dvaṃdvamelāpanauṣadhaiḥ | 
 pācitaṃ gālitaṃ caitat | sāraṇā tailamucyate || (RA_8.85) 
 rasatulyaṃ yathā bījaṃ | gataṃ garbhadrutiṃ priye | 
 vyāpakatvena sarve ca | samabhāgāstatheṣyate || (RA_8.86) 
 pakvaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ samaṃ garbhe | yaddravedrañjayec ca tam ||
                    (RA_8.87) 
 evamuktāni bījāni | jārayed viḍayogataḥ | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_8.88) 
 
 

                9 [Viḍakathana]

                  śrīdevyuvāca 
 bījānāṃ kalanaṃ proktaṃ | viśeṣeṇa ca sādhanam | 
 jāryante tāni yaiḥ sūte | tān viḍān vaktumarhasi || (RA_9.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 kāsīsaṃ saindhavaṃ kāṅkṣī | sauvīraṃ vyoṣagandhakam | 
 sauvarcalaṃ sarjikā ca | mālatīnīrasambhavam | 
 śigrumūlarasaiḥ sikto | viḍo 'yaṃ sarvajāraṇaḥ || (RA_9.2) 
 nirdagdhaṃ śaṅkhacūrṇaṃ tu | ravikṣīraśataplutam | 
 puṭitaṃ bahuśo devi | praśasto jāraṇāviḍaḥ || (RA_9.3) 
 śataśo vā plutaṃ cūrṇaṃ | gandhakasya gavāṃ jalaiḥ ||
                    (RA_9.4) 
 nirdagdhaṃ śaṅkhacūrṇaṃ tu | śigrumūlāmbubhāvitam | 
 śataśo viṣasindhūttha- | saṃyutaṃ vaḍavāmukham || (RA_9.5) 
 ṭaṅkaṇaṃ śataśo devi | bhāvayet kiṃśukadravaiḥ | 
 viḍo vahnimukhākhyo 'yaṃ | lohānāṃ jāraṇe priye || (RA_9.6) 
 cūlikā gandhapāṣāṇaḥ | kāntasya ca mukhaṃ priye | 
 ekaikameva paryāptaṃ | lauhacūrṇasya jāraṇe || (RA_9.7) 
 gandhatālakasindhūtthaṃ | cūlīṭaṅkaṇabhūkhagam | 
 kṣārairmūtraiś ca vipaced | ayaṃ jvālāmukho viḍaḥ || (RA_9.8) 
 ekaviṃśatiparyāyaṃ | devadālīdaladravaiḥ | 
 bhāvito niculakṣāraḥ | sarvasattvāni jārayet || (RA_9.9) 
 vāstukair aṇḍakadalī- | devadālīpunarnavam | 
 vāsā palāśaniculaṃ | tilakāñcanamākṣikam || (RA_9.10) 
 sarvāṅgaṃ khaṇḍaśaśchinnaṃ | nātiśuṣkaṃ śilātale | 
 dagdhakāṇḍais tilānāṃ tu | pañcāṅgaṃ mūlakasya ca ||
                    (RA_9.11) 
 plāvayen mūtravargeṇa | jalaṃ tasmāt parisrutam | 
 lohapātre pacedyantre | haṃsapāke 'gnimānavit || (RA_9.12) 
 bāṣpāṇāṃ budbudānāṃ ca | bahūnāmudgamo yadā | 
 tadā kāsīsasaurāṣṭrī- | kṣāratrayakaṭutrayam || (RA_9.13) 
 gandhakaṃ ca sitaṃ hiṅgu- | lavaṇāni ca ṣaṭ tathā | 
 eṣāṃ cūrṇaṃ kṣipedeṣa | lohasampuṭamadhyagaḥ | 
 saptāhaṃ bhūgataḥ paścād | dhānyasthaḥ pravaro viḍaḥ ||
                    (RA_9.14) 
 jambīrāmlena pacanaṃ | śigrumūladraveṇa ca | 
 cūlikāgandhakāsiktau | dvau viḍau śataśaḥ kramāt ||
                    (RA_9.15) 
 koṣātakīdalarasaiḥ | kṣārair vā niculodbhavaiḥ | 
 devadālīśivābījaṃ | guñjāsaindhavaṭaṅkaṇam | 
 bhāvayed amlavargeṇa | viḍo 'yaṃ hemajāraṇaḥ || (RA_9.16) 
 mūlakārdrakacitrāṇāṃ | kṣārair gomūtragālitaiḥ | 
 gandhakaḥ śataśo bhāvyo | viḍo 'yaṃ hemajāraṇe || (RA_9.17) 
 haritālaśilākṣāro | lavaṇaṃ śaṅkhaśuktikā | 
 haṃsapākavipakvo 'yaṃ | viḍaḥ syād dhemajāraṇe || (RA_9.18) 
 evaṃ saṃgṛhya sambhārān | rasakarma samācaret | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_9.19) 
 
 

                10 [Rasaśodhana]


                  śrīdevyuvāca 
 rasasya lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃvā | rasakarma ca kīdṛśam | 
 tanna jānāmi deveśa | vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ || (RA_10.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 prāgevoktā rasotpattis | tallakṣaṇam ataḥ śṛṇu || (RA_10.2) 
 tasya nāmasahasrāṇi | ayutānyarbudāni ca | 
 śakyate na mayā vaktuṃ | saṃkṣepāt kathyate śṛṇu ||
                    (RA_10.3) 
 raso rasendraḥ sūtaś ca | pāradaścātha miśrakaḥ || (RA_10.4) 
 rasaṃ siddharasaṃ vidyāt | siddhakṣetrasamāśrayam | 
 nāśayet sakalān rogān | valīpalitam eva saḥ || (RA_10.5) 
 dehalohakaraṃ śuddhaṃ | rasendramadhunā śṛṇu | 
 śarīre hemni kartā ca | jāraṇe sāraṇāsu ca || (RA_10.6) 
 īṣatpītaś ca rūkṣāṅgo | doṣayuktaś ca sūtakaḥ || (RA_10.7) 
 yo bāhyābhyantare śveto | bahulaṃ kañcukāvṛtaḥ | 
 taṃ vidyāt pāradaṃ devi | tārakarmaṇi yojayet ||
                    (RA_10.8:1) 
 yathā kāñjikasaṃsparśāt | kṣīrabhāṇḍaṃ vinaśyati | 
 tathā hema śarīraṃ ca | pāradena vinaśyati || (RA_10.8:2) 
 mayūrapattrikābhāsaṃ | miśrakaṃ ca vidurbudhāḥ | 
 dhūmravarṇaṃ rasaṃ dṛṣṭvā | viśeṣeṇopalabhyate | 
 miśrakaṃ tu vijānīyād | udvāhakarmakārakam || (RA_10.9) 
 evaṃ pañcavidhā devi | rasabhedā nirūpitāḥ || (RA_10.10) 
 svedanaṃ mardanaṃ caiva | cāraṇaṃ jāraṇaṃ tathā | 
 drāvaṇaṃ rañjanaṃ caiva | sāraṇaṃ krāmaṇaṃ kramāt | 
 iti yo vetti tattvena | tasya sidhyati sūtakaḥ ||
                    (RA_10.11) 
 tīvratvaṃ jāyate svedāt | amalatvaṃ ca mardanāt | 
 cāraṇena balaṃ kuryāt | jāraṇādbandhanaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_10.12) 
 ekatvaṃ drāvaṇāt tasya | raktatvaṃ raktakāñjanāt | 
 vyāpitvaṃ sāraṇāt tasya | krāmitvaṃ krāmaṇāttathā ||
                    (RA_10.13) 
 malago malarūpeṇa | tvarito haṃsago bhavet | 
 malago malarūpeṇa | sadhūmo dhūmago bhavet || (RA_10.14) 
 anyā jīvagatirdevi | jīvo 'ṇḍādiva niṣkramet | 
 sa tāvajjīvayejjīvaṃ | tena jīvo rasaḥ smṛtaḥ || (RA_10.15) 
 catuṣṭayī gatistasya | nipuṇena tu labhyate | 
 catasro gatayo dṛśyā | adṛśyā pañcamī gatiḥ || (RA_10.16) 
 mantradhyānādinā tasya | kṣīyate pañcamī gatiḥ ||
                    (RA_10.17) 
 dhūmaściṭiciṭiścaiva | maṇḍūkaplutireva ca | 
 akampaś ca vikampaś ca | pañcāvasthā rasasya tu ||
                    (RA_10.18) 
 mathyamānasya kalkena | sambhaveddhi gatitrayam | 
 jale gatirmalagatiḥ | punar haṃsagatistataḥ || (RA_10.19) 
 hema dattvā tataḥ śuddhaṃ | tat tu stambhen niyāmake | 
 niyāmakagaṇauṣadhyā | rasaṃ dattvā vipācayet || (RA_10.20) 
 niyamito na prayāti | tathā dhūmagatiṃ śive || (RA_10.21) 
 kaṇikācālarahito | budbudaiścāpavarjitaḥ | 
 niyamito bhavatyeṣa | cullikāgnisahastathā || (RA_10.22) 
 aniyamya yadā sūtaṃ | jārayet kāñjikāśaye | 
 jāyate niścitaṃ bhadre | tadā tasya gatitrayam ||
                    (RA_10.23) 
 dolāsvedena cāvaśyaṃ | svedito hi dinatrayam | 
 vasubhaṇṭādibhirdevi | rasarājo na hīyate || (RA_10.24) 
 akṣīṇaṃ tu rasaṃ dṛṣṭvā | dadyādvyomādikaṃ tataḥ | 
 svedanaṃ ca tataḥ karma | dīyamānasya mardanam ||
                    (RA_10.25) 
 rasāliṅgita āhāraḥ | piṣṭiketyabhidhīyate | 
 taddrutaṃ rasagarbhe tu | jāraṇaṃ parikīrtitam ||
                    (RA_10.26) 
 jāraṇā tatsamākhyātā | tadevaṃ copalabhyate | 
 jīrṇānte rañjanaṃ kāryaṃ | raktavargagaṇena ca ||
                    (RA_10.27) 
 jīrṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ tu saṃraktaṃ | samahemnā tu sārayet | 
 sāraṇāyantrayogena | badhyate sārito rasaḥ || (RA_10.28) 
 sāritaḥ sāritaścaiva | yathā bhavati sūtakaḥ | 
 krāmaṇena samāyuktaṃ | taṃ ca vedhe niyojayet || (RA_10.29) 
 āroṭaḥ pārado brahmā | mūrchitas tu janārdanaḥ | 
 baddhas tu rudrarūpaḥ syāt | karmayogabalādrasaḥ ||
                    (RA_10.30) 
 śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi | karmayogasya vistaram || (RA_10.31) 
 pāradasya trayo doṣā | viṣaṃ vahnirmalas tathā | 
 viṣeṇa saviṣaṃ vidyāt | vahnau kuṣṭhī bhavennaraḥ | 
 malenodararogī syāt | mriyate ca rasāyane || (RA_10.32) 
 ṣaṭtruṭyaścaikalikṣā syāt | ṣaḍlikṣā yūka eva ca | 
 ṣaḍyūkāstu rajaḥsaṃjñāḥ | kathitāstava suvrate ||
                    (RA_10.33) 
 ṣaḍrajaḥ sarṣapaḥ sākṣāt | siddhārthaḥ sa ca kīrtitaḥ | 
 ṣaṭsiddhārthāś ca deveśi | yavastvekaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||
                    (RA_10.34) 
 ṣaḍyavair ekaguñjā syāt | ṣaḍguñjāścaikamāṣakaḥ | 
 māṣā dvādaśa tolaḥ syāt | aṣṭau tolāḥ palaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_10.35) 
 dvātriṃśatpalakaṃ devi | śubhaṃ tu parikīrtitam | 
 śubhasya tu sahasre dve | bhāra ekaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||
                    (RA_10.36) 
 dve sahasre palānāṃ tu | sahasraṃ śatameva vā | 
 aṣṭāviṃśat palānāṃ tu | daśa pañcakameva vā || (RA_10.37) 
 palārdhenaiva saṃskāraḥ | kartavyaḥ sūtakasya tu ||
                    (RA_10.38) 
 mahābalā nāgabalā | meghanādā punarnavā | 
 meṣaśṛṅgī ca tatsāraiḥ | navasārasamanvitam | 
 pāradaṃ devadeveśi | svedayed divasatrayam || (RA_10.39) 
 girikarṇī ca mīnākṣī | sahadevī punarnavā | 
 uragā triphalā kāntā | laghuparṇī śatāvarī || (RA_10.40) 
 tuṣavarje tu dhānyāmle | sarvaṃ saṃkṣubhya nikṣipet | 
 ekādaśaguṇe 'mle 'smin | ṣoḍaśāṃśair vimarditam ||
                    (RA_10.41) 
 āsurīlavaṇavyoṣa- | citrakārdrakamūlakaiḥ | 
 dolāyāṃ svedayed devi | tridinaṃ mṛdunāgninā || (RA_10.42) 
 aṅkolas tu viṣaṃ hanti | vahnimāragvadhaḥ priye | 
 citrakas tu malaṃ hanyāt | kumārī saptakañcukam ||
                    (RA_10.43) 
 tasmād ebhiḥ samopetair | mardayet pātayed budhaḥ ||
                    (RA_10.44) 
 vidyādhareṇa yantreṇa | bhāvayed doṣavarjitam | 
 tatastriguṇavastrasthaṃ | taṃ rasaṃ devi gālitam ||
                    (RA_10.45) 
 triphalāvahnimūlatvāt | gṛhakanyārasānvitam | 
 nirudgāre tu pāṣāṇe | mardayet pātayet punaḥ || (RA_10.46) 
 dhūmasāraguḍavyoṣa- | rajanīsitasarṣapaiḥ | 
 iṣṭikākāñjikorṇābhiḥ | tridinaṃ mardayet tataḥ ||
                    (RA_10.47) 
 nirmalo jāyate sūtaḥ | matprabhāvaṃ prakāśayet ||
                    (RA_10.48) 
 vāsakena vibhītena | mardayet pātayet punaḥ | 
 nāgavaṅgādikā doṣā | yānti nāśam upādhijāḥ || (RA_10.49) 
 saptavāraṃ kākamācyā | gatadoṣaṃ vimardayet | 
 pātayet saptavāraṃ ca | giridoṣaṃ tyajedrasaḥ || (RA_10.50) 
 kṣetradoṣaṃ tyajeddevi | gokarṇarasamūrchitaḥ || (RA_10.51) 
 kārpāsapattraniryāse | svinnas trikaṭukānvite | 
 saptakañcukanirmuktaḥ | saptāhājjāyate rasaḥ || (RA_10.52) 
 kākamācī jayā brāhmī | gāṅgerī raktacitrakaḥ | 
 maṇḍūkī mudgaparṇī ca | śṛṅgaveraṃ rasāṅkuśaḥ || (RA_10.53) 
 devadālī śaṅkhapuṣpī | kākajaṅghā śatāvarī | 
 kumārī bhṛṅgarājaś ca | nirguṇḍī grīṣmasundaraḥ ||
                    (RA_10.54) 
 śūlinī śūrpaparṇī ca | gojihvā kṣīrakañcukaḥ | 
 tadrasair marditaḥ pātyaḥ | saptadhā nirmalo bhavet ||
                    (RA_10.55) 
 tāmreṇa piṣṭikāṃ kṛtvā | pātayed ūrdhvapātane | 
 vaṅganāgau parityajya | śuddho bhavati sūtakaḥ ||
                    (RA_10.56) 
 marditas triphalāśigru- | rājikāpaṭucitrakaiḥ | 
 ūrdhvabhāṇḍagataḥ pācyaḥ | pradīptair upalair adhaḥ ||
                    (RA_10.57) 
 sṛṣṭyambujanirodhena | labdhaprāyo bhavedrasaḥ | 
 karkoṭīkañcukībimbī- | sarpākṣyambujasaṃyutam || (RA_10.58) 
 rasaṃ niyāmake dadyāt | tejasvī nirmalo bhavet | 
 evaṃ viśodhitaḥ sūto | bhadrāṣṭāṃśaviśoṣitaḥ || (RA_10.59) 
 kṣudrāmlalavaṇakṣāra- | bhūkhagoṣaṇaśigrubhiḥ | 
 rājikāṭaṅkaṇayutair | āranāle dinatrayam | 
 svedanāddīpito devi | grāsārthī jāyate rasaḥ || (RA_10.60) 
 vyomasattvādibījāni | rasajāraṇaśodhane | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_10.61) 
 
 

                11 [Bālajāraṇa]


                  śrīdevyuvāca 
 lakṣaṇaṃ śodhanaṃ caiva | pāradasya śrutaṃ mayā | 
 cāraṇaṃ jāraṇaṃ caiva | śrotumicchāmi bhairava || (RA_11.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 sarvapāpakṣaye jāte | prāpyate rasajāraṇā | 
 tatprāptau prāptameva syād | vijñānaṃ muktikāraṇam ||
                    (RA_11.2) 
 mokṣābhivyañjakaṃ devi | jāraṇaṃ sādhakasya tu | 
 yāvanna jāryate sūtaḥ | tāvat tu na ca nirvṛtiḥ || (RA_11.3) 
 khallas tu pīṭhikā devi | rasendro liṅgamucyate | 
 mardanaṃ vandanaṃ tasya | grāsaḥ pūjā vidhīyate || (RA_11.4) 
 yāvad dināni vahnistho | jāryate dhāryate rasaḥ | 
 tāvadyugasahasrāṇi | śivaloke mahīyate || (RA_11.5) 
 dinamekaṃ rasendrasya | yo dadāti hutāśanam | 
 dravanti tasya pāpāni | kurvannapi na lipyate || (RA_11.6) 
 jāraṇā dvividhā bāla- | jāraṇā baddhajāraṇā | 
 tatrādau parameśāni | vakṣyate bālajāraṇā || (RA_11.7) 
 gaganaṃ jārayed ādau | sarvasattvamataḥ param | 
 tato mākṣikaśuddhaṃ ca | suvarṇaṃ tadanantaram || (RA_11.8) 
 garbhasthaṃ drāvayitvā tu | tato bāhyadrutiṃ dravet | 
 sitaṃ sitena dravyeṇa | raktaṃ raktena rañjayet || (RA_11.9) 
 sāraṇaṃ krāmaṇaṃ jñātvā | tato vedhaṃ prayojayet ||
                    (RA_11.10) 
 oṃ namo 'mṛtalohāya parāmṛtarasodbhavāya huṃ svāhā || Ras_11.11 || 
 sarvasattvopakārāya | bhagavan tvadanujñayā | 
 jāraṇaṃ kartumicchāmi | grāsaṃ gṛhṇa mama prabho ||
                    (RA_11.12) 
 kuruṣveti śivenoktaṃ | grāhyameva subuddhinā || (RA_11.13) 
 śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi | vyomajāraṇam uttamam | 
 pattrābhrajāraṇaṃ sattva- | jāraṇaṃ ceti taddvidhā ||
                    (RA_11.14) 
 nirmukhaṃ samukhaṃ caiva | vāsanāmukhameva ca | 
 ekaikaṃ trividhaṃ tac ca | tad vakṣyāmy ānupūrvaśaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.15) 
 vaikrāntavajrasaṃsparśād | divyauṣadhibalena vā | 
 nirmukho bhakṣayed devi | kṣaṇena gaganaṃ rasaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.16) 
 hemakarmaṇi hemaiva | tāre tāro mukhaṃ bhavet || (RA_11.17) 
 taptakhallakṛtā piṣṭiḥ | ślakṣṇam alpālpamabhrakam | 
 amlavetasajambīra- | bījapūrāmlabhūkhagaiḥ | 
 marditaṃ carate devi | seyaṃ samukhajāraṇā || (RA_11.18) 
 kṣāratrayaṃ pañcapaṭu | kākṣīkāsīsagandhakam | 
 mākṣikaṃ cāmlasaṃyuktaṃ | tāmrapātre tu jārayet ||
                    (RA_11.19) 
 etaccābhiṣavād divyaṃ | kārayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ | 
 jāraṇārthaṃ ca bījānāṃ | vajrāṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||
                    (RA_11.20) 
 tasminnāvartitaṃ nāgaṃ | vaṅgaṃ vā suravandite | 
 niṣecayec chataṃ vāraṃ | na rasāyanakarmaṇi || (RA_11.21) 
 anena sakalaṃ devi | cāraṇāvas tu bhāvayet | 
 kṣārāmle bhāvitaṃ vyoma | rajasā prathamena ca ||
                    (RA_11.22) 
 sṛṣṭitrayodakakaṇā- | tumburudravamarditam | 
 carejjaredvā puṭitaṃ | yavaciñcārasena ca || (RA_11.23) 
 śatāvarī gadā rambhā | meghanādā punarnavā | 
 śigruko yavaciñcā ca | bhāvitaṃ tadrasaiḥ kramāt ||
                    (RA_11.24) 
 mūlaṃ hilamucāyāstu | kauverīmūlameva ca | 
 kadalīmusalīśigru- | tāmbūlīvāṇapīlukam || (RA_11.25) 
 alambuṣā balā kolam | āsphoṭaḥ kharamañjarī | 
 tumburustiktaśākaṃ vāpy | eṣām ekarasena tu | 
 rājikāvyoṣayuktena | tridinaṃ svinnamabhrakam || (RA_11.26) 
 kāsīsatuvarīsindhu- | ṭaṅkaṇakṣārasaṃyutaḥ | 
 pūrvābhiṣavayogena | sūtakaścarati kṣaṇāt || (RA_11.27) 
 golako bhavati kṣipraṃ | sarvasiddhipradāyakaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.28) 
 gṛhītvā devi dhānyāmlam | amlavargeṇa saṃyutam | 
 kvāthayitvābhrakaṃ tat tu | snuhīkṣīreṇa mardayet ||
                    (RA_11.29) 
 āraṇyagomayenaiva | kapotākhyaṃ puṭaṃ tataḥ || (RA_11.30) 
 kadalīkandaniryāsair | mūlakandarasena ca | 
 kākamācī ca mīnākṣī | apāmārgo munistathā || (RA_11.31) 
 eraṇḍamārdrakaṃ caiva | meghanādā punarnavā | 
 ekaikasya dravair eva | puṭaikaikaṃ pradāpayet ||
                    (RA_11.32) 
 vajrīkṣīreṇa saṃyuktaṃ | dolāyantreṇa pācayet | 
 chāyāśuṣkaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā | caṇakāmlena saṃyutam ||
                    (RA_11.33) 
 navasāraṃ ca kāsīsaṃ | vacāṃ nimbaṃ tathaiva ca | 
 abhrasya ṣoḍaśāṃśena | ekaikaṃ tatra nikṣipet || (RA_11.34) 
 nidhāya tāmrapātre tu | gharṣayet tac ca suvrate | 
 navavāraṃ tato devi | lohapātre tu jārayet || (RA_11.35) 
 rasena saha deveśi | caṇakāmlena kāñjikam | 
 mṛdvagninā tu niṣkvāthyaṃ | praharārdhena jāyeta ||
                    (RA_11.36) 
 somavallīrasaiḥ piṣṭvā | vyoma sauvarcalānvitam | 
 śanaiḥ śanair haṃsapādyā | dāpayec ca puṭatrayam ||
                    (RA_11.37) 
 somavallīrasenaiva | saptavāraṃ ca dāpayet | 
 pātayen mṛnmaye bhāṇḍe | rasena saha saṃyutam || (RA_11.38) 
 mūlaṃ siteṣupuṅkhāyā | gavyakṣīreṇa gharṣayet | 
 kalkena lepayet sūtaṃ | gaganaṃ ca tadūrdhvagam ||
                    (RA_11.39) 
 tāpayed ravitāpena | nirmukhaṃ grasate kṣaṇam | 
 jāyate piṣṭikā śīghraṃ | nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || (RA_11.40) 
 tilaparṇīrasenaiva | gaganaṃ bhāvayet priye | 
 mardanājjāyate piṣṭī | nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || (RA_11.41) 
 muṇḍīniryāsake nāgaṃ | bahuśas tu niṣecayet | 
 tenābhrakaṃ tu saṃplāvya | bhūyobhūyaḥ puṭe dahet ||
                    (RA_11.42) 
 citrakārdrakamūlānām | ekaikena tu saptadhā | 
 plāvitavyaṃ prayatnena | gandhakābhrakacūrṇakam ||
                    (RA_11.43) 
 nāgaśuṇḍīrasastanya- | rajoluṅgāmlabhāvitam | 
 ṣoḍaśāṃśena tadvattaṃ | dolāyāṃ tu caredrasaḥ || (RA_11.44) 
 catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ devi | dvātriṃśadguṇameva vā | 
 athavā ṣoḍaśaguṇaṃ | tathāṣṭaguṇameva vā | 
 caturguṇaṃ vā dviguṇaṃ | samaṃ vā cārayet priye ||
                    (RA_11.45) 
 paramabhrakasattvasya | jāraṇaṃ śṛṇu pārvati || (RA_11.46) 
 vyomasattvaṃ samāṃśena | tāpyasattvena saṃyutam | 
 sa khalvevaṃ careddevi | garbhadrāvī bhavedrasaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.47) 
 nāgābhraṃ devi vaṅgābhraṃ | tīkṣṇābhraṃ bhāskarābhrakam | 
 tārābhraṃ devi hemābhraṃ | rasagarbheṇa jārayet ||
                    (RA_11.48) 
 pūrvābhiṣekayogena | garbhe dravati mardanāt || (RA_11.49) 
 catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśakaḥ pūrvaḥ | dvātriṃśāṃśo dvitīyakaḥ | 
 tṛtīyaḥ ṣoḍaśāṃśas tu | caturtho 'ṣṭāṃśa eva ca ||
                    (RA_11.50) 
 pañcamas tu caturthāṃśaḥ | ṣaṣṭho dvyaṃśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ | 
 grāso rasasya dātavyaḥ | sasattvasyābhrakasya ca ||
                    (RA_11.51) 
 catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśake grāse | daṇḍadhārī bhavedrasaḥ | 
 jalaukāvaddvitīye ca | grāsayoge sureśvari || (RA_11.52) 
 grāsena tu tṛtīyena | kākaviṣṭhāsamo bhavet | 
 grāsena tu caturthena | dadhimaṇḍasamo bhavet || (RA_11.53) 
 pañcame carite grāse | navanītasamo bhavet | 
 ṣaṣṭhe tu golakākāraḥ | kramājjīrṇasya lakṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_11.54) 
 kāñjikena niṣiktena | raktavyoma śataplutam | 
 khallāntaścārayet tac ca | śulvavāsanayā saha || (RA_11.55) 
 hema tāraṃ ca saṃghṛṣya | khalle tatra rasaṃ nyaset | 
 kāñjīsahitakāsīsaṃ | sindhunā carate rasaḥ || (RA_11.56) 
 hema sīsaṃ tu saṃghṛṣya | rasaṃ tatra pradāpayet | 
 nāgahemayutaṃ vyoma | samajīrṇaṃ drutaṃ bhavet | 
 abhrakoparasān kṣipraṃ | mukhenaiva caratyayam ||
                    (RA_11.57) 
 tāraṃ vaṅgaṃ ca saṃghṛṣya | rasaṃ tatra pradāpayet | 
 nāgahemayutaṃ vyoma | samajīrṇaṃ drutaṃ bhavet | 
 mukhena carate vyoma | tārakarmaṇi śasyate || (RA_11.58) 
 samukhaṃ nirmukhaṃ vāpi | yatnataś cārayen nabhaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.59) 
 cāraṇāṃ trividhāmevaṃ | kṛtvā garbhadrutiṃ rase | 
 jārayet svedayet piṇḍaṃ | pariṇāmakramais tribhiḥ ||
                    (RA_11.60) 
 paṭvamlakṣāragomūtra- | snuhīkṣīraiḥ pralepitam | 
 bahiś ca baddhaṃ vastreṇa | bhūyo grāsaṃ niveditam | 
 kṣārāranālataileṣu | svedayen mṛdunāgninā || (RA_11.61) 
 krameṇānena deveśi | jāryate divasais tribhiḥ | 
 yantrād uddhṛtamātraṃ tu | lohapātre sthitaṃ rasam ||
                    (RA_11.62) 
 koṣṇena kāñjikenādau | kṣālitaṃ vastragālitam | 
 pātre sukhoṣṇahastena | yāvat śeṣaṃ vimardayet ||
                    (RA_11.63) 
 caturguṇena vastreṇa | pīḍito nirmalaś ca saḥ || (RA_11.64) 
 gālanakriyayā grāse | sati niṣpeṣanirgate | 
 sa bhaveddaṇḍadhārī ca | jīrṇagrāsastathā rasaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.65) 
 ajīrṇe pācayet piṣṭīṃ | svedayen mardayet tathā | 
 vetasāmlaprayogeṇa | jīrṇe grāsaṃ tu dāpayet || (RA_11.66) 
 iṣṭikāguḍadagdhorṇā- | rājīsaindhavadhūmajaiḥ | 
 ṣoḍaśāṃśaiḥ sa dhānyāmlaiḥ | mardyaḥ svedyaś ca pāradaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.67) 
 nirmalīkaraṇārthaṃ tu | grāse grāse punaḥ punaḥ | 
 jīrṇābhro jīrṇabījo 'pi | rāgān gṛhṇāti nirmalaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.68) 
 krameṇānena dolāyāṃ | cāryaṃ grāsacatuṣṭayam | 
 tataḥ kacchapayantreṇa | jvālanaṃ bandhanaṃ kramāt ||
                    (RA_11.69) 
 ūrdhvādhaś cāṣṭamāṃśena | viḍaṃ dattvāpi jārayet | 
 samajīrṇābhrakaḥ sūtaḥ | śatavedhī bhavet priye ||
                    (RA_11.70) 
 sahasravedhī dviguṇe | triguṇe 'yutavedhakaḥ | 
 caturguṇe lakṣavedhī | sa bhavedbhūcaro rasaḥ || (RA_11.71) 
 jīrṇe pañcaguṇe devi | brahmāyurjāyate rasaḥ | 
 āyustu ṣaḍguṇe viṣṇoḥ | koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ || (RA_11.72) 
 rasasya sarvadoṣāstu | ṣaḍguṇenābhrakena tu | 
 jīrṇena nāśamāyānti | nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || (RA_11.73) 
 rasarāje yadā jīrṇaṃ | ṣaḍguṇaṃ gaganaṃ priye | 
 tadā grasati lohāni | tyajec ca gatimātmanaḥ || (RA_11.74) 
 dhūmaś ciṭiciṭiścaiva | maṇḍūkaplutireva ca | 
 sakampaś ca vikampaś ca | pañcāvasthā rasasya tu ||
                    (RA_11.75) 
 kapilo 'tha nirudgāri- | vipluṣaś caiva muñcati | 
 agnau tiṣṭhati niṣkampo | vyomajīrṇasya lakṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_11.76) 
 samajīrṇo bhavedbālo | yauvanasthaścaturguṇam | 
 vṛddhas tu ṣaḍguṇaṃ jīrṇaḥ | kuryāt karma pṛthak pṛthak ||
                    (RA_11.77) 
 bālas tu pattralepena | kalkayogena yauvanaḥ | 
 vṛddho vidhyati lohāni | jāritaḥ sārito 'thavā ||
                    (RA_11.78) 
 kumāras tu raso devi | na samartho rasāyane | 
 yauvanastho raso devi | kṣamo dehasya rakṣaṇe || (RA_11.79) 
 jarāvastho raso yaś ca | dehe lohena saṃkramet | 
 abhāve 'bhrakasattvasya | kāntasattvaṃ pradāpayet ||
                    (RA_11.80) 
 kāntasya cāpyabhāve tu | tīkṣṇalohaṃ tu dāpayet | 
 anena kramayogena | sarvasattvāni jārayet || (RA_11.81) 
 eko 'pi hemasaṃyuktaś | cāmīkarakaraḥ kṣaṇāt | 
 gandhakāt parato nāsti | raseṣūparaseṣu vā || (RA_11.82) 
 pūrvoktayantrayogena | dvir aṣṭaguṇagandhakam | 
 athavā dvādaśaguṇaṃ | ṣaḍguṇaṃ vāpi jārayet || (RA_11.83) 
 mākṣikaṃ sattvamādāya | pādāṃśena tu jārayet | 
 tato 'pi sarvasattvāni | drāvayet sūtagarbhataḥ ||
                    (RA_11.84) 
 hemapāvakayoḥ sakhyaṃ | tathā kāñcanasūtayoḥ | 
 vahnisūtakayor vairaṃ | tayormitreṇa mitratā || (RA_11.85) 
 agniko yavaciñcā ca | vasuhaṭṭaś ca rāgiṇī | 
 dolāsvedena tat pakvaṃ | hemajāraṇamuttamam || (RA_11.86) 
 palāśabhasmāpāmārgo | yavakṣāraś ca kāñjikam | 
 sauvarcalaṃ ca kāsīsaṃ | sāmudraṃ saindhavaṃ tathā ||
                    (RA_11.87) 
 āsurī ṭaṅkaṇaścaiva | navasārastathaiva ca | 
 karpūraścaiva mākṣīkaṃ | samabhāgāni kārayet || (RA_11.88) 
 snuhyarkadugdhair deveśi | mūṣālepaṃ tu kārayet | 
 viḍacūrṇaṃ tato dattvā | kanakaṃ jārayet priye ||
                    (RA_11.89) 
 śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi | bhūcarākhyaṃ tu jāraṇam ||
                    (RA_11.90) 
 kṛṣṇaṃ pītaṃ raktamabhraṃ | śulve tīkṣṇe ca melayet ||
                    (RA_11.91) 
 śulve tīkṣṇaṃ yadā cūrṇaṃ | dvāviṃśatiguṇaṃ priye | 
 gandhanāgaṃ tato 'rdhaṃ tu | krameṇaiva tu melayet ||
                    (RA_11.92) 
 hemnā tu saha dātavyaṃ | sūtakaikena ṣoḍaśa | 
 gandhanāgaṃ yadā jīrṇaṃ | tadā baddho bhavedrasaḥ | 
 hemni jīrṇe tato 'rdhena | mṛtalohena rañjayet ||
                    (RA_11.93) 
 gandhakena hataṃ śulvaṃ | mākṣikaṃ daradāyasam | 
 puṭena mārayec chuddhaṃ | hema dadyāt tu ṣaḍguṇam ||
                    (RA_11.94) 
 sūtake hemabījaṃ ca | yadā jīrṇaṃ caturguṇam | 
 baddharāgaṃ vijānīyāt | hemābho jāyate rasaḥ || (RA_11.95) 
 sāraṇāyantramadhyasthaṃ | tenaiva saha sārayet | 
 tribhāgasāritaṃ kṛtvā | punas tatraiva jārayet ||
                    (RA_11.96) 
 jāritaḥ sāritaścaiva | punarjāritasāritaḥ | 
 saptaśṛṅkhalikāyogāt | koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ || (RA_11.97) 
 bhūcarī jāraṇā proktā | khecarīṃ jāraṇāṃ śṛṇu || (RA_11.98) 
 hīramukhyāni ratnāni | rasocchiṣṭāni kārayet | 
 kaṭutumbasya bījāni | tasyārdhena tu dāpayet || (RA_11.99) 
 mahājāraṇamityuktaṃ | kalkaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ | 
 vajramūṣāmukhe caiva | tanmadhye sthāpayed rasam ||
                    (RA_11.100) 
 katakaṃ kanakaṃ caivam | ekīkṛtya ca mardayet | 
 padmarāgaṃ prayatnena | rase grāsaṃ tu dāpayet ||
                    (RA_11.101) 
 ekādaśaguṇaṃ yāvat | padmarāgaṃ tu sūtake | 
 rāgajīrṇas tu deveśi | liṅgākāro bhavedrasaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.102) 
 rakṣitavyaṃ prayatnena | lokapālāṣṭakena ca | 
 ṣaḍbhāgaṃ sūtakendrasya | teṣu sarveṣu dāpayet ||
                    (RA_11.103) 
 bhakṣitavyaṃ prayatnena | natvā ca gurudevayoḥ | 
 sarvasiddhānnamaskṛtya | devatāś ca viśeṣataḥ ||
                    (RA_11.104) 
 mūrchāṅgadāhaś ca tato | jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ | 
 ātmānamutthitaṃ paśyet | divyatejomahābalam || (RA_11.105) 
 śaṅkhakāhalanirghoṣaiḥ | siddhavidyādharaiḥ saha | 
 icchayā vicarellokān | kāmarūpī vimānagaḥ || (RA_11.106) 
 devāś ca yatra līyante | siddhastatraiva līyate ||
                    (RA_11.107) 
 punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi | jāraṇāyogamuttamam || (RA_11.108) 
 sughṛṣṭaṃ pācitaṃ sūtaṃ | sarvadoṣojjhitaṃ tataḥ | 
 śākapallavasāreṇa | viṣṇukrāntārasena ca || (RA_11.109) 
 palāśapuṣpatoyena | bhāvitaṃ gandhakaṃ samam | 
 samaṃ kṛṣṇābhrasattvaṃ ca | rasakaṃ cāṣṭakaṃ guṇam ||
                    (RA_11.110) 
 tīkṣṇaśulvoragaṃ caiva | kūrmayantreṇa jārayet | 
 kāñcanaṃ jārayet paścāt | viḍayogena pārvati ||
                    (RA_11.111) 
 tataḥ siddhaṃ vijānīyāt | dvaidhaṃ śulvasya dāpayet | 
 karmasaṃkhyāpramāṇena | nāgo bhavati kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_11.112) 
 ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi | jāraṇākramamuttamam ||
                    (RA_11.113) 
 bījacūrṇāni tailena | bhāvayitvā punaḥ punaḥ | 
 ṣoḍaśāṃśena tadgrāsam | aṅgulyā mardayec chanaiḥ ||
                    (RA_11.114) 
 ārdrakādi tato yogād | dātavyaṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśataḥ | 
 bhūrje dattvā tato deyaṃ | dolāyantre vinikṣipet ||
                    (RA_11.115) 
 ahorātreṇa tadbījaṃ | sūtako grasati priye | 
 tamuddhṛtya rasaṃ devi | khalle saṃmardayet tataḥ ||
                    (RA_11.116) 
 tato yantre vinikṣipya | divārātraṃ dṛḍhāgninā | 
 taptaṃ samuddhṛtaṃ yantrāt | taptakhalle vimardayet ||
                    (RA_11.117) 
 mardayitvābhrake piṇḍaṃ | kṣiptvā tatra puṭaṃ dadet | 
 tato garbhe patatyāśu | jārayet tat sukhena tu ||
                    (RA_11.118) 
 dolāyantre tato dattvā | ārdrapiṇḍena saṃyutam | 
 tṛtīye divase sūto | jarate grasate tataḥ || (RA_11.119) 
 samajīrṇaṃ tato yāvat | dolāyantre vicakṣaṇaḥ | 
 paścāt kacchapayantreṇa | samajīrṇaṃ tu pārvati | 
 taṃ grāsadvādaśāṃśena | kacchapena tu jārayet ||
                    (RA_11.120) 
 prāgvadārdrakayogaṃ ca | garbhadrāvaṇameva ca | 
 paścāttaṃ devi nikṣipya | puṭaṃ dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.121) 
 aṣṭāṃśena tato grāsaṃ | garbhadrāvaṃ ca pūrvavat | 
 kandodare sūraṇasya | taṃ vinikṣipya sūtakam | 
 puṭet tu jāritastāvat | yāvat kando na dahyate ||
                    (RA_11.122) 
 pādāṃśena tu mūṣāyā | grāsaḥ sūte vidhīyate | 
 pūrvavac ca viḍaṃ dadyāt | garbhadrāvaṇameva ca ||
                    (RA_11.123) 
 evaṃ caturguṇe jīrṇe | sūtako balavān bhavet | 
 tataḥ śalākayā grāsān | agnistho grasate rasaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.124) 
 tato ratnāni jāryāṇi | vakṣyamāṇakrameṇa tu || (RA_11.125) 
 abhrakaṃ bhrāmakaṃ caiva | śaṅkhanābhiṃ tathaiva ca | 
 rasānuparasān dattvā | mahājāraṇasaṃyutān || (RA_11.126) 
 vajrakandaṃ vajralatā | meṣaśṛṅgyamṛtāyasam | 
 kaṭutumbasya bījāni | mṛtalohāni pācayet || (RA_11.127) 
 sarvāṇi samabhāgāni | śikhiśoṇitamātritam | 
 tāvattaṃ mardayet prājño | yāvat karma dṛḍhaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_11.128) 
 mūṣā vallākṛtiścaiva | kartavyā chādanaiḥ saha | 
 tanmadhye sthāpayet sūtam | adhovātena dhāmayet ||
                    (RA_11.129) 
 ādau tatraiva dātavyaṃ | vajramauṣadhalepitam | 
 gṛhyate ko 'tra saṃdeho | yathā tīvre hutāśane ||
                    (RA_11.130) 
 kuliśena puṭe dagdhe | karṣvagnau tena mardayet | 
 yāvad ekādaśaguṇaṃ | kuliśaṃ jārayet punaḥ || (RA_11.131) 
 sudagdhaśaṅkhanābhiś ca | mātuluṅgarasaplutaḥ | 
 muktāphalaṃ tato deyaṃ | vajrajīrṇe tu sūtake ||
                    (RA_11.132) 
 anena kramayogena | hy ekādaśaguṇaṃ bhavet | 
 kevalaṃ śikhipittaṃ ca | nīlī niryāsamiśritam ||
                    (RA_11.133) 
 nīlotpalāni liptāni | prakṣiptāni tu sūtake | 
 rase kalpenmahārāgān | hīnarāgān parityajet || (RA_11.134) 
 raktāni śikhipittaṃ ca | mahāratnasamanvitam | 
 sadratnaṃ lepayet tena | pradravet rasamadhyataḥ ||
                    (RA_11.135) 
 rajanīṃ caiva kuṣṭhaṃ ca | brahmaniryāsabhāvitam | 
 jāraṇaṃ puṣparāgasya | tenaiva saha dāpayet || (RA_11.136) 
 bahuratneṣu jīrṇeṣu | bhṛṅgarāgeṣu suvrate | 
 rasendro dṛśyate devi | nīlapītāruṇacchaviḥ || (RA_11.137) 
 śuddhāni hemapattrāṇi | śatāṃśena tu lepayet | 
 puṭena mārayed etad | indragopanibhaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_11.138) 
 saṃsparśādvedhayetsarvam | idaṃ hema mṛtaṃ priye | 
 tribhāgaṃ sūtakendrasya | tenaiva saha sārayet ||
                    (RA_11.139) 
 mūṣāmadhyasthite tasmin | punas tenaiva jārayet | 
 dhūmavedhī bhaveddevi | punaḥ sāritajāritaḥ || (RA_11.140) 
 anena kramayogena | yadi jīrṇā triśṛṅkhalā | 
 vedhayen nātra saṃdeho | giripātālabhūtalam || (RA_11.141) 
 pārśvajyotiḥ pradṛśyeta | cordhvaṃ naiva tu dṛśyate | 
 bhūcaraṃ taṃ vijānīyāt | rasendraṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.142) 
 tenāśrāntagatirdevi | yojanānāṃ śataṃ vrajet | 
 divyatejā mahākāyo | divyadṛṣṭirmahābalaḥ || (RA_11.143) 
 sarvarogavinirmukto | jīvedācandratārakam | 
 tasya mūtrapurīṣaṃ tu | sarvalohāni vidhyati ||
                    (RA_11.144) 
 samajīrṇena vajreṇa | hemnā ca sahitena ca | 
 agnistho jārayellohān | bandhamāyāti sūtakaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.145) 
 sārayet tena bījena | sahasram api vedhayet | 
 sāritaṃ jārayet paścāt | lepyaṃ kṣepyaṃ sahasraśaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.146) 
 sārayet tena bījena | lakṣavedhamavāpnuyāt | 
 anena kramayogena | koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ || (RA_11.147) 
 kevalaṃ tu yadā vajraṃ | samajīrṇaṃ tu jārayet | 
 baddhaḥ sūtastadā jñeyo | niṣkampo nirupadravaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.148) 
 agnistho jāyate sūtaḥ | śalākāṃ grasate kṣaṇāt | 
 haṭhāgninā dhāmyamāno | grasate sarvamādarāt ||
                    (RA_11.149) 
 carate jarate sūta | āyurdravyapradāyakaḥ | 
 mūṣāsthaṃ dhamayet sūtaṃ | haṭhāgnau naiva kampate ||
                    (RA_11.150) 
 jārayet sarvaratnāni | baddhaḥ khecaratāṃ nayet | 
 iti lohe 'ṣṭaguṇite | jīrṇe syādrasabandhanam ||
                    (RA_11.151) 
 lohāni sattvaṃ triguṇaṃ | dviguṇaṃ kanakaṃ tathā | 
 dhūmāvalokavedhī syāt | bhavennirvāṇado rasaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.152) 
 ādāv aṣṭaguṇaṃ jāryaṃ | vyomasattvaṃ mahārasam | 
 samaṃ hemadaśāṃśena | vajraratnāni jārayet || (RA_11.153) 
 sarvaṃ ca jārayed vajraṃ | tadāsau khecaro rasaḥ | 
 bhramet pradakṣiṇāvartaḥ | koṭivedhī ca jāyate ||
                    (RA_11.154) 
 same tu pannage jīrṇe | daśavedhī bhavedrasaḥ | 
 dviguṇe śatavedhī syāt | triguṇe tu sahasrakam ||
                    (RA_11.155) 
 caturguṇe 'yutaṃ devi | krameṇānena vardhayet | 
 uttarottaravṛddhyātu | jārayet tatra pannagam ||
                    (RA_11.156) 
 kuṭilaṃ pannagaṃ jāryaṃ | tatra saṃkhyākrameṇa tu | 
 tadvādameti deveśi | koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ || (RA_11.157) 
 ruruṇā dānavendreṇa | bhakṣito bhasmasūtakaḥ | 
 jāritaṃ dvādaśaguṇaṃ | yatra tīkṣṇaṃ sureśvari ||
                    (RA_11.158) 
 bhakṣayitvā palaikaṃ tu | dānavo baladarpitaḥ | 
 jagadutpāṭitaṃ tena | kailāso 'pi ca cūrṇitaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.159) 
 tatra mayā kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā | dṛṣṭvā tanmāyayā kṛtam | 
 jāritaṃ pannage sūtaṃ | samāṃśaṃ śilayā hatam ||
                    (RA_11.160) 
 tena sūtena saṃliptaṃ | triśūlaṃ himaśailaje | 
 tena śūlena nihato | dānavo baladarpitaḥ || (RA_11.161) 
 hema śulvaṃ tathā tīkṣṇaṃ | vājaraṃ ca paḍālakam | 
 rohaṇaṃ kāntalohaṃ ca | jārayet tattvasaṃkhyayā ||
                    (RA_11.162) 
 ekaike rasarājo 'yaṃ | baddhaḥ khecaratāṃ nayet | 
 gandhanāge drute devi | jāraṇāṃ sukarāṃ śṛṇu ||
                    (RA_11.163) 
 ādau saṃśodhitaṃ sūtaṃ | rajanīcūrṇasaṃyutam | 
 mardayed yāvad ākṛṣṇaṃ | kṣālayed uṣṇakāñjikaiḥ ||
                    (RA_11.164) 
 evaṃ muhurmuhurghṛṣṭo | gandhanāgo drutiṃ caret ||
                    (RA_11.165) 
 nāgasya mūtre deveśi | vatsasya mahiṣasya vā | 
 āvartyāvartya bhujagaṃ | sapta vārān niṣecayet ||
                    (RA_11.166) 
 kṛtvā kaṇṭakavedhyāni | tasya pattrāṇi sundari | 
 caturthāṃśapramāṇena | gandhakasya tu yojayet ||
                    (RA_11.167) 
 prasārya lākṣāpaṭalaṃ | romāṇi tadanantaram | 
 ūrdhvaṃ gandhakacūrṇaṃ ca | tato nāgadalaṃ tathā ||
                    (RA_11.168) 
 gandhakaṃ naralomāni | lākṣāyāḥ paṭalaṃ kramāt | 
 ūrdhvaṃ prasārya saṃsthāpya | sūtrair vartiṃ tu kārayet ||
                    (RA_11.169) 
 karañjatailamadhye tu | daśarātraṃ nidhāpayet | 
 dīptāgrabhāgāṃ tāṃ vartiṃ | saṇḍaśyā tu vidhārayet ||
                    (RA_11.170) 
 tāṃ drutiṃ pātayetpātre | sauvīraṭaṅkaṇānvite | 
 kācakūpyāś ca madhye tu | tattailaṃ sthāpayet priye ||
                    (RA_11.171) 
 kṛtvā gostanamūṣāyāṃ | liptāyāṃ śilayā rasam | 
 catuḥṣaṣṭyādibhāgena | jñātvā devi balābalam ||
                    (RA_11.172) 
 gandhanāgadrutiṃ dattvā | tāṃ mūṣāṃ suravandite | 
 garte gomayasampūrṇe | vinyasya puṭapācanam | 
 dadyāt karīṣatuṣayoḥ | prasṛtidvitayena ca || (RA_11.173) 
 dadyādajīrṇaśaṅkāyāṃ | siṃhavallīrasasya tu | 
 caturbindūn puṭe prāgvad | evaṃ pratidinaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_11.174) 
 jāraṇātriguṇāt sūto | bhavejjambūphalaprabhaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.175) 
 mākṣikaṃ sattvamalpālpaṃ | mṛtanāgasamanvitam | 
 mūṣāgataṃ bhavedyāvat | kācaṃ dattvādharottaram | 
 evaṃ dvādaśavārāṃstu | sudhmātaṃ rañjitaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_11.176) 
 tena pakvaṃ bījacūrṇaṃ | pārade pādabhāgikam | 
 marditaṃ caṇakāmlena | kṣaṇādgarbhadrutirbhavet ||
                    (RA_11.177) 
 garbhadrutirna ceddevi | varṇikādvayagandhayoḥ | 
 raktasindhūdbhavālarka- | ṭaṅkaṇāśugapuṅkhataḥ | 
 kalkena liptaṃ puṭitaṃ | bījaṃ garbhe drutaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_11.178) 
 bīje pādārdhatulyāṃśe | jīrṇe vedhaṃ karoti saḥ | 
 daśaṣoḍaśabhāgena | dvāviṃśāṃśena ca kramāt || (RA_11.179) 
 saṃyojya triguṇāṃ rītiṃ | tāre tārāvaśeṣitaiḥ | 
 tārāriṣṭamidaṃ liptvā | tena sūtena vedhayet ||
                    (RA_11.180) 
 ataḥ paraṃ tu saṃskāraṃ | vakṣye nāgābhrajāraṇam | 
 karavīrāruṇāṃ devi | cūrṇayitvā manaḥśilām || (RA_11.181) 
 bhāvayed viṃśatiṃ vārān | yavaciñcārasena tu | 
 tena kalkena saṃlipya | nāgapattraṃ prayatnataḥ | 
 karṣvanalena vipacet | yāvattat cūrṇitaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_11.182) 
 rasakasya ca bhāgāṃs trīn | bhāgaikaṃ daradasya ca | 
 peṣayen mātuluṅgena | pādagandhaṃ śilāviṣam || (RA_11.183) 
 kalkenānena liptāyāṃ | mūṣāyāṃ puṭapācitam | 
 taṃ nāgaṃ dhamayed evaṃ | saptadhā hemavadbhavet ||
                    (RA_11.184) 
 pītābhrakaṃ tv ekadalaṃ | liptāyāṃ maricena tu | 
 mūṣāyāṃ dhmātamagnyābhaṃ | saubhāñjanarase kṣipet ||
                    (RA_11.185) 
 pātayetpūrvavidhinā | tat sattvaṃ hemabhāsuram ||
                    (RA_11.186) 
 pattraṃ rañjitanāgasya | sattvaṃ pītābhrakasya ca | 
 strīstanyakācadhūmottha- | guñjāyaskāntaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ | 
 tutthena saṃyutenaitan | nāgābhraṃ dvaṃdvitaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_11.187) 
 kiṃvāranālasiddhārtha- | dhūmasāreṣṭakāguḍaiḥ | 
 mardayet tridinaṃ sūtaṃ | dolāyāṃ svedayet tryaham ||
                    (RA_11.188) 
 punarnavāmeṣaśṛṅgī- | sarpākṣīkalkasaṃyutam | 
 athāsurī sindhuviṣaṃ | maricaiḥ paripeṣitaiḥ | 
 dolāyantre punarapi | svedayed divasatrayam || (RA_11.189) 
 aṣṭamāṃśena nāgābhraṃ | cārayitvā sureśvari | 
 śilābhāgadvayaṃ caikaṃ | sindhusauvarcalaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_11.190) 
 ṭaṅkārdhaṃ viṣapādaṃ ca | viḍaḥ piṇḍāṣṭamāṃśataḥ | 
 tridine kacchape jāryam | evaṃ jāryaṃ tu ṣaḍguṇam ||
                    (RA_11.191) 
 śailaṃ tutthoragaṃ tāmraṃ | tīkṣṇaghoṣārakāñcanam | 
 kramavṛddham idaṃ tutthaṃ | tāpyasattvanipātanāt ||
                    (RA_11.192) 
 hemāvaśeṣaṃ tadbījaṃ | pādāṃśaṃ mātulāmbhasā | 
 cārayed rasarājasya | jārayet kanakānvitaiḥ || (RA_11.193) 
 tāpyasauvarcalaśilā- | gandhakāsīsaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ | 
 padmayantre niveśyātha | kīlaṃ dattvā sureśvari ||
                    (RA_11.194) 
 dhameddinatrayaṃ mandaṃ | yāvad bījaṃ drutaṃ bhavet | 
 tameva samajīrṇaṃ tu | vahnau niṣkampanaṃ rasam ||
                    (RA_11.195) 
 tataḥ ṣaḍguṇabījena | sāraṇā kramayogataḥ | 
 tārāriṣṭamahiṃ śulbaṃ | sahasrāṃśena vedhayet ||
                    (RA_11.196) 
 viṣagandhakatāpyābhra- | kākaviṣṭhā ghanadhvaniḥ | 
 sahadevīvahniśikhā- | kalkena kramate rasaḥ || (RA_11.197) 
 mūrchito mṛtasūtaś ca | jalūkābandha eva ca | 
 caturtho mūrtibandhas tu | paṭṭabandhas tu pañcamaḥ | 
 bhasmasūtaś ca khoṭaś ca | saṃskārāt saptadhā rasaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.198) 
 nāgavarṇaṃ bhavet sūtaṃ | vihāya ghanacāpalam | 
 lakṣaṇaṃ dṛśyate yasya | mūrchitaṃ taṃ vadanti hi ||
                    (RA_11.199) 
 ārdratvaṃ ca ghanatvaṃ ca | tejogauravacāpalam | 
 yasyaitāni na dṛśyante | taṃ vidyānmṛtasūtakam ||
                    (RA_11.200) 
 nānāvarṇaṃ tathā svacchaṃ | drutaṃ yonau jalūkavat | 
 badhyate sūtakaṃ yac ca | jalūkābandhalakṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_11.201) 
 gurutvamaruṇatvaṃ ca | tejasā sūryasaṃnibham | 
 śikhimadhye dhṛtaṃ tiṣṭhet | mūrtibandhasya lakṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_11.202) 
 śalākājāraṇādvāpi | mūrtibandhatvamiṣyate || (RA_11.203) 
 śvetaṃ pītaṃ guru tathā | mṛdu sikthakasaṃnibham | 
 agnimadhye yadā tiṣṭhet | paṭṭabandhasya lakṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_11.204) 
 kṛṣṇaṃ śvetaṃ tathā pītaṃ | nīlaṃ bhasmanibhaṃ tathā | 
 capalatvaṃ yadā naṣṭaṃ | bhasmasūtasya lakṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_11.205) 
 kukkuṭāṇḍanibhaṃ sūtaṃ | yadā lavaṇabhedi ca | 
 āvartate rasastadvat | khoṭakasya ca lakṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_11.206) 
 athavā chedane snigdhaṃ | raśminā mṛdunā dravet | 
 akṣayaṃ kaṭhinaṃ śvetaṃ | khoṭabandhasya lakṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_11.207) 
 khoṭādayas tu ye pañca | vihāya jalukākṛti | 
 haṭhāgnau dhāmitāḥ santi | na tiṣṭhatyeva mūrchitaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.208) 
 taruṇādityasaṃkāśo | nānāvarṇaḥ sureśvari | 
 vedhayed dehalohāni | rañjito rasabhairavaḥ || (RA_11.209) 
 śodhanaṃ sūtakasyādau | grāsamānamataḥ param | 
 jāraṇaṃ vyomasattvasya | sarvasattvasya jāraṇam ||
                    (RA_11.210) 
 garbhabāhyadrutiḥ paścāt | suvarṇasya tu jāraṇam | 
 divyauṣadhipuṭaḥ paścāt | ratnabandhamataḥ param ||
                    (RA_11.211) 
 rañjanaṃ ca tato devi | jāraṇā cānusāraṇā | 
 krāmaṇaṃ ca tato deyaṃ | sūtakasya vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||
                    (RA_11.212) 
 evaṃ kramaṃ tu yo vetti | tasya siddhirna saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.213) 
 vedhakaṃ yas tu jānāti | dehe lohe rasāyane | 
 tasya janma jarā vyādhir | naśyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.214) 
 dehe tu pañcaratnāni | nāgaṃ vaṅgaṃ tathāyasam | 
 krāmaṇaṃ rasarājasya | bheṣajaṃ vyādhināśanam ||
                    (RA_11.215) 
 auṣadhaiḥ kramate sūto | yogaśaktikrameṇa tu | 
 kramate vyādhisaṃghāte | grasate duṣṭamāmayam ||
                    (RA_11.216) 
 tasya tu krāmaṇaṃ jñātvā | tato vaidyair upācaret | 
 krāmaṇena vinā sūto | na kramet na ca vedhayet | 
 dehalohāmayān sarvān | vṛthā syāt kevalaṃ śramaḥ ||
                    (RA_11.217) 
 yasya rogasya yo yogas | tenaiva saha yojayet | 
 rasendro harati vyādhīn | narakuñjaravājinām ||
                    (RA_11.218) 
 āroṭo balamādhatte | mūrchito vyādhināśanaḥ | 
 baddhena khecarīsiddhiḥ | māritenājarāmaraḥ || (RA_11.219) 
 viśeṣādvyādhiśamano | gandhakena tu mūrchitaḥ | 
 oṣadhyā ghātitaḥ sūto | yathā bhūyo na jīvati ||
                    (RA_11.220) 
 sahi krāmati loheṣu | tena kuryādrasāyanam | 
 tan mam ācakṣva deveśi | kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||
                    (RA_11.221) 
 
 

                12


                  śrīdevyuvāca 
 oṣadhī kīdṛśī nātha | rasamūrchākarī śubhā | 
 kena vā bhasmasūtaḥ syāt | kena vā khoṭabandhanam ||
                    (RA_12.1) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 śṛṇu bhairavi yatnena | rahasyaṃ rasabandhanam | 
 brahmaviṣṇusurendrādyair | na jñātaṃ vīravandite ||
                    (RA_12.2) 
 gaṅgāyamunayor madhye | prayogo nāma rākṣasaḥ | 
 tasyāsanne varārohe | kṣaṇād badhyeta sūtakaḥ || (RA_12.3) 
 niśācarasya pattrāṇi | gṛhṇīyāt sādhakottamaḥ | 
 adho niṣpīḍitaṃ devi | raso bhavati cottamaḥ || (RA_12.4) 
 rasaṃ saṃmardya tenaiva | dināni trīṇi vārttikaḥ | 
 āroṭaṃ bandhayet kṣipraṃ | gaganaṃ tatra jārayet ||
                    (RA_12.5) 
 tena pattrarasenaiva | sādhayed gaganaṃ punaḥ | 
 saptadhā bhāvitaṃ tena | tryūṣaṇena sahaikataḥ | 
 yantre vidyādhare devi | gaganaṃ tatra jārayet || (RA_12.6) 
 māsamātreṇa deveśi | jīryate tat samaṃ same | 
 samajīrṇe rase devi | śatavedhī bhavedrasaḥ || (RA_12.7) 
 niśācararase devi | gandhakaṃ bhāvayet tataḥ | 
 bhāvayet saptavāraṃ tu | dvipadyāś ca rasena tu || (RA_12.8) 
 tārasya pattralepena | ardhārdhakāñcanottamam | 
 gandhake samajīrṇe 'smin | śatavedhī raso bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.9) 
 punas taṃ gandhakaṃ dattvā | pattralepe raviṃ haret | 
 taṃ raviṃ tāramadhye tu | triguṇaṃ vāhayet tataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.10) 
 hemārdhe militaṃ hema | mātṛkāsamatāṃ vrajet | 
 punas taṃ gandhakaṃ sākṣād | drāvayitvā drutaṃ kuru ||
                    (RA_12.11) 
 rasendraṃ mardayet tena | gatadehaṃ tu kārayet | 
 lepamātreṇa tenaiva | kuṣṭhānaṣṭādaśa priye | 
 arśo bhagaṃdaraṃ lūtāṃ | śirorogāṃś ca nāśayet ||
                    (RA_12.12) 
 niśācararase bhāvyaṃ | saptavāraṃ tu tālakam | 
 tenaiva ghātayed vaṅgaṃ | vaṅgaṃ tāre tu nirvahet ||
                    (RA_12.13) 
 taṃ tāraṃ jārayet sūte | tatsūtaṃ bandhanaṃ vrajet | 
 lepamātreṇa tenaiva | catuḥṣaṣṭitamo bhavet || (RA_12.14) 
 catuḥṣaṣṭitame bhāge | śulvavedhaṃ tu dāpayet | 
 śulvaṃ tu dāpayet tāre | tattāraṃ kāñcanaṃ bhavet | 
 tattāraṃ jāyate śreṣṭhaṃ | dharmakāmārthamokṣadam ||
                    (RA_12.15) 
 niśācarasya puṣpāṇi | sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet | 
 palāni daśa cūrṇasya | rasair dhātryāstu bhāvayet ||
                    (RA_12.16) 
 ghṛtena madhunāloḍya | navabhāṇḍe vinikṣipet | 
 dhānyarāśau nidhātavyaṃ | trisaptāhaṃ sureśvari ||
                    (RA_12.17) 
 tena bhakṣitamātreṇa | valīpalitavarjitaḥ || (RA_12.18) 
 valkalaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tu | madhunā sahitaṃ lihet | 
 ardhamāsaprayogeṇa | pratyakṣo 'yaṃ bhavet priye ||
                    (RA_12.19) 
 tasya mūtrapurīṣeṇa | śulvaṃ bhavati kāñcanam | 
 māsamātraprayogeṇa | pannagaḥ kāñcanaṃ bhavet || (RA_12.20) 
 grāhyaṃ tatphalatailaṃ vā | yantre pātālasaṃjñake | 
 tena tailena deveśi | rasaṃ saṃkocayed budhaḥ || (RA_12.21) 
 tatkṣaṇājjāyate devi | paṭṭabaddho mahārasaḥ || (RA_12.22) 
 kaṭukaṃ kaṅkaṇaṃ kāryaṃ | rasaliṅge varānane | 
 saṃkocya māraṇaṃ tena | kartavyaṃ paramādbhutam ||
                    (RA_12.23) 
 niśācararase kṣiptaṃ | saptavāraṃ tu bhāskaram | 
 kālikārahitaṃ tena | jāyate kanakaprabham || (RA_12.24) 
 tattāreṇa samaṃ bāhyaṃ | tena siktaṃ tu vāpitam | 
 daśāṃśaṃ vedhayet sūtaṃ | daśa pītaṃ śatena ca ||
                    (RA_12.25) 
 śataṃ vedhayate lakṣaṃ | sahasraṃ koṭivedhakam | 
 daśāṃśaṃ koṭivedhi syāt | koṭivedhi samena ca || (RA_12.26) 
 punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham ||
                    (RA_12.27) 
 trailokyajananī yā syād | oṣadhī ajanāyikā | 
 tasyāḥ samparkamātreṇa | baddhastiṣṭhati pāradaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.28) 
 saptāhaṃ marditastasyā | mahauṣadhyā rasena saḥ | 
 śatāṃśenaiva vedhena | kurute divyakāñcanam || (RA_12.29) 
 dvisaptāhaṃ rase tasyā | mardanādvaravarṇini | 
 lakṣavedhī rasaḥ sākṣād | aṣṭau lohāni kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.30) 
 trisaptāhena deveśi | daśalakṣāṇi vidhyati | 
 caturthe caiva saptāhe | koṭivedhī mahārasaḥ || (RA_12.31) 
 svedatāpananighṛṣṭo | mahauṣadhyā rasena tu | 
 dadāti khecarīṃ siddhim | anivāritagocaraḥ || (RA_12.32) 
 kāmayet kāminīnāṃ tu | sahasraṃ divasāntare | 
 naṣṭacchāyo hy adṛśyaś ca | trailokyaṃ ca bhramedrasaiḥ ||
                    (RA_12.33) 
 mahauṣadhyā rasenaiva | mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ bhavet | 
 anena ghātayet sūtaṃ | pañcāvasthaṃ kuru priye ||
                    (RA_12.34) 
 mṛtasya dāpayen nasyaṃ | hastapādau tu mardayet | 
 tasya tu praviśejjīvo | mṛtasyāpi varānane || (RA_12.35) 
 punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham | 
 narasārarasenaiva | kṣaṇād badhyeta sūtakaḥ || (RA_12.36) 
 narasārarasaṃ dattvā | dvipadīrajasā saha | 
 dinānte bandhamāyāti | sarvalohāni rañjayet || (RA_12.37) 
 narasārarasenaiva | jīrṇe ṣaḍguṇapannage | 
 tāre tāmre 'pi vā devi | bhāvayet taṃ manaḥśilām ||
                    (RA_12.38) 
 nirgandhā jāyate sā tu | ghātayet tadrasāyanam | 
 dvipadīrajasā sārdhaṃ | niḥsattvaḥ pannago bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.39) 
 narasārarasenaiva | jīrṇe ṣaḍguṇapannage | 
 tāre tāmre 'pi vā devi | koṭivedhī bhavedrasaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.40) 
 narasārarasastanye | bhāvanāḥ saptadhā pṛthak | 
 rasendraṃ dāpayed grāsaṃ | yantre vidyādharāhvaye ||
                    (RA_12.41) 
 jīryate gaganaṃ devi | nirmukhaṃ ca varānane | 
 narasārarasenaiva | kīṭamārīrasena ca | 
 drāvayed gaganaṃ devi | tīkṣṇaṃ lohaṃ ca pannagam ||
                    (RA_12.42) 
 narasārarasenaiva | hanūmatyā rasena ca | 
 jāyate kāñcanaṃ divyaṃ | niṣekād bhāskarapriye ||
                    (RA_12.43) 
 narasārarase dattvā | mañjiṣṭhāraktacandanam | 
 svarase mardayet paścāt | pannagaṃ devi secayet ||
                    (RA_12.44) 
 tatkṣaṇāt kāñcanaṃ divyaṃ | saptavāraṃ niṣecitam | 
 ravighṛṣṭaṃ tu taṃ devi | pannagaṃ triguṇaṃ priye ||
                    (RA_12.45) 
 tacchulvaṃ hemasaṃkāśaṃ | tārapañcāṃśayojitam | 
 aṣṭamāṃśayutaṃ hema | hemakarmaṇi cauṣadham || (RA_12.46) 
 narasārarase bhāvyaṃ | saptavāraṃ tu hiṅgulam | 
 tenaiva ghātayet tīkṣṇaṃ | bhasmībhūtatvamādiśet ||
                    (RA_12.47) 
 tadbhasma tāmrapiṣṭaṃ tu | triguṇaṃ tena nirvahet ||
                    (RA_12.48) 
 tacchulvaṃ hemasaṃkāśaṃ | tāramaṣṭāṃśayojitam | 
 tārahema samāṃśaṃ tu | dviguṇaṃ pittalaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.49) 
 narasārarase bhāvyaṃ | rasakaṃ saptavārataḥ | 
 taṃ rasaṃ rasakaṃ caiva | tīkṣṇaṃ lohaṃ ca pannagam ||
                    (RA_12.50:1) 
 narasārarasenaiva | tenaivaikatra mardayet | 
 tatkṣaṇājjāyate bandho | rasasya rasakasya ca ||
                    (RA_12.50:2) 
 tīkṣṇaṃ nāgaṃ tathā śulvaṃ | rasakena tu rañjayet | 
 samastaṃ jāyate hema | kūṣmāṇḍakusumaprabham || (RA_12.51) 
 punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham ||
                    (RA_12.52) 
 kaṅkālakhecarī nāma | oṣadhī parameśvari | 
 tasyāstailaṃ tu saṃgṛhya | māghakhecarisaṃyutam | 
 bhāvayet dinamekaṃ tu | pātre bhāskaranirmite || (RA_12.53) 
 dvitīye vāsare prāpte | vajraratnaṃ tu ghātayet | 
 anale dhāmayet tat tu | sutaptajvalanaprabham || (RA_12.54) 
 kaṅkālakhecarītaile | vajraratnaṃ niṣecayet | 
 daśavāraṃ niṣiktaṃ tu | bhasmākāraṃ hi jāyate || (RA_12.55) 
 taddhemapakvabījaṃ tu | tena bhasmasamaṃ kuru | 
 tribhāgaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ dattvā | andhamūṣāgataṃ dhamet | 
 tatkṣaṇānmilati dvaṃdvaṃ | vajraratnaṃ ca kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.56) 
 candrahema varārohe | samaṃ jārayate yadi | 
 koṭivedhī raso devi | lohānyaṣṭau ca vidhyati || (RA_12.57) 
 punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham ||
                    (RA_12.58) 
 sabījā cauṣadhī grāhyā | kācid gulmalatā priye | 
 mantrasiṃhāsanī nāma | dvitīyā devi khecarī | 
 pātālayantre tattailaṃ | gṛhṇīyāttāmrabhājane || (RA_12.59) 
 tasya tailasya madhye tu | prakṣipet khecarīrasam | 
 medinīyantramadhye tu | sthāpayet tu varānane || (RA_12.60) 
 pūrvauṣadhyā tu taddevi | gaganaṃ medinītale | 
 rasagrāsaṃ tato dattvā | mardanādgolakaṃ kuru || (RA_12.61) 
 baddhvā poṭalikāṃ tena | gaganaṃ tena jārayet | 
 same tu gagane jīrṇe | baddhastiṣṭhati sūtakaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.62) 
 bhastrāphūtkārayuktena | dhāmyamānena naśyati | 
 kākaviṣṭhāsamaṃ rūpaṃ | samajīrṇasya jāyate || (RA_12.63) 
 dviguṇe gagane jīrṇe | aṣṭau lohāni saṃharet || (RA_12.64) 
 punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabandhaṃ sudurlabham ||
                    (RA_12.65) 
 śivadehāt samutpannā | oṣadhī turasiṃhanī | 
 jārayed gandhakaṃ sā tu | jārayet sāpi tālakam ||
                    (RA_12.66) 
 kāñcanaṃ jārayet sāpi | rasendraṃ sā ca baddhayet | 
 pravālaṃ jārayet sā tu | gaganaṃ drāvayet tathā | 
 vajraṃ ca ghātayet sā tu | sarvasattvaṃ ca pātayet ||
                    (RA_12.67) 
 jārayetsarvalohāni | sattvānyapi ca pācayet | 
 harīṃdarīrase nyasya | gośṛṅge tu varānane | 
 dhānyarāśau nidhātavyaṃ | mṛtaṃ tiṣṭhati sūtakam ||
                    (RA_12.68) 
 divyauṣadhyā rasenaiva | rasendraḥ suravandite | 
 same tu kanake jīrṇe | daśakoṭīstu vedhayet || (RA_12.69) 
 pañcame lakṣakoṭistu | ṣaḍguṇe sparśavedhakaḥ | 
 saptame dhūmavedhī syāt | aṣṭame tv avalokataḥ | 
 navame śabdavedhī syād | ata ūrdhvaṃ na vidyate ||
                    (RA_12.70) 
 bhramanti paśavo mūḍhāḥ | kulauṣadhivivarjitāḥ | 
 tṛṇauṣadhirasānāṃ ca | naiva siddhiḥ prajāyate ||
                    (RA_12.71) 
 tasmāt sarvaprayatnena | jñātavyā tu kulauṣadhī ||
                    (RA_12.72) 
 divyauṣadhī catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ | kulamadhye vyavasthitā | 
 naiva jānanti mūḍhāste | devamohena mohitāḥ || (RA_12.73) 
 adivyāstu tṛṇauṣadhyo | jāyante girigahvare || (RA_12.74) 
 tṛṇauṣadhyā rase sūtaṃ | naiva baddhaṃ kadācana | 
 akṣayaṃ ca varārohe | vahnimadhye na tiṣṭhati || (RA_12.75) 
 na khoṭo na ca vā bhasma | naiva dravyaṃ karoti saḥ | 
 kiṃ tat dravyaṃ prakurvīta | dhāmyamāno na tiṣṭhati ||
                    (RA_12.76) 
 pattre pāke kaṭe chede | naiva tiṣṭhati kāñcane | 
 na vedhaṃ ca śatād ūrdhvaṃ | karoti sa rasaḥ priye ||
                    (RA_12.77) 
 yāvanna baddhamekaṃ tu | vikrītaṃ tat tu kāñcanam | 
 dharmārthakāmamokṣārthaṃ | naiva dadyāt tu tat priye ||
                    (RA_12.78) 
  śrīdevyuvāca 
 nirjīvatvaṃ gataḥ sūtaḥ | kathaṃ jīvaṃ dadāti ca | 
 nirjīvena tu nirjīvaḥ | kathaṃ jīvati śaṃkara || (RA_12.79) 
  śrībhairava uvāca 
 divyauṣadhyā yadā devi | rasendro mūrchito bhavet | 
 kālikārahitaḥ sūtas | tadā bhavati pārvati || (RA_12.80) 
 parasya harate kālaṃ | kālikārahito rasaḥ | 
 aṣṭānāṃ caiva lohānāṃ | malaṃ śamayati kṣaṇāt || (RA_12.81) 
 mahāmūrchāgataṃ sūtaṃ | ko vāpi kathayen mṛtam | 
 divyauṣadhyā rasenaiva | jāyate naṣṭacetanaḥ || (RA_12.82) 
 pañcabhūtātmakaḥ sūtas | tiṣṭhatyeva sadāśivaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.83) 
 punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabandhanamīśvari || (RA_12.84) 
 kṣmāpālena hataṃ vajram | anenaiva tu kāñcanam | 
 vajrabhasma hemabhasma | tadvai ekatra bandhayet ||
                    (RA_12.85) 
 niśācararase jāryaṃ | narajīvena jārayet | 
 taṃ sūtaṃ mārayed bhadre | gajāridivyakauṣadhī ||
                    (RA_12.86) 
 bhakṣitaḥ sa raso yena | so 'pi sākṣāt sadāśivaḥ | 
 bhakṣite tolakaikena | sparśavedhī bhavennaraḥ ||
                    (RA_12.87) 
 prasvedāttasya gātrasya | rasarājaś ca vedhyate | 
 prasvedādapi mūtreṇa | aṣṭau lohāni kāñcanam || (RA_12.88) 
 lakṣavarṣasahasrāṇi | sa jīvet sādhakottamaḥ | 
 prajāpatiḥ kṛṣṇatejāḥ | kṣaṇādbadhnāti sūtakam ||
                    (RA_12.89) 
 gajārisparśanāddevi | kṣmāpālena ca badhyate || (RA_12.90) 
 vajravallīrasenaiva | bhāvitaṃ gaganaṃ priye | 
 jārayed vālukāyantre | khoṭo bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.91) 
 mṛtagolakamāṣaikaṃ | māṣaikaṃ hemagolakam | 
 ekīkṛtya tu saṃmardya | luṅgāmlena dinatrayam | 
 karṣaikaṃ nāgapattrāṇi | rasakalkena lepayet || (RA_12.92) 
 veṣṭayed vṛścikālyā ca | tatpiṇḍaṃ lepayet tataḥ | 
 mārayet pannagaṃ devi | śakragopanibhaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.93) 
 karṣaikaṃ tārapattrāṇi | mṛtanāgena lepayet | 
 vṛścikālyā ca tat pattraṃ | lepitaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.94) 
 tattāraṃ mriyate devi | sindūrāruṇasaṃnibham | 
 sahasrāṃśena tenaiva | śulbavedhaṃ pradāpayet || (RA_12.95) 
 jāyate kanakaṃ divyaṃ | devābharaṇabhūṣaṇam || (RA_12.96) 
 kṣīrayuktā bahuphalā | granthiyuktā ca pārvati | 
 nāmnā caṭulaparṇīti | śasyate rasabandhane || (RA_12.97) 
 ekavīrākandarase | mūkamūṣāgataṃ rasam | 
 dhamenmukhānilair baddho | bhakṣaṇāya praśasyate ||
                    (RA_12.98) 
 raktakañcukikandaṃ tu | strīstanyena tu peṣitam | 
 mūṣāyāṃ pūrvayogena | kurute rasabandhanam || (RA_12.99) 
 vṛścikāpattrikābījaṃ | nārīkṣīrasamanvitam | 
 dhamayet pūrvavat sūtaṃ | bhakṣaṇārthāya vārttikaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.100) 
 vajrakandaṃ samādāya | rasamadhye vinikṣipet | 
 gajendrākhyaṃ puṭaṃ dattvā | saptadhā baddhatāṃ nayet ||
                    (RA_12.101) 
 bhakṣayet taṃ rasaṃ prājñaḥ | ṣaṇmāsādamaro bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.102) 
 lāṅgalīkandamādāya | karkoṭīkandameva ca | 
 rasaṃ tanmadhyagaṃ kṛtvā | svedayen mardayetpunaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.103) 
 mriyate nātra saṃdeho | dhmātastīvrānalena tu | 
 śukacañcugataṃ sūtaṃ | puṭayed dhāmayet tataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.104) 
 śatāṃśaṃ vedhakartāyaṃ | dehasiddhikaro bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.105) 
 haṃsapādīrasaṃ sūtaṃ | śūkakandodare kṣipet | 
 gajendrapuṭanaṃ dadyāt | mriyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.106) 
 haṃsāṅghriṃ śukatuṇḍīṃ ca | gṛhītvā mardayed rasam | 
 krauñcapādodare dattvā | tato dadyāt puṭatrayam ||
                    (RA_12.107) 
 mriyate nātra saṃdeho | lakṣavedhī mahārasaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.108) 
 tṛṇajyotiriti khyātā | śṛṇu divyauṣadhī priye | 
 niśāsu prajvalennityaṃ | nāhni jvalati pārvati | 
 tasyā mūle tu nikṣiptaṃ | kṣīraṃ raktaṃ bhavet priye ||
                    (RA_12.109) 
 tanmūlarasagandhābhrair | mātuluṅgāmlapeṣitaiḥ | 
 śulbapattraṃ viliptaṃ tu | bhaveddhema puṭatrayāt ||
                    (RA_12.110) 
 tanmūlacūrṇasaṃyukto | rasarājaḥ sureśvari | 
 mātuluṅgarase ghṛṣṭam | abhrakaṃ carati kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.111) 
 athoccaṭīṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabandhakarīṃ priye | 
 ekameva bhavennālaṃ | tasya roma tu veṣṭanam ||
                    (RA_12.112) 
 tasyāgre ca bhavet puṣpaṃ | śukatuṇḍasya saṃnibham | 
 tatpattrāṇi ca deveśi | śukapicchanibhāni ca | 
 tatkandaṃ kuṣṭhasaṃsthānaṃ | kṣīraṃ sindūrasaṃnibham ||
                    (RA_12.113) 
 jalaṃ sravenmadhūcchiṣṭaṃ | tatsamādāya pārvati | 
 vedhayet sarvalohāni | kāñcanāni bhavanti ca ||
                    (RA_12.114) 
 rasatālakatutthāni | mardayed uccaṭīrasaiḥ | 
 ātape mriyate tapto | raso divyauṣadhībalāt || (RA_12.115) 
 vedhayet sapta lohāni | lakṣāṃśena varānane || (RA_12.116) 
 atha raktasnuhīkalpaṃ | vakṣyāmi surasundari | 
 snuhīkṣīreṇa śulbasya | pattralepaṃ tu kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.117) 
 kṣīreṇa tāpayed bhūyaḥ | saptavāraṃ varānane | 
 āvartitaṃ bhaved yāvaj | jāmbūnadasamaprabham ||
                    (RA_12.118) 
 athātastilatailena | pācayec ca dinatrayam | 
 tathā śulvasya pattrāṇi | vedhyaṃ jāmbunadaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.119:1) 
 rasaṃ raktasnuhīkṣīraṃ | kunaṭīṃ gandhakābhrakam | 
 daradaṃ caiva lohāni | sahasrāṃśena vedhayet ||
                    (RA_12.119:2) 
 snuhīkṣīraṃ samādāya | niśārdhaṃ hema cobhayam | 
 kunaṭīṃ gandhacūrṇaṃ ca | sarvamekatra mardayet ||
                    (RA_12.120) 
 anenaiva prakāreṇa | niśārdhaṃ hema śodhayet | 
 guṭikākṛtya tenaiva | nāgaṃ vidhyati tatkṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.121) 
 athātaḥ sthalapadminyā | divyauṣadhyā vidhiṃ śṛṇu ||
                    (RA_12.122) 
 padminīsadṛśī pattraiḥ | puṣpair api ca tādṛśī | 
 bhaṅge caiva bhavet kṣīraṃ | raktavarṇaṃ suśobhanam ||
                    (RA_12.123) 
 ākramya vāmapādena | paśyed gaganamaṇḍalam | 
 paśyec ca tārakāyuktaṃ | grahanakṣatramaṇḍalam | 
 lakṣayojanato devi | sā jñeyā sthalapadminī || (RA_12.124) 
 tasyāḥ pañcāṅgamādāya | haragaurīsamanvitam | 
 manaḥśilātālayuktaṃ | mākṣikeṇa samanvitam || (RA_12.125) 
 mardayet saptarātraṃ tu | tena śulvaṃ ca vedhayet | 
 sahasrāṃśena deveśi | viddhaṃ bhavati kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.126) 
 tasyāḥ pañcāṅgamādāya | pūrvoktavidhinā priye | 
 cārayet sūtarājaṃ tu | mūkamūṣāgataṃ dhamet || (RA_12.127) 
 mriyate mūṣikāmadhye | saṃkocena na saṃśayaḥ | 
 tenaiva sarvalohāni | sahasrāṃśena vedhayet || (RA_12.128) 
 athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi | kumudinyā vidhiṃ priye | 
 bhittvā kāśmīripāṣāṇe | pūrṇimāyāṃ tu kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.129) 
 tasyāḥ pañcāṅgam ādāya | bhāvayet tu manaḥśilām | 
 kharpare dhārayitvā tu | bhāvayet tu punaḥ punaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.130) 
 kharpare drāvitaṃ nāgaṃ | tatkalkena yutaṃ kuru | 
 kāśmīradravatulyaṃ hi | jāyate kanakaṃ dhruvam ||
                    (RA_12.131) 
 citrakasya yathā grāhyaṃ | kathayāmi samāsataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.132) 
 citrakastrividho jñeyo | raktaḥ kṛṣṇo rasāyane | 
 śuklo vyādhipraśamane | śreṣṭho madhyaḥ kanīyasaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.133) 
 kṛṣṇaṃ raktaṃ sitaṃ vāpi | hemante noddharedbudhaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.134) 
 kṛṣṇacitrakamutpāṭya | gobhir nāghrātamīśvari | 
 kṣīramadhyasthitaṃ kṣīraṃ | kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ bhavet kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.135) 
 tasya pañcāṅgacūrṇena | pāradaṃ saha mardayet | 
 dhamec ca mūkamūṣāyāṃ | khoṭo bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.136) 
 raktāmbaradharo bhūtvā | raktamālyānulepanaḥ | 
 kṛṣṇapakṣe tu pañcamyāṃ | raktaśālyodanena tu | 
 baliṃ dattvā mahādevi | raktacitrakamuddharet ||
                    (RA_12.137) 
 raktacitrakacūrṇena | vaṅgas tāpais tribhis tribhiḥ | 
 sarvadoṣavinirmuktaḥ | stambhamāyāti tatkṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.138) 
 tanmūlaṃ sūtakaṃ cāmle | kaṅguṇītailasevanāt | 
 ekaviṃśativāreṇa | śulvaṃ śuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
                    (RA_12.139) 
 raktacitrakabhallāta- | tailaliptaṃ puṭena tu | 
 candrārkapattraṃ deveśi | jāyate hema śobhanam ||
                    (RA_12.140) 
 nāginīkandasūtendraṃ | raktacitrakasaṃyutam | 
 pattralepapramāṇena | candrārkaṃ kāñcanaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.141) 
 raktacitrakasaṃyukto | raso 'pi sarvado bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.142) 
 jyotiṣmatītailavidhiṃ | vakṣyāmi śṛṇu pārvati ||
                    (RA_12.143) 
 jyotiṣmatī nāma latā | yā ca kāñcanasaṃnibhā | 
 vallīvitānabahulā | hemavarṇaphalā śubhā || (RA_12.144) 
 āṣāḍhapūrvapakṣe tu | gṛhītvā bījamuttamam | 
 tilavat kvāthayitvā tu | hastaiḥ pādair athāpi vā | 
 tasya tailaṃ samādāya | kumbhe tāmramaye kṣipet ||
                    (RA_12.145) 
 tāpayed bhūgataṃ kumbhaṃ | kramādūrdhvaṃ tuṣāgninā | 
 ṣaṇmāse tu vyatikrānte | sa ghaṭaḥ kāñcanaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.146) 
 taṃ tu hemamayaṃ kṛtvā | tailamākṣikamiśritam | 
 prativāpe niṣiñcet tat | hema tāmrasamaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.147) 
 tathāca śatavedhi syād | vidyāratnamanuttamam ||
                    (RA_12.148) 
 dagdhārohāṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabandhakarīṃ priye | 
 sparśavedhe tu sā jñeyā | sarvakāryārthasādhinī ||
                    (RA_12.149) 
 śastracchinnā mahādevi | dagdhā vā pāvakena tu | 
 prarohati kṣaṇāddivyā | dagdhā chinnā mahauṣadhī ||
                    (RA_12.150) 
 raktaṃ pītaṃ sitaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ | tasyāḥ puṣpaṃ prajāyate | 
 caṇakasyeva pattrāṇi | suprasūtāni lakṣayet || (RA_12.151) 
 sā sthitā gomatītīre | gaṅgāyām arbude girau | 
 ujjayinyā dakṣiṇato | vanānteṣu ca dṛśyate || (RA_12.152) 
 tasyāḥ kandarasaṃ divyaṃ | kṛṣṇarājisamanvitam | 
 tāmbūlena samaṃ kṛtvā | guṭikāṃ kārayed budhaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.153) 
 sarveṣāmeva lohānāṃ | drutānāṃ vahnimadhyataḥ | 
 sahasraṃ vedhayitvā tu | kāñcanaṃ kurute kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.154) 
 tathaiva mriyate sūtaḥ | kāntahemābhrasaṃyutaḥ | 
 kurute kāñcanaṃ divyaṃ | devābharaṇabhūṣaṇam ||
                    (RA_12.155) 
 kaṭutumbīti vikhyātāṃ | devi divyauṣadhīṃ śṛṇu ||
                    (RA_12.156) 
 tasyā bījāni saṃgṛhya | sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.157) 
 ekaviṃśativārāṃstu | bhāvyaṃ dhātrīrasena tu | 
 payasā sahitenaiva | viśvabheṣajasaṃyutam || (RA_12.158) 
 bījaṃ yantre vinikṣipya | tailaṃ saṃgṛhya paṇḍitaḥ | 
 rasaṃ mūrchāpayet tena | cakramardena mardayet ||
                    (RA_12.159) 
 gopittaṃ śikhipittaṃ ca | kāṅkṣīkāsīsasaṃyutam | 
 tāratulyāni caitāni | sarveṣāṃ sūtakaḥ samaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.160) 
 meṣaśṛṅge nidhātavyaṃ | māsamekaṃ nirantaram | 
 lohadaṇḍena saṃsiktaṃ | sarvalohāni vedhayet ||
                    (RA_12.161) 
 gandhakaṃ lohadaṇḍena | ekaviṃśatibhāvitam | 
 yuktaṃ lohamanenaiva | jambīrarasasaṃyutam ||
                    (RA_12.162:1) 
 sabījaṃ sūtakopetam | andhamūṣāniveśitam | 
 bhūgataṃ māsamekaṃ tu | tāraṃ kāñcanatāṃ nayet ||
                    (RA_12.162:2) 
 dalasya bhāgamekaṃ tu | tārapañcakameva ca | 
 śulvasya pañcabhāgaṃ ca | bījasyaikaṃ ca yojayet ||
                    (RA_12.163) 
 ete dvādaśa bhāgāḥ syuḥ | sarvaṃ taddhārayet kṣitau | 
 sthānasyāsya niṣekaṃ tu | bhūdaṇḍena tu kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.164) 
 pañcaviṃśaddinānte tu | jāyate kanakottamam || (RA_12.165) 
 kṣīrakandavidhiṃ vakṣye | sarvasiddhikaraṃ param | 
 caturvarṇavidhaṃ tatra | raktakandaḥ praśasyate ||
                    (RA_12.166) 
 bhagnam etacchravet kṣīraṃ | raktavarṇaṃ suśobhanam ||
                    (RA_12.167) 
 meghānāṃ tu ninādena | saṃjātair upaśobhitaiḥ | 
 pattraiḥ snuhīsamaiḥ snigdhaiḥ | saptabhir hemasuprabhaiḥ | 
 bandhanaṃ rasarājasya | sarvasattvavaśaṃkaram ||
                    (RA_12.168) 
 tasya kṣīraṃ tu saṃgṛhya | tāraṃ nirvāpayed budhaḥ | 
 dhameddhavāgninā caiva | jāyate hema śobhanam ||
                    (RA_12.169) 
 tintiṇīpattraniryāsair | īṣattāmrarajoyutam | 
 mardayet pāradaṃ prājño | rasabandho bhaviṣyati ||
                    (RA_12.170) 
 toyamadhye vinikṣipya | guṭikā vajravad bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.171) 
 śākavṛkṣasya deveśi | niṣpīḍya rasamuttamam | 
 raktacandanasaṃyuktaṃ | sarvalohāni jārayet || (RA_12.172) 
 gandhapāṣāṇagandhena | āyase viniyojayet | 
 milanti sarvalohāni | dravanti salilaṃ yathā ||
                    (RA_12.173) 
 gandhakaṃ rasakaṃ tāpyaṃ | pāradaṃ raktacandanam | 
 rudantyā rasasaṃyuktaṃ | tāramāyāti kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.174) 
 śākavṛkṣasya niryāsaṃ | pattre tasya ca gālayet | 
 śigrumūlasya cūrṇaṃ tu | tadrasena vimardayet ||
                    (RA_12.175) 
 pralipya śulvapattrāṇi | puṭe kṣiptvā vipācayet | 
 taddrutaṃ kāñcanaṃ divyaṃ | bhavellakṣaṇasaṃyutam ||
                    (RA_12.176) 
 phalāni śākavṛkṣasya | paripakvāni saṃgṛhet | 
 tadrasena yutaṃ prājñaḥ | saptarātraṃ tu bhāvayet ||
                    (RA_12.177) 
 tadrasena samāyuktaṃ | mañjiṣṭhāmiśritaṃ tathā | 
 lepayet tārapattrāṇi | dhmātaṃ bhavati kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.178) 
 devadālyā mahauṣadhyā | vidhiṃ vakṣyāmi tatparam | 
 sā śvetā vyādhināśe ca | kṛṣṇā pītā rasāyane ||
                    (RA_12.179) 
 paurṇamāsyāṃ trayodaśyāṃ | rāhugraste divākare | 
 athavā kṛṣṇapañcamyām | imāṃ vidhivaduddharet ||
                    (RA_12.180) 
 devadālīphalaṃ devi | viṣṇukrāntā ca sūtakam | 
 mūrchayed bandhayet kṣipraṃ | śulvaṃ hema karoti ca ||
                    (RA_12.181) 
 devadālīphalaṃ mūlam | īśvarīrasa eva ca | 
 toyena marditaṃ kṛtvā | vaṅgaṃ stambhayati kṣaṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.182) 
 ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi | śvetaguñjāvidhiṃ priye ||
                    (RA_12.183) 
 kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyām | aṣṭamyāṃ vā surārcite | 
 kapāle mṛttikāṃ nyasya | secayet salilena tu ||
                    (RA_12.184) 
 bījāni sitaguñjāyāḥ | puṣpayogena vāpayet | 
 vakṣyamāṇena mantreṇa | kuryāt saṃgrahaṇaṃ tathā ||
                    (RA_12.185) 
 namo bhagavati śvetavalli śvetaparvatavāsini sarvakāryāṇi kuru kuru apratihate
                    namo namaḥ svāhā | 
 anena manunā proktā | siddhirbhavati nānyathā | 
 ṣaṇmāsena tathā vallīṃ | mantrapūtena rakṣayet ||
                    (RA_12.186) 
 śuddhaśulvaṃ tu saṃgṛhya | mūṣāmadhye tu saṃsthitam | 
 tripañcapalasaṃkhyaṃ tu | karṣārdhasitaguñjayā ||
                    (RA_12.187) 
 sahaikatra bhavet tāraṃ | tasya gandhavivarjitam | 
 brahmarītisamāyuktaṃ | guñjācūrṇaṃ sahaikataḥ | 
 devānāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ devi | jāyate hema śobhanam ||
                    (RA_12.188) 
 candrodakena deveśi | vakṣyāmi rasabandhanam ||
                    (RA_12.189) 
 śuklapakṣe pūrṇamāsyāṃ | dṛṣṭvā pūrṇendumaṇḍalam | 
 nirgacchanti mahīṃ bhittvā | candratoyānyanekadhā ||
                    (RA_12.190) 
 kānicinmṛttivarṇāni | rasena lavaṇāni tu | 
 kāniciccandratulyāni | vyomabhāsāni kānicit | 
 candravṛddhyābhivardheran | kṣīyeran tatkṣayeṇa tu ||
                    (RA_12.191) 
 dṛṣṭvā candrodakaṃ mantrī | paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣataḥ | 
 nirgacchati mahīṃ bhittvā | candravṛddhyā vivardhate ||
                    (RA_12.192) 
 kṣetrabandhaṃ purā kṛtvā | devamabhyarcya śaṃkaram | 
 caturdaśyāṃ ca tatkṣetraṃ | pūjayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ | 
 ahorātroṣito bhūtvā | baliṃ tatra nivedayet || (RA_12.193) 
 pūrṇamāsyāṃ ca rātrau ca | gatvā tasya samīpataḥ | 
 candrodakaṃ tu saṃgṛhya | mantrayuktaṃ sumantritam | 
 āloḍya madhusarpirbhyāṃ | pibettat tu samāhitaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.194) 
 pītamātreṇa tenaiva | mūrchā bhavati tatkṣaṇāt | 
 candrodaye tato dṛṣṭe | kṣīraṃ tasya tu dāpayet | 
 saptarātraprayogeṇa | candravannirmalo bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.195) 
 ekaviṃśatirātreṇa | jīvedbrahmadinatrayam | 
 ekamāsaprayogeṇa | brahmāyuḥ sa bhavennaraḥ || (RA_12.196) 
 candrodakena gaganaṃ | rasaṃ hema ca mardayet | 
 mūṣāmadhyagataṃ dhmātaṃ | tatkṣaṇādguṭikā bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.197) 
 ayaṃ ca sparśamātreṇa | lohānyaṣṭau ca vedhayet ||
                    (RA_12.198) 
 tadrasena rasaṃ bhāvyaṃ | vajreṇa samajāritam | 
 catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśataḥ piṇḍe | dviguṇe tu sahasrakam ||
                    (RA_12.199) 
 daśasaṃkalikābaddhaṃ | guñjāmātraṃ rasaṃ naraḥ | 
 trilohaveṣṭitaṃ vaktre | dhṛtvā cādṛśyatāṃ vrajet ||
                    (RA_12.200) 
 oṃ namo rudrāya daṃṣṭrotkaṭāya vighnanāśāya diśāṃ rakṣa rakṣa vidiśāṃ rakṣa rakṣa
                    rudro vijñāpayati huṃ phaṭ svāhā | 
 oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya triśūlahastāya amṛtodbhavāya rakṣa rakṣa phaṭ svāhā
                    | 
 athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi | kartarīrasabandhanam ||
                    (RA_12.201) 
 asurāṇāṃ samāyoge | krodhāviṣṭena cetasā | 
 sudarśanaṃ mahācakraṃ | preritaṃ muravairiṇā ||
                    (RA_12.202) 
 bhālapaṭṭāttatastasya | nipetuḥ svedabindavaḥ | 
 te bhūmau patitā divyāḥ | saṃjātāḥ kartarīrasaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.203) 
 rakṣārthaṃ sthāpitaṃ tatra | viṣṇunā ca sudarśanam | 
 cakratulyaṃ bhramatyetad | āyudhāni nikṛntati ||
                    (RA_12.204) 
 kurute garjitaṃ nādaṃ | dhūmaṃ jvālāṃ vimuñcati | 
 kartarī dṛṣṭimātreṇa | tathānyā śabdakartarī ||
                    (RA_12.205) 
 sā sparśakartarī chāyā- | kartarī dhūmakartarī | 
 sā jvālākartarī caiva | śaktirghorasya kartarī ||
                    (RA_12.206) 
 lokānāṃ tu hitārthāya | ghoraśaktir vyavasthitā | 
 rasarūpā mahāghorā | asiddhānāṃ tu chedinī || (RA_12.207) 
 tasyāḥ kṣetraṃ yadā gacchet | aghorāstraṃ japettadā | 
 punarghoraṃ nyasettatra | athāstraṃ vinyasedbudhaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.208) 
 anulomavilomena | dehe 'dhiṣṭhāpya kartarīm | 
 mudrayā mudrayet tāṃ tu | aghorāstreṇa yojitām ||
                    (RA_12.209) 
 dīpenārādhayet tāṃ tu | stambhayed dhūpanena ca | 
 viṣṭarāmudrayā tāṃ tu | sthānayogaṃ niyojayet ||
                    (RA_12.210) 
 kañcukī tu śilā krāntā | kumārī vajrakandakam | 
 yoṣidraktaṃ gavāṃ mūtraṃ | tilakaḥ sarvavaśyakṛt ||
                    (RA_12.211) 
 athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi | viṣodarasabandhanam ||
                    (RA_12.212) 
 viṣodakaṃ viṣasamaṃ | ghṛtavac ca ghṛtodakam | 
 sitapītādivarṇāḍhyaṃ | tac ca devi rasottamam ||
                    (RA_12.213) 
 tatra gatvā vanoddeśe | smaredghorasahasrakam | 
 keśāḥ kṣiptāḥ sphuṭantyasmin | ātmacchāyā na dṛśyate ||
                    (RA_12.214) 
 tailaṃ ca golakākāraṃ | ghṛtaṃ caiva visarpati |

                    (RA_12.215) 
 āptvā pālāśapattreṇa | kaṭukālābuke kṣipet | 
 viṣodakaṃ gandhakaṃ ca | harabījaṃ ca tatsamam ||
                    (RA_12.216) 
 ajākṣīreṇa piṣṭvā tu | śulvapattrāṇi lepayet |

 śatāṃśenaiva deveśi | sarvalohāni vedhayet || (RA_12.217) 
 anena vidhinā devi | nāgaḥ sindūratāṃ vrajet |

                    (RA_12.218) 
 raktaṃ pītaṃ tathā kṛṣṇam | uttarottarakāryakṛt ||
                    (RA_12.219) 
 tripalaṃ kāntapātre vā | pātre 'lābumaye 'pi vā |

                    (RA_12.220) 
 sthāpayed dhānyarāśau tu | divasānekaviṃśatim |

                    (RA_12.221) 
 pāyasaṃ bhakṣayed yas tu | madhvājyena tu saṃyutam |

                    (RA_12.222) 
 lāṅgalī gṛhadhūmaṃ ca | sindūraṃ rajanīdvayam |

                    (RA_12.223:1) 
 sabījaṃ sūtakaṃ caiva | viṣatoyena marditam |

                    (RA_12.223:2) 
 athavā bhāvayet tat tu | yāvaccūrṇaṃ tu tadbhavet |

                    (RA_12.224)

                    (RA_12.225)
