                    (RA_12.226) 
 viṣapānīyamādāya | yavāgau vartitaṃ śubham | 
 niṣiktaṃ tac ca varte 'yaṃ | tāraṃ bhavati śobhanam ||
                    (RA_12.227) 
 viṣapānīyamādāya | prakṣipec ca rasottame | 
 kunaṭīgandhapāṣāṇa- | viṣaṭaṅkaṇalāṅgalī ||
                    (RA_12.228:1) 
 naṣṭapiṣṭīkṛtaṃ khalle | tārapattrāṇi lepayet | 
 andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ | nirbījaṃ kanakaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.228:2) 
 oṃ śrīnīlakaṇṭhāya ṭha ṭhaḥ | 
 asyāyutaṃ japet | 
 viṣatṛṇavidhiṃ vakṣye | samāhitamanāḥ śṛṇu || (RA_12.229) 
 gandhamākṣīkadaradaṃ | kunaṭyā rasasaṃyutam | 
 viṣatṛṇasamāyuktaṃ | mātuluṅgāmlamarditam || (RA_12.230) 
 etat kalkaṃ palamātraṃ | cauṣadhyā lepanaṃ kuru | 
 niryāse tu puṭaṃ kuryāt | trivāraṃ hema śobhanam ||
                    (RA_12.231) 
 saṃjīvanījalasyātha | vidhiṃ vakṣyāmi pārvati ||
                    (RA_12.232) 
 śukreṇārādhito devi | prāgahaṃ suravandite | 
 dānavānāṃ hitārthāya | mṛtānāṃ devasaṃgare || (RA_12.233) 
 mayā saṃjīvanī vidyā | dattā codakarūpiṇī | 
 tayā saṃjīvitā daityā | ye mṛtā devasaṃgare || (RA_12.234) 
 nikṣiptā martyaloke sā | samyak te kathayāmyaham ||
                    (RA_12.235) 
 asti martye mahāpuṇyā | pavitrā dakṣiṇāpathe | 
 nadī godāvarī nāma | prasiddhā jāhnavī yathā ||
                    (RA_12.236) 
 dakṣiṇe ca taṭe tasyāḥ | kadalīnagaraṃ param | 
 tasya dakṣiṇataḥ śailaḥ | sarvalokeṣu viśrutaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.237) 
 nāmnā kṛṣṇagiriśceti | dṛśyate sarvamaṅgale | 
 suprasiddhāmbikā nāma | grāmastasyāsti saṃnidhau ||
                    (RA_12.238) 
 tatrāpyudakamālokya | parīkṣyeta surārcite || (RA_12.239) 
 gṛhītvā śuṣkavaṃśaṃ tu | kṣipettoyasya madhyataḥ | 
 jāyate haritaṃ snigdham | ahorātreṇa niścitam | 
 muñcatyaṅkurapattrāṇi | dṛśyate tanmanoharam ||
                    (RA_12.240) 
 balipuṣpopahāreṇa | tato devīṃ samarcayet | 
 kṣetrādhipaṃ gaṇeśaṃca | caṇḍayonīśvaraṃ tathā ||
                    (RA_12.241) 
 tasya mantraṃ pravakṣyāmi | triṣu lokeṣu durlabham ||
                    (RA_12.242) 
 oṃ caṇḍāya pinākine śūlahastāya oṃ diśāṃ bandhaya vidiśāṃ bandhaya ṭhaṭhaḥ | 
 tilāṃś ca taṇḍulāṃścaiva | mantreṇānena sarṣapān | 
 saptābhimantritānkṛtvā | sādhako dikṣu nikṣipet ||
                    (RA_12.243) 
 kaṭukālābuke toyaṃ | kṛtarakṣaṃ samāhitaḥ | 
 gṛhītvā tatprayatnena | nijasthānaṃ samāśrayet ||
                    (RA_12.244) 
 oṃ namo 'mṛte 'mṛtarūpiṇi amṛtaṃ me kuru kuru evaṃ rudra ājñāpayati svāhā | 
 saptābhimantritaṃ kṛtvā | mantreṇānena tajjalam | 
 dinamekaṃ tathā sūtaṃ | svarṇamāṣadvayānvitam | 
 mardayet tena toyena | pibettat tu vicakṣaṇaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.245) 
 ekaviṃśatirātreṇa | kṣīrāhāro 'tha yatnataḥ | 
 jīvet kalpāyutaṃ sāgraṃ | kāmarūpo mahābalaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.246) 
 yojanānāṃ śataṃ gatvā | punareva nivartate | 
 avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ | svec chācāraḥ sa khecaraḥ ||
                    (RA_12.247) 
 kanakaṃ pāradaṃ vyoma | samamekatra yojayet | 
 mardayet tena toyena | saptavāraṃ tu svedayet ||
                    (RA_12.248) 
 sa rasaḥ sarvalohāni | ṣaṣṭyaṃśena tu vedhayet ||
                    (RA_12.249) 
 athavā taṃ rasaṃ divyaṃ | madhunā saha bhakṣayet | 
 māsamātraprayogeṇa | jīvedbrahmadināyutam || (RA_12.250) 
 tasya mūtramalasvedaiḥ | śulvaṃ bhavati kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.251) 
 nirvāte toyamādāya | añjalitritayaṃ pibet | 
 pītamātre bhavenmūrchā | svāsthyaṃ syāt praharatrayāt ||
                    (RA_12.252) 
 ekaviṃśaddinānyevaṃ | kṣīrāhāro bhavet tataḥ | 
 aṣṭavarṣākṛtiḥ prājñaḥ | kāmarūpo mahābalaḥ || (RA_12.253) 
 paśyec chidrāṃ mahīṃ sarvāṃ | saptapātālasaṃyutām | 
 avadhyo devadaityānāṃ | kalpāyuś ca prajāyate ||
                    (RA_12.254) 
 athavodakamādāya | pāradaṃ ca manaḥśilām | 
 mardayet khallapāṣāṇe | naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ bhavet tataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.255) 
 svedayet saptarātraṃ tu | trilohena ca veṣṭayet ||
                    (RA_12.256) 
 antardhānaṃ kṣaṇādgacchet | vidyādharapatirbhavet | 
 siddhakanyāśatavṛto | yāvat kalpān caturdaśa ||
                    (RA_12.257) 
 dineṣu teṣu sarveṣu | dadyāc chālyodanaṃ ghṛtam | 
 payasā ca samāyuktaṃ | nityamevaṃ tu kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.258) 
 uṣṇodakavidhiṃ vakṣye | samāhitamanāḥ śṛṇu | 
 paśyed uṣṇodakaṃ yatra | vāsaṃ tatraiva kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.259) 
 asti godāvarī nāma | mahārāṣṭre 'tiviśrutā | 
 tasyā uttarabhāge tu | sahyādriḥ puṇyaparvataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.260) 
 tatra mātāpuraṃ nāma | prasiddhaṃ devatāgṛham | 
 tasmāduttarato devi | kampākhyaṃ nagaraṃ param ||
                    (RA_12.261) 
 tatra kampeśvaro devas | tatrāstyuṣṇodakaṃ dhruvam | 
 praṇītākhyā nadī tatra | snātvā vai sādhakottamaḥ | 
 paścāduṣṇodake kuṇḍe | vidhiṃ kuryād yathoditaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.262) 
 śarvarīm uṣitastatra | dhanavāṃś ca dine dine | 
 bhakṣayen māsamātraṃ tu | jīved varṣaśatāṣṭakam ||
                    (RA_12.263) 
 varṣamekaṃ prayuñjīta | jīvedvarṣāyutaṃ sukhī | 
 valīpalitanirmukto | bhogī caiva puraṃdaraḥ || (RA_12.264) 
 varṣamekaṃ pibet toyaṃ | jīvec candrārkatārakam | 
 tasya mūtrapurīṣeṇa | śulvaṃ bhavati kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.265) 
 uṣṇodakaṃ ca kāsīsaṃ | gandhapāṣāṇasaṃyutam | 
 caturthāṃśena rasakaṃ | daśabhāgaṃ vinikṣipet ||
                    (RA_12.266) 
 śulvaṃ ca mardayet sarvaṃ | naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ kṣaṇena tu | 
 tena lepitamātreṇa | śulvaṃ bhavati kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.267) 
 niṣiktaṃ tena toyena | prativāpaṃ daded budhaḥ | 
 śulvaṃ ca jāyate hema | taruṇādityavarcasam || (RA_12.268) 
 tajjalena niṣiktaṃ ca | hema bījārthasaṃyutam | 
 tāraṃ cānena mārgeṇa | niṣiktaṃ hematāṃ vrajet ||
                    (RA_12.269) 
 uṣṇodakena bhallātaṃ | tilapiṣṭaṃ ca bhakṣayet | 
 māsadvayaprayogeṇa | jīvedvarṣaśatatrayam || (RA_12.270) 
 rasagandhāśmarasakaṃ | tutthaṃ daradamākṣikam | 
 yāmamuṣṇāmbhasā ghṛṣṭaṃ | tārapattrāṇi lepayet ||
                    (RA_12.271) 
 dvivāraṃ tu dhameddevi | syāccaturdaśavarṇakam | 
 krameṇānena deveśi | śulvaṃ ṣoḍaśavarṇakam || (RA_12.272) 
 ekaikaṃ hematārāṃśaṃ | dvaṃdvaṃ kāntābhrayoḥ pṛthak | 
 uṣṇodakena saṃmardya | dhamanāt khoṭatāṃ vrajet ||
                    (RA_12.273) 
 tanmukhe dhārayen māsaṃ | vajrakāyo bhavennaraḥ | 
 taccūrṇaṃ yavamātraṃ tu | bhakṣayen madhusarpiṣā | 
 yāvat palaṃ tasya malaiḥ | śulvaṃ bhavati kāñcanam ||
                    (RA_12.274) 
 uṣṇodapācitān khādet | kulatthān kṣīrapo bhavet | 
 snānamuṣṇāmbhasā kuryāt | varṣādvarṣaśatāyuṣam ||
                    (RA_12.275) 
 kṣīramuṣṇodakaṃ kvāthaṃ | triphalāyāś ca pācayet | 
 pāyasaṃ kāntapātre tan | māsam ekaṃ tu bhakṣayet | 
 bhuktvā jīvet kalpaśataṃ | vaiṣṇavāyur bhavennaraḥ ||
                    (RA_12.276) 
 ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi | śailodakavidhiṃ priye | 
 kardamāpo mahīśailaṃ | śilaṃ ceti caturvidham ||
                    (RA_12.277) 
 kānicit kṣaṇavedhīni | dinavedhīni kānicit | 
 pakṣamāsādiṣaṇmāsa- | vedhanāni mahītale || (RA_12.278) 
 kṣiptaṃ yadā bhavet kāṣṭhaṃ | śailībhūtaṃ ca dṛśyate | 
 bahirantaś ca deveśi | vedhakaṃ tat prakīrtitam ||
                    (RA_12.279) 
 hiṅgulaṃ haritālaṃ ca | gandhakaṃ ca manaḥśilā | 
 eṣāṃ gandhāpahāraṃ yat | kurute tac ca vedhakam ||
                    (RA_12.280) 
 gandhakaṃ tālakaṃ caiva | toyapūrṇe ghaṭe kṣipet | 
 yadā tadbudbudākāraṃ | tadā śailodakaṃ bhavet | 
 anyathā veṣṭakaṃ devi | tadagrāhyaṃ nirarthakam ||
                    (RA_12.281) 
 śrīśaile śrīvanaprānte | paryaṅkākhye śilātale | 
 tatrasthaṃ kṣaṇavedhi syāt | nadībhagavatītaṭe | 
 ekāhe vedhakaṃ tatra | gokarṇe tu dinatrayam ||
                    (RA_12.282) 
 bhadrāṅge dinavedhi syāt | tristhalānte trivāsaram | 
 dhāreśvare pākṣikaṃ syāt | varṣāpuryāṃ dinaikataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.283) 
 brahmeśvare māsikaṃ syāt | vyāghrapuryāṃ tu vāsaram | 
 aghoreśe māsikaṃ tu | siṃhadvīpe tathā punaḥ | 
 dinamekaṃ brahmagirau | vindhye tu kṣaṇavedhakam ||
                    (RA_12.284) 
 vāsaraṃ mālyavanteṣu | kṣaṇavedhi śilodakam || (RA_12.285) 
 kiṣkindhyāparvate ramye | pampātīre tṛṇodakam | 
 tasya paścimato devi | yojanadvitaye punaḥ | 
 bhūśailamasti tatraiva | tridinaṃ vedhi parvate ||
                    (RA_12.286) 
 sahyācale pure devyāḥ | kṣīrakṣetrasya saṃnidhau | 
 śailodakaṃ koṭivedhi | durjadeśe 'pi vāsaram | 
 lakṣavedhi nṛsiṃhasya | nagare gokulābhidhe || (RA_12.287) 
 anyatra yatra tatrāpi | brahmaviṣṇuśivodbhavam | 
 amṛtaṃ tatra tatrāpi | vajrīkaraṇam uttamam || (RA_12.288) 
 tasyotpattiṃ pravakṣyāmi | yathā jānanti sādhakāḥ ||
                    (RA_12.289) 
 mahīṃ samuddhṛtavato | varāhasya kalevarāt | 
 yaḥ svedaḥ patitastasmāj | jātaṃ śailodakaṃ param ||
                    (RA_12.290) 
 tanmukhe kṣaṇikaṃ jātaṃ | kroḍadeśe tu vāsaram | 
 bāhubhyāṃ tryahavedhi syāt | māsavedhi tu pārśvayoḥ | 
 ṣaṇmāsamaparāṅge ca | sarvaṃ samaphalaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.291) 
 aghorāstreṇa tatkṣetra- | rakṣāṃ kṛtvā diśāṃ balim | 
 dattvā lakṣaṃ japitvā tu | gṛhṇīyādamṛtaṃ param ||
                    (RA_12.292) 
 śaradgrīṣmavasanteṣu | hemante vā surārcite | 
 āyase tāmrapātre vā | pātre 'lābumaye 'thavā | 
 śailāmbupalamaṣṭau tu | palaṃ kṣīrasya nikṣipet ||
                    (RA_12.293) 
 kṣīrāvaśeṣaṃ saṃkvāthya | trisaptāhaṃ pibennaraḥ | 
 jīved varṣasahasraṃ tu | valīpalitavarjitaḥ || (RA_12.294) 
 athavāṣṭapalaṃ kṣīraṃ | palaikenāmbunā yutam | 
 kṣīrāvaśeṣaṃ seveta | pūrvoktaṃ labhate phalam ||
                    (RA_12.295) 
 kulatthāṣṭaguṇaṃ vāri | pacedaṣṭāvaśeṣitam | 
 caturguṇena tenājyaṃ | pācayed dhṛtaśeṣitam || (RA_12.296) 
 lihyānmadhusamopetaṃ | trisaptāhaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ | 
 māsena śāstrasampattiṃ | jñātvā devi balābalam | 
 dvir aṣṭavarṣakākāraḥ | sahasrāyur na saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.297) 
 avaśiṣṭakulatthaṃ tu | pādāṃśaṃ madhusarpiṣā | 
 bhakṣayed varṣam ekaṃ tu | māsenāyutajīvitaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.298) 
 tatsiddhatailenābhyaṅgaṃ | mardanaṃ cāpi kārayet | 
 māsamekaṃ tato mardyaṃ | dehasiddhiṃ karoti ca ||
                    (RA_12.299) 
 pāmāvicarcikādadru- | kuṣṭhāni sahasā jayet | 
 valīpalitanirmuktaḥ | sahasrāyuś ca jāyate || (RA_12.300) 
 yaḥ pibet prātarutthāya | śailāmbuculukatrayam | 
 ṣaṇmāsāt syāt sahasrāyur | valīpalitavarjitaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.301) 
 athavā sūtakaṃ devi | vāriṇā saha mardayet | 
 māsenaikena deveśi | naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ bhaviṣyati || (RA_12.302) 
 māsamātraṃ samaśnīyāt | sa bhavedajarāmaraḥ || (RA_12.303) 
 athavā taṃ rasaṃ hemnā | hemabhasma tato balī | 
 mardayet tena toyena | dhāmayet khadirāgninā ||
                    (RA_12.304) 
 guṭikā sundarī nāma | sarvāyudhanivāraṇī | 
 kartā hartā svayaṃ siddho | jīvec candrārkatārakam ||
                    (RA_12.305) 
 kunaṭī cābhramākṣīkaṃ | hema tāraṃ tathaiva ca | 
 tat sarvaṃ payasā kṣīrair | madyaṃ pācyaṃ dinatrayam | 
 māsamātraprayogeṇa | valīpalitavarjitaḥ || (RA_12.306) 
 atha tenodakenaiva | kṣīrārdhaṃ pāyasaṃ pacet | 
 māsamātraprayogeṇa | valīpalitanāśanam || (RA_12.307) 
 paktvā tenāmbhasā pathyāḥ | ṣaṣṭiṃ trīṇi śatāni ca | 
 madhu saṃyojya bhāṇḍasthaṃ | bhūmau sarvaṃ nidhāpayet ||
                    (RA_12.308) 
 dine dine tathaikaikaṃ | bhakṣayet prātarutthitaḥ | 
 valīpalitanirmukto | jīvedvarṣasahasrakam || (RA_12.309) 
 śailībhūtaṃ kulatthaṃ vā | bhakṣayen madhusarpiṣā | 
 ṣaṇmāsena prāśanena | jīvedvarṣasahasrakam || (RA_12.310) 
 kūṣmāṇḍaṃ māritaṃ kṛtvā | yāni kāni phalāni ca | 
 jale kṣiptāni lohāni | śailībhūtāni bhakṣayet | 
 kṣīrāhāraś ca jīrṇānte | vajrakāyo bhavennaraḥ ||
                    (RA_12.311) 
 tenodakena saṃmardya | abhrakaṃ kvāthayet priye | 
 kaṭutrayayutaṃ khādet | jīvedvarṣasahasrakam ||
                    (RA_12.312) 
 athavā rasakarṣaikaṃ | tajjalena tu mardayet | 
 iṅgudīphalamadhyasthaṃ | tacchailodakamadhyagam | 
 kālena triguṇenaiva | kāṭhinyaṃ tasya jāyate ||
                    (RA_12.313) 
 ṣaṇmāsaṃ tanmukhe dhāryaṃ | vajrakāyaṃ karoti ca | 
 daśanāgasamaprāṇo | devaiḥ saha ca modate || (RA_12.314) 
 gṛhītvā triphalāṃ tatra | śailavāriṇi nikṣipet | 
 yadā bhavati tacchailaṃ | gṛhītvā cūrṇayet tataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.315) 
 kāntajīrṇarasaṃ tena | sārdhaṃ ghṛtamadhuplutam | 
 bhakṣayed varṣamekaṃ tu | tataḥ kṣīrāśano bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.316) 
 udayādityasaṃkāśo | medhāvī priyadarśanaḥ | 
 nīlakuñcitakeśaś ca | jīvec candrārkatārakam ||
                    (RA_12.317) 
 pāradaṃ haritālaṃ ca | śilā mākṣikameva ca | 
 daradaṃ ca viṣaṃ caiva | sarvamekatra kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.318) 
 mardayet khallapāṣāṇe | mātuluṅgarasena ca | 
 golakaṃ kārayitvā tu | vārimadhye nidhāpayet ||
                    (RA_12.319) 
 tena tāraṃ ca śulvaṃ ca | kāñcanaṃ bhavati dhruvam ||
                    (RA_12.320) 
 upayuñjīta māsaikaṃ | valīpalitavarjitaḥ | 
 sahasraṃ jīvitaṃ tasya | mahābalaparākramaḥ || (RA_12.321) 
 śailībhūtāṃ haridrāṃ tu | taccūrṇavāpamātrataḥ | 
 hematvaṃ labhate nāgo | bālārkasadṛśaprabham ||
                    (RA_12.322) 
 śailodake vinikṣipya | bhūśaile kardame 'pi vā | 
 jñātvā kālapramāṇena | bandhayet pāradaṃ tataḥ ||
                    (RA_12.323) 
 raktakṣārayutaṃ dhmātaṃ | suvarṇaṃ samasāritam | 
 śatāṃśena tu lohānāṃ | sarveṣāṃ hemakārakam || (RA_12.324) 
 dvitīyasāraṇāṃ prāpya | bhakṣayen madhusarpiṣā | 
 tatkālaṃ cittajātānām | ūrdhvaṃ bhavati cānilaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.325) 
 kālajñānaṃ bhavet tasya | jīvedayutapañcakam ||
                    (RA_12.326) 
 dvitīyasāraṇāṃ prāpya | sahasrāṃśena vidhyati | 
 taṃ khoṭaṃ dhārayed vaktre | divyatvaṃ labhate dhruvam ||
                    (RA_12.327) 
 nicule kakubhe caiva | kiṃśuke madhuke 'pi vā | 
 iṅgudīphalamadhye vā | rajanīdvayamadhyataḥ || (RA_12.328) 
 pāradaṃ gandhakaṃ caiva | mardayet gulikākṛti | 
 pācayed dinamekaṃ tu | hemnā saṃveṣṭya dhārayet ||
                    (RA_12.329) 
 triphalāvyoṣakalkena | veṣṭayitvā prayatnataḥ | 
 pādena kanakaṃ dattvā | pāradaṃ tatra yojayet | 
 kṣipec chailāmbumadhyasthaṃ | gulikā vajravadbhavet ||
                    (RA_12.330) 
 pūrvavat sāraṇā kāryā | pūrvavat siddhidā bhavet | 
 dhāryamāṇā mukhe sā tu | sahasrāyuṣkarī bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.331) 
 dvitīyasāraṇāyogād | ayutaṃ vedhayet tu sā | 
 dhāryamāṇā mukhe seyam | ayutāyuḥpradā bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.332) 
 tṛtīyasāraṇāyogāj | jāyate lakṣavedhinī | 
 taṃ khoṭaṃ dhārayed vaktre | lakṣāyurjāyate naraḥ ||
                    (RA_12.333) 
 caturthīṃ sāraṇāṃ prāpya | koṭivedho na saṃśayaḥ | 
 koṭyāyurjīvitaṃ tasya | khecaratvaṃ ca labhyate ||
                    (RA_12.334) 
 pañcabhir daśakoṭiḥ syāt | ṣaḍbhiḥ koṭiśataṃ bhavet | 
 yāvaccandrārkajīvitvam | anantabalavīryavān || (RA_12.335) 
 dadāti saptamīṃ sāpi | sāraṇāṃ guṭikā parā | 
 khecarī nāma vikhyātā | bhairaveṇa pracoditā ||
                    (RA_12.336) 
 yas tu tadrājikāmātraṃ | māsamekaṃ tu bhakṣayet | 
 vajradehaḥ sa siddhaḥ syāt | divyastrījanavallabhaḥ | 
 krīḍate khecarair bhogaiḥ | svec chayā śivatāṃ vrajet ||
                    (RA_12.337) 
 nānāvidhaphalaṃ ca syāt | tadrasair bījatailataḥ | 
 tadbaddhaṃ pāradaṃ caiva | guṭikāṃ śṛṇu sundari ||
                    (RA_12.338) 
 śuddhabaddharasendras tu | gandhakaṃ tatra jārayet | 
 triguṇe gandhake jīrṇe | tena hema tu kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.339) 
 kārayed bhasma sūtaṃ tu | kāñcanaṃ tatra sūtakam | 
 tadbhasma sūtake jāryaṃ | rasendrasya same samam ||
                    (RA_12.340) 
 tena sūtakajīrṇena | vajraratnaṃ tu jārayet | 
 tadvajraṃ jāyate bhasma | sindūrāruṇasaṃnibham ||
                    (RA_12.341) 
 tadbhasma jārayate sūte | triguṇe tu surārcite | 
 hāṭake sārayet taṃ tu | guṭikāṃ tena kārayet ||
                    (RA_12.342) 
 trilohāveṣṭitaṃ taṃ tu | mukhe prakṣipya sādhakaḥ | 
 naṣṭacchāyo bhavet so 'yam | adṛśyo devadānavaiḥ ||
                    (RA_12.343) 
 tat kṣaṇād vedhayed devi | sarvalohāni kāñcanam | 
 bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi | nirvalīpalito bhavet || (RA_12.344) 
 śūlinaṃ śaktisaṃyuktaṃ | ratnādiguṇabhūṣitam | 
 vaktre kare ca bibhṛyāt | sarvāyudhanivāraṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.345) 
 vyoma mākṣikasattvaṃ ca | tārāmātraṃ surāyudham | 
 vaikrāntaṃ tālakaṃ sūtaṃ | ratnādiguṇabhūṣitam ||
                    (RA_12.346) 
 guṭikā sā varārohe | madhuratrayasaṃyutā | 
 vaktrasthā nāśayet sākṣāt | palitaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ | 
 śivaśaktiś ca deveśi | ratnādiśivagā yathā || (RA_12.347) 
 hema tāraṃ tathā bhānuṃ | samabhāgāni kārayet | 
 strīrajo vyāghramadhyasthaṃ | padmasūtreṇa veṣṭayet ||
                    (RA_12.348) 
 secayet tat tathāveṣṭya | guhyasthāne nidhāpayet | 
 raṇe rājakule dyūte | divye kāmye jayo bhavet | 
 yanmukhe caiva tadgolaṃ | sa sarvarañjako bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.349) 
 vaikrāntābhrakakāntaṃ tu | sasyakaṃ tu surāyudham | 
 vibhītakādisambhūta- | kāñcikasya samaṃ bhavet ||
                    (RA_12.350) 
 rājāvartaṃ tataḥ sūte | yojayet pādayogataḥ | 
 kumārīrasasaṃghṛṣṭā | kṛtaikā guṭikā śubhā | 
 rogamṛtyujarā hanti | vaktrasthā nātra saṃśayaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.351) 
 pañcatāraṃ varārohe | sūtakaṃ dvayameva ca | 
 trayo gaganabhāgāḥ syur | ekaikaṃ hemakāntayoḥ ||
                    (RA_12.352) 
 ardhaśulvavidhānena | guṭikāmarasundari | 
 akṣayo hy ajaraścaiva | bhavet tena mahābalaḥ | 
 sarvarogavinirmukto | jīvedvaktre vidhāraṇāt ||
                    (RA_12.353) 
 bhasmasūtapalaikaṃ ca | mṛtakāntapalaṃ tathā | 
 mākṣikasya palaṃ caiva | śilājatupalaṃ punaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.354) 
 palamekaṃ viḍaṅgasya | pathyācūrṇapalaṃ tathā | 
 ekīkṛtyātha tat sarvaṃ | madhvājyena tu peṣayet ||
                    (RA_12.355) 
 guṭikāḥ kārayed devi | ṣaṣṭyadhikaśatatrayam |

                    (RA_12.356) 
 jīvedvarṣasahasrāṇi | rudratulyo mahābalaḥ || (RA_12.357) 
 ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi | rasabhasmarasāyanam | 
 vijñeyaṃ niṣparīhāraṃ | sākṣāddivyauṣadhaṃ param ||
                    (RA_12.358) 
 āmalakyādi kāntaṃ ca | pāradaṃ ca manaḥśilām | 
 vākucīsaptabhāgaṃ ca | kṣīriṇīrasapeṣitam | 
 meghanādarasopetaṃ | mūkamūṣāgataṃ puṭet || (RA_12.359) 
 māṣaṃ trimāṣaṃ triguṇaṃ | bhakṣayet tu krameṇa tu | 
 varṣatrayaparaṃ devi | pādaniṣkārdhakaṃ kramāt ||
                    (RA_12.360) 
 ṣaṭ saptāṣṭau ca varṣāṇi | kramān niṣkapramāṇataḥ | 
 bhuñjīta sa ca divyānnaṃ | jarāvairūpyavarjitaḥ ||
                    (RA_12.361) 
 kiṃcit kāñcanasaṃyuktaṃ | niṣkaṃ niṣkārdhameva ca | 
 yo bhakṣayet tribhirvarṣaiḥ | sarvavyādhīn jayatyalam ||
                    (RA_12.362) 
 aṣṭavarṣe sahasrāyuḥ | dvādaśe lakṣavedhakaḥ |

                    bhāgamaṣṭāvaśeṣam |

                    mṛtaṃ ca || Ras_12.364 ||

                    || Ras_12.365 ||

                    || (RA_12.369) 
 kāntahemaravicandram abhrakaṃ | vajraratnam ahirājagolakam |

                    (RA_12.370)

                    || (RA_12.372)

 ṣaṇmāsena prayogeṇa | hy ajarāmaratāṃ vrajet ||

 srotoñjanayutaṃ dhmātaṃ | sattvaṃ pāradamiśritam |

 yasya yo vidhir āmnāta | udakasya śivāgame | 
 rasenaiva tu kāle tu | kuryād eva rasāyanam || (RA_12.382)

                 śrīdevyuvāca / (RA_13.1.1) 
 deva tvaṃ pāradendrasya proktā me bālajāraṇā / (RA_13.1.2) 
 ataḥ paraṃ samācakṣva samyagbaddhasya jāraṇām //
                    (RA_13.1.3) 
 śrībhairava uvāca / (2.1) 
  yā pūrvaṃ varṇitā seyamadhamā bālajāraṇā / (2.2) 
 uttamā durlabhā caiva śrūyatāṃ baddhajāraṇā // (RA_13.2.3) 
 abaddhaṃ jārayed yas tu jīryamāṇaḥ kṣayaṃ vrajet /
                    (RA_13.3.1) 
 baddhasya jīryate grāso jīrṇasya ca mukhaṃ bhavet //
                    (RA_13.3.2) 
 sumukho nirmukho dhatte sampūrṇottamalakṣaṇe / (RA_13.4.1) 
 sāmānyo 'gnisahatvena mahāratnāni jārakaḥ // (RA_13.4.2) 
 sāmānyaḥ prathamaṃ kāryaḥ sagrāsas tu susaṃmataḥ / (5.1) 
 vasudehakaro devi sāmānyo hi bhavedayam // (RA_13.5.2) 
 grāsahīnas tu yo baddho divyasiddhikaro bhavet // (RA_13.6) 
 uttamo mūlabandhas tu madhyamaṃ rasabandhanam / (7.1) 
 adhamaḥ pākabandhaḥ syādevaṃ trividhabandhanam //
                    (RA_13.7.2) 
 mūlabandhana mūlabandhas tu yo bandho vāsanābandha ucyate /
                    (8.1) 
 syāc catuḥṣaṣṭimūlebhyaḥ kiṃcin mūlena bandhanam //
                    (RA_13.8.2) 
 prāṇyaṅgamasurādīnāṃ mūlāṅgaṃ devatāmatam / (RA_13.9.1) 
 pāṣāṇaṃ caiva siddhānāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ ca pūjitam //
                    (RA_13.9.2) 
 piṇḍikādrutisaṃkocais trividhaṃ bandhanaṃ bhavet /
                    (RA_13.10.1) 
 divyābhiroṣadhībhiś ca prāguktaṃ śuddhabandhanam //
                    (10.2) 
 kṣaṇabandha drutibhirbadhyate sūtaḥ kṣaṇabandha udāhṛtaḥ //
                    (11) 
 abhrakaṃ harabījaṃ ca ṣoḍaśāṃśena kāñcanam / (12.1)

                    (RA_13.12.2) 
 dakṣiṇāvartitaṃ dhmātaṃ harabījena melakam / (RA_13.13.1) 
 mūṣāṃ tyaktvā varārohe tiṣṭhate baddhavadrasaḥ //
                    (RA_13.13.2) 
 raktikārdhārdhamātreṇa parvatānapi vedhayet /
                    (RA_13.14.1) 
 bhakṣaṇāttasya deveśi rudratulyo bhavennaraḥ /
                    (RA_13.14.2) 
 krīḍate saptalokeṣu śivatulyaparākramaḥ // (RA_13.14.3) 
 drutimelana mit divyauṣadhis drutīnāṃ melanaṃ devi
                    divyauṣadhiparaṃ śṛṇu // (15) 
 vajrakandaṃ lāṅgalī ca uccāṭena samanvitam / (RA_13.16.1) 
 abhrakaṃ kramate śīghram anyathā nāsti saṃkramaḥ //
                    (16.2) 
 melana von druti und rasa
                    kṛṣṇāguruśaṅkhanābhīrasonasitarāmaṭhaiḥ / (17.1) 
 nārīkusumapālāśabījatailasamanvitaiḥ / (RA_13.17.2) 
 soṣṇair milanti kvathitā drutayaḥ sakalā rasaiḥ //
                    (RA_13.17.3) 
 sarvadvandvamelāpana mākṣikaṃ ca viṣaṃ guñjā ṭaṅkaṇaṃ
                    strīrajastathā / (18.1)

                    (RA_13.18.2) 
 loha-, drutimelāpana jīvāhivyomapāṣāṇaiḥ
                    kroṣṭujihvāsubhāvitam / (19.1)

                    (RA_13.19.2)

                    (20.1) 
 ṭaṅkaṇaṃ ca rasaṃ vyoma vajraṃ cāpi praveśayet //
                    (RA_13.20.2) 
 abhraṃ hemadrutiṃ sūtaṃ trayamekatra melayet /
                    (RA_13.21.1)

                    (RA_13.21.2) 
 tuṣakarṣvagninā bhūmau svedena milati kṣaṇāt //
                    (RA_13.21.3) 
 śatavedhī bhavet so'yamāratāre ca śulvake / (RA_13.22.1) 
 tasya madhye tathā deyā abhrahemadrutiḥ punaḥ //
                    (RA_13.22.2) 
 tuṣakarṣvagninā svedyaṃ yāvat sūtāvaśeṣitam /
                    (RA_13.23.1) 
 sahasravedhī sa bhavet nātra kāryā vicāraṇā //
                    (RA_13.23.2) 
 saṃkalaiḥ saṃkalair bandhe vedhaṃ daśaguṇottaram /
                    (RA_13.24.1) 
 saptasaṃkalikābaddhaḥ koṭivedhī mahārasaḥ // (RA_13.24.2) 
 śarīrārthaṃ yadā bhakṣet guñjāmātraṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ /
                    (RA_13.25.1) 
 trikaṭutriphalāyuktaṃ ghṛtena madhunā saha / (RA_13.25.2) 
 jīrṇe jīrṇe tu saṃgrāhyaṃ yāvat syādaṣṭaraktikāḥ //
                    (25.3) 
 śatādikoṭiparyantaṃ saṃkalair yo hato rasaḥ /
                    (RA_13.26.1) 
 jīvet tena pramāṇena vajravallī yathā rasaḥ //
                    (RA_13.26.2) 
 Erlangen von viṣṇutva durch drutis
                     hemābhraśulbadrutibhiḥ pāradastu samanvitaḥ / (27.1) 
 vedhayet pūrvayogena bhakṣayet sarvayogataḥ /
                    (RA_13.27.2) 
 labhate vaiṣṇavaṃ sthānaṃ viṣṇutulyaparākramaḥ //
                    (RA_13.27.3) 
 stambhana verschiedener Metalle
                     ārābhrahemadrutayaḥ pāradena samanvitāḥ / (28.1)

                    (RA_13.30.1)

                    (30.2)

                 śrībhairava uvāca / (1.1) 
 punar anyaṃ pravakṣyāmi vajrabandhaṃ sureśvari //
                    (RA_14.1.2) 
 rasabandhana, -jāraṇa mit strīrajas gandhakaṃ bhakṣayen nārī
                    dinānāmekaviṃśatim / (2.1) 
 tadrajo rasarājasya bandhane jāraṇe hitam // (RA_14.2.2)

 dvipadī rajasāmardya yāvat tat kalkatāṃ gatam //
                    (RA_14.3.2) 
 pādāṃśena suvarṇasya pattralepaṃ tu kārayet // (RA_14.4) 
 vyomavallīrasaṃ kāntaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ ca sucūrṇitam /
                    (RA_14.5.1) 
 abhrakamaṣṭamāṃśena khalle kṛtvā vimardayet // (RA_14.5.2) 
 naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ catuṣkaṃ tadandhayitvā puṭettataḥ /
                    (RA_14.6.1) 
 andhamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ krāmaṇena samanvitam / (RA_14.6.2) 
 khoṭas tu jāyate devi śatavedhī mahārasaḥ // (RA_14.6.3) 
 sauvīraṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ kācaṃ dattvā dattvā viśodhayet /
                    (RA_14.7.1) 
 ajīrṇe milite hemnā samāvartas tu jāyate // (RA_14.7.2)

 saṃkalikā ekaguṇena sūtena ekā saṃkalikocyate / (9.1) 
 triguṇena tu sūtena dvitīyā saṃkalī bhavet // (RA_14.9.2) 
 ṣaḍguṇena tu sūtena tṛtīyā saṃkalī bhavet / (RA_14.10.1) 
 daśaguṇena sūtena caturthī saṃkalī bhavet // (RA_14.10.2) 
 pañcadaśaguṇeneśi pañcamī saṃkalī bhavet / (RA_14.11.1) 
 ekaviṃśadguṇeneśi ṣaṣṭhī saṃkalikā matā // (RA_14.11.2) 
 aṣṭāviṃśadguṇeneśi saptamī saṃkalī smṛtā / (RA_14.12.1) 
 ṣaṭtriṃśadguṇasambaddhā bhavet saṃkalikāṣṭamī //
                    (RA_14.12.2) 
 pañcacatvāriṃśadguṇaiḥ saṃkalī navamī matā / (RA_14.13.1) 
 pañcapañcāśadguṇena daśamī saṃkalī smṛtā // (RA_14.13.2) 
 evaṃ ca kramavṛddhyāsya saṃkalīdaśabandhanam // (RA_14.14) 
 vedhitva prathame daśavedhī syāt śatavedhī dvitīyake /
                    (15.1) 
 tṛtīye sahasravedhī ca caturthe 'yutavedhakaḥ //
                    (RA_14.15.2) 
 pañcame lakṣavedhī syāt daśalakṣaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhake /
                    (RA_14.16.1) 
 saptame koṭivedhī ca daśakoṭi tathāṣṭame // (RA_14.16.2) 
 dhūmāvaloko navame daśame śabdavedhakaḥ / (RA_14.17.1) 
 saṃkalaiḥ saṃkalair baddho vedho daśaguṇo bhavet //
                    (17.2) 
 daśasaṃkalikābaddhaḥ śabdavedhī mahārasaḥ / (RA_14.18.1) 
 yathā lohe tathā dehe kramate nātra saṃśayaḥ //
                    (RA_14.18.2) 
 vedhayet tatpramāṇena dhātūṃś caiva śarīrakam /
                    (RA_14.19.1) 
 kārayed guṭikāṃ divyāṃ badarāsthipramāṇataḥ // (19.2) 
 mahākālīṃ pūjayitvā dhārayet satataṃ budhaḥ /
                    (RA_14.20.1) 
 tasya mantraṃ pravakṣyāmi tridaśair api durlabham //
                    (20.2) 
 praṇavo bhuvaneśībījaṃ lakṣmībījaṃ tataḥ param //
                    (RA_14.21) 
 oṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ kālikā kāli mahākāli māṃsaśoṇitabhojini /
                    (22.1) 
 hrīṃ hrīṃ huṃ raktakṛṣṇamukhe devi rasasiddhiṃ dadasva me //
                    (22.2) 
 śrīṃ hrīṃ aiṃ ramā śaktiś ca tārākhyo mantro'yaṃ sarvasiddhidaḥ
                    // (23) 
 pūjayitvā tato devīṃ siddhacakraṃ viśeṣataḥ /
                    (RA_14.24.1) 
 tāṃ kṣiped vaktramadhye tu guṭikāṃ divyarūpiṇīm //
                    (RA_14.24.2) 
 śatavedhena yā baddhā rasena guṭikā priye / (RA_14.25.1) 
 māsamekaṃ tu vaktrasthā jīveccaiva yugāvadhi //
                    (RA_14.25.2) 
 tathā sahasravedhena yā baddhā guṭikā śubhā /
                    (RA_14.26.1) 
 māsadvayaṃ tu vaktrasthā jīveccandrārkatārakam //
                    (RA_14.26.2)

 śakratulyaṃ tadāyuḥ syāt tribhir māsair varānane //

 lakṣavedhena yā baddhā guṭikā divyarūpiṇī / (RA_14.28.1) 
 caturmāsaṃ tu vaktrasthā brahmāyuṣaṃ prayacchati //
                    (28.2) 
 daśalakṣeṇa yā baddhā guṭikā divyarūpiṇī / (RA_14.29.1)

                    (RA_14.29.2)

                    (31.2) 
 dhūmāvalokane baddhā guṭikā śivarūpiṇī / (RA_14.32.1) 
 aṣṭamāsaṃ tu vaktrasthā īśānasya phalaṃ labhet //
                    (RA_14.32.2) 
 śabdavedhena yā baddhā guṭikā śivarūpiṇī / (RA_14.33.1) 
 navamāsaṃ tu vaktrasthā sa bhavedvyāpako naraḥ //
                    (RA_14.33.2) 
 navasaṃkalikābaddhaḥ svayambhurvā maheśvaraḥ /
                    (RA_14.34.1) 
 kartā hartā svayaṃ bhoktā śāpānugrahakārakaḥ //
                    (RA_14.34.2) 
 sarvajñaḥ sarvakartā ca sūkṣmarūpo nirañjanaḥ /
                    (RA_14.35.1) 
 icchayā kurute sṛṣṭimicchayā saṃharejjagat //
                    (RA_14.35.2)

                    (RA_14.36.2) 
 punar anyaṃ pravakṣyāmi vajrabandhaṃ sudurlabham //
                    (RA_14.37)

                    (38.1) 
 mṛtavajraṃ palāṃśena mardayed dvipadīrasaiḥ //
                    (RA_14.38.2)

                    (39.2)

                    (RA_14.40.1) 
 caturviṃśatisiddhānāṃ nāyakaḥ sarvasiddhidaḥ //
                    (RA_14.40.2)

                    (41.2) 
 dhmātaḥ khoṭo bhavatyāśu śodhitaḥ kācaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ /
                    (RA_14.42.1) 
 yāvacchakrodayaprakhyo jāyate sa rasaḥ priye //
                    (RA_14.42.2) 
 vajrasattvaṃ ca gaganaṃ rasaṃ hema ca melayet /
                    (RA_14.43.1)

                    (RA_18.189.2) 
 vidhihīno raso devi naiva sidhyet kadācana /
                    (RA_18.190.1) 
 śāstrahīnasya deveśi naiva siddhir varānane //
                    (RA_18.190.2) 
 aśubhaiḥ karmabhiḥ sarvaiḥ sampradāyo na sidhyati /
                    (191.1) 
 na sidhyedrasaśāstre tu na sidhyet tādṛśo guruḥ //
                    (191.2) 
 na prāpet tādṛśīmājñāṃ naiva jñānaṃ ca tādṛśam /
                    (RA_18.192.1) 
 na prāpet tādṛśīṃ nārīm ekacittāṃ varānane //
                    (RA_18.192.2) 
 na prāped rasavantaṃ ca tāṃ ca devīṃ rasāṅkuśīm /
                    (193.1) 
 yasya tuṣṭaḥ śivaḥ sākṣāt tasya siddhī rasāyane //
                    (193.2) 
 punar anyat pravakṣyāmi golabandhanam uttamam / (194.1) 
 yena bhakṣitamātreṇa jāyate hyajarāmaraḥ //
                    (RA_18.194.2) 
 gandhābhrakāntasahitaṃ bhānukharparakāñcanam /
                    (RA_18.195.1) 
 samaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ rasendrasya baddhaṃ kṛtvā tu golakam //
                    (195.2) 
 rasendraṃ pañcapalikaṃ samabhāgena melayet /
                    (RA_18.196.1) 
 saptajambīratoyena mardayed golakasya ca //
                    (RA_18.196.2) 
 chāyāviśuṣkaṃ golaṃ tu śaśibhāvaṃ karoti tat /
                    (RA_18.197.1) 
 etat sarvaṃ vimardyaṃ tu sūtakaṃ golakasya ca //
                    (RA_18.197.2) 
 tat karīṣāgninā bhūmau mṛdusvedaṃ tu kārayet /
                    (RA_18.198.1) 
 vaktre sthitamidaṃ golaṃ cāmaratāpradāyakam //
                    (RA_18.198.2) 
 sūtagolakajātasya phalaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyate /
                    (RA_18.199.1) 
 rasāyane varṇakaro rasasiddhipradāyakaḥ // (RA_18.199.2) 
 sugandhalepatāmbūlakastūrīkuṅkumāguru / (RA_18.200.1) 
 śrīkhaṇḍaṃ mṛganābhiś ca kaṅkolaṃ jātikāphalam /
                    (RA_18.200.2) 
 anyāni ca sugandhīni snāne pāne pradāpayet //
                    (RA_18.200.3) 
 kuñcitāgrās tu yat keśā yā śyāmā padmalocanā /
                    (RA_18.201.1) 
 vistīrṇaṃ jaghanaṃ yasyāḥ saṃkīrṇaṃ hṛdayaṃ bhavet //
                    (201.2) 
 kṛṣṇapakṣe bhavedyasyā yuvatyāḥ puṣpadarśanam /
                    (RA_18.202.1) 
 kāminī sā samākhyātā uttamā ca rasāyane // (RA_18.202.2) 
 āliṅgane sparśane ca maithunālāpayorapi / (RA_18.203.1) 
 sarvarogavinirmukto valīpalitavarjitaḥ // (RA_18.203.2) 
 śatarogaṃ vinaśyeta mukhamadhye dhṛteṣu ca /
                    (RA_18.204.1) 
 yavatulyapramāṇeṣu jīved varṣaśatatrayam //
                    (RA_18.204.2) 
 atha ṣoḍaśavarṣāṇi ṣoḍaśāni sureśvari / (RA_18.205.1) 
 dhṛtāni mukhamadhye tu teṣu vakṣyāmi ye guṇāḥ //
                    (RA_18.205.2) 
 nāsau chidyeta śastraiś ca pāvakena na dahyate /
                    (RA_18.206.1) 
 vāyuvego mahātejāḥ kāmadeva ivāparaḥ // (RA_18.206.2) 
 icchayā jāyate dṛśyo hyadṛśyaś caiva jāyate /
                    (RA_18.207.1) 
 tasya saṃsparśamātreṇa sarvalohāni kāñcanam //
                    (RA_18.207.2) 
 punar anyaṃ pravakṣyāmi vajrabandhaṃ surārcite //
                    (RA_18.208) 
 hīnāṅgo'bhyadhikāṅgaś ca savyādhiḥ kubja ānataḥ /
                    (209.1) 
 natāṅghriḥ pāṇiniḥsūto jarayā stobhitendriyaḥ //
                    (RA_18.209.2) 
 jaḍagadgadamūko'pi gatihīnastathaiva ca / (RA_18.210.1) 
 śaṅkhatvacavinirmukto jīvitair eva tiṣṭhati //
                    (RA_18.210.2) 
 baddhasyāsya prabhāvena samāvarto yadā bhavet /
                    (RA_18.211.1) 
 koṭivedhi rasaṃ grāhyaṃ piṇḍaṣaṭkena saṃyutam //
                    (RA_18.211.2) 
 ekaikasya tu madhyasthāṃ guṭikāṃ kārayed budhaḥ //
                    (RA_18.212) 
 guṭikāḥ pañcasaṃkhyātāḥ ṣaṣṭhī caiva tu pañcamī /
                    (213.1) 
 ṣaṭsaṃguṇitapiṇḍaṃ syāt tāmrapātraṃ suśobhanam /
                    (RA_18.213.2) 
 ūrdhvaṃ puruṣamātraṃ tu puruṣārdhaṃ ca maṇḍalam /
                    (213.3) 
 caturmukhakṛtaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ tasyopari nivedayet //
                    (RA_18.213.4) 
 saghṛtaṃ ca mahātailaṃ samabhāgena lepayet /
                    (RA_18.214.1) 
 pūjayitvā kaṭāhaṃ tu dikpālāṃś caiva pūjayet //
                    (RA_18.214.2) 
 kumārīṃ pūjayet paścād dadyāddikṣu baliṃ tathā /
                    (RA_18.215.1) 
 dhamanaṃ tatra kurvīta caturdikṣu śanaiḥ śanaiḥ //
                    (215.2) 
 sutaptaṃ ca vidhātavyaṃ nirdhūmaṃ ca yadā bhavet /
                    (216.1) 
 tadā natvā guruṃ devaṃ candrārkādigrahānapi /
                    (RA_18.216.2) 
 nakṣatrāṇi ca sampūjya ātmānaṃ tatra nikṣipet //
                    (RA_18.216.3) 
 pṛthivyāpastathā tejo vāyurākāśameva ca / (RA_18.217.1) 
 sudurlabhaṃ vijānīyāt siddhirūpaṃ niyojayet //
                    (RA_18.217.2) 
 kalalaṃ ca bhavet sarvaṃ puraś cāpo vinikṣipet /
                    (RA_18.218.1) 
 raktavarṇaṃ vijānīyāttejastejasi yojayet //
                    (RA_18.218.2) 
 māṃsapiṇḍaṃ bhavet tatra vāyuṃ tatraiva nikṣipet /
                    (219.1) 
 kāntavarṇaṃ tadā kāryaṃ nikṣipet khaṃ kapālake //
                    (219.2) 
 dhamantaṃ hemasaṃkāśaṃ kṣāratvaṃ taṃ tu pādayet //
                    (RA_18.220) 
 kṛtvā tatra mahārāvaṃ huṅkāraṃ surapūjitam /
                    (RA_18.221.1) 
 uttiṣṭhati na sandehaḥ puṣṭāṅgo bhāskaro yathā /
                    (RA_18.221.2) 
 divyatejā mahākāyo divyadṛṣṭir mahābalaḥ //
                    (RA_18.221.3) 
 śatayojanavistīrṇaghaṇṭārāvaṃ supūjitam / (RA_18.222.1) 
 dīptahemamayaṃ divyaṃ ratnamāṇikyaśobhitam //
                    (RA_18.222.2) 
 puṣpamālāpatākāḍhyaṃ kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitam / (RA_18.223) 
 vimānottamamārūḍhaṃ śaṅkhakāhalaniḥsvanaiḥ //
                    (RA_18.223.1) 
 apsarogītavāditrairnṛtyair api manoharaiḥ /
                    (RA_18.224.1) 
 divyābharaṇasampūrṇā divyamālyopaśobhitā //
                    (RA_18.224.2) 
 apāṅgarāgasampannā surūpā madavihvalā / (RA_18.225.1) 
 āgacchati na sandeho devakanyoditaṃ prati //
                    (RA_18.225.2) 
 gṛhītvā sādhakendraṃ ca siddhaloke vaset tataḥ //
                    (RA_18.226) 
 divyāni snānapānāni divyāny ābharaṇāni saḥ /
                    (RA_18.227.1) 
 ramate śatasāhasraṃ siddhakanyāḥ smarāturāḥ //
                    (RA_18.227.2) 
 tasminnekārṇave ghore naṣṭasthāvarajaṅgame /
                    (RA_18.228.1) 
 devā yatra vilīyante siddhastatraiva līyate //
                    (RA_18.228.2) 
 bhūtakālāntako nāma caṇḍo'yam upavarṇitaḥ // (RA_18.229) 
 tattvato'yaṃ mahādevi yadā kartuṃ na śakyate /
                    (RA_18.230.1) 
 anenaiva śarīreṇa tadā siddhir bhaviṣyati //
                    (RA_18.230.2)
